 apadāna 
 khuddaka nikāya  sutta piṭaka 
 i  
  buddhavaggo paṭhamo  
 buddhāpadānaṃ 
 namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa  
 atha buddhāpadānāni suṇātha suddhamānasā  
 tiṃsapāramīsampuṇṇā dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā   apbud    
 sambodhiṃ buddhaseṭṭhānaṃ sasaṅghe lokanāyake  
 dasaṅgulī namassitvā sirasā abhivādayiṃ   apbud    
 yāvatā buddhakhettesu ratanā vijjanti  saṅkhiyā   
 ākāsaṭṭhā ca bhūmaṭṭhā manasā sabbam āhare    apbud    
 tattha rūpiyabhūmiyaṃ pāsādaṃ māpaye  ahaṃ  
 nekabhūmiṃ  ratanamayaṃ ubbiddhaṃ nabham uggataṃ   apbud    
 vicittathambhaṃ sukataṃ suvibhattaṃ mahārahaṃ  
 kanakāmayasaṅghātaṃ toraṇacchattamaṇḍitaṃ    apbud    
 paṭhamā veluriyā bhūmi vimalabbhasamā subhā  
 naḷinājalajākiṇṇā  varakañcanabhūmiyā   apbud    
 pavāḷaṃ sapavāḷavaṇṇā kāci  lohitakāsubhā  
 indagopakavaṇṇābhā bhūmi obhāsati  disā   apbud    
 suvibhattā gharamukhā  niyyuhā sīhapañjarā  
 caturo vedikā jālā gandhaveḷā manoramā   apbud    
 nīlā pītā lohitakā odātā suddhakāḷakā  
 kūṭāgāravarūpetā sattaratanavibhūsitā   apbud

   apadāna 
 olokamayā padumā vāḷāvihaṅgasobhitā  
 nakkhattatārakākiṇṇā candasuriyehi maṇḍitā   apbud     
 hemajālena sañchannā  soṇṇakiṅkiṇikāyutā  
 vātavegena kūjanti soṇṇamālā manoramā   apbud     
 mañjeṭṭhakaṃ lohitakaṃ pītakaṃ haripañjaraṃ  
 nānāraṅgehi sampītaṃ ussitaddhajamālinī   apbud     
 nānābahū  nekasatā phalakā rajatāmayā  
 maṇimayā lohitaṅkā masāragallamayā tathā   apbud     
 nānāsayanavicittā  saṇhākāsikasanthatā  
 kambalā dukulā cīnā paṭṭuṇṇā paṇḍupāvurā  
 vividhattharaṇaṃ  sabbaṃ manasā paññapem  ahaṃ   apbud     
 tāsu tāsveva  bhūmisu ratanakūṭalaṅkataṃ  
 maṇiverocanā ukkā dhārayantā sutiṭṭhare   apbud     
 sobhanti esikā thambhā subhā kañcanatoraṇā  
 jambonadā sāramayā atho rajatamayā pi ca   apbud     
 nekāsandhīsu vibhattā kavāṭaggaḷacittitā   
 ubhato puṇṇaghatā neke  padumuppalasaṃyutā   apbud     
 atīte sabba buddhe ca sasaṅghe lokanāyake  
 pakatīvaṇṇarūpena nimminitvā sasāvake   apbud     
 tena dvārena pavisitvā sabbe buddhā sasāvakā  
 sabbasovaṇṇaye  pīṭhe   nisinnā ariyamaṇḍalā   apbud     
 ye ca etarahi atthi buddhā loke anuttarā  
  atītā vattamānā ca bhavanaṃ sabbe samāruhuṃ    apbud     
 paccekabuddhe nekasate sayambhū aparājite  
 atīte vattamāne ca bhavanaṃ sabbe samāhariṃ     apbud     
 kapparukkhā bahū atthi ye dibbā ye ca mānusā  
 sabbaṃ dussaṃ samāhantvā acchādemi ticīvaraṃ     apbud     
 khajjaṃ bhojjaṃ sāyaniyaṃ sampannaṃ pānabhojanaṃ    
 maṇimaye subhe patte sampūretvā adās  ahaṃ  apbud     
 dibbavatthā samāhutvā   maṭṭhacīvarasaṃyutā  
 madhurā sakkharā ceva telā ca madhuphānitā    
 tappitā paramannena sabbe te ariyamaṇḍalā   apbud

  page      
 buddhāpadānaṃ   
  ratanagabbhaṃ  pavisitvā kesarī va guhāsayā  
 mahārahamhi sayane sīhaseyyam akappayuṃ   apbud     
 sampajānā samuṭṭhāya sayane pallaṅkam ābhujuṃ   
 gocaraṃ sabbabuddhānaṃ jhānaratisamappitā   apbud     
 aññe dhammāni desenti aññe  kīḷanti iddhiyā  
 aññe abhiññā appenti abhiññā  vasibhāvitā  
 vikubbanā vikubbanti aññe nekasatasahassiyo   apbud     
 buddhā  pi  buddhe pucchanti visayaṃ sabbaññum  ālayaṃ  
 gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ paññāya vinibujjhare   apbud     
 sāvakā buddhe pucchanti buddhā pucchanti sāvake  
 aññamaññañ ca pucchanti añña maññaṃ byākaronti te    apbud     
 buddhā paccekabuddhā ca sāvakā paricārakā   
 evaṃ ratīsu rammānā  pāsāde bhiramanti te   apbud     
 suvaṇṇajālābhi saṃyuttaṃ rajatajālamaṇīhi ca   
 muttajālaparikkhittaṃ  chattaṃ  dhārentu  matthake   apbud     
 bhavantu celavitānā soṇṇatārakacittitā  
 vicittā malyavitatā sabbe dhārentu  matthake   apbud     
 vitatā malyadāmehi gandhadāmehi sobhitā  
 dussadāmehi parikiṇṇā ratanadāmavibhūsitā   apbud     
 pupphābhikiṇṇā sucittā surabhigandhadhūpitā   
 gandhapañcaṅgulaṅkitā   hemacchadanachāditā   apbud     
 catuddisā pokkharañño padumuppalasanthatā  
 sovaṇṇarūpe   khāyantu padumareṇurajuggatā   apbud     
 pupphantu pādapā   sabbe pāsādassa samantato  
 sayañ ca pupphā muñcitvā gandhā   bhavanam okiruṃ     apbud     
 sikhino tattha naccantu divyā   haṃsā pakūjare  
 karavīkā ca gāyantu dijasaṅghā samantato   apbud     
 bheriyo sabbā vajjantu vīṇā sabbā ravantu tā  
 sabbā saṅgītī vattantu pāsādassa sāmantato   apbud

  page      
   apadāna 
 yāvatā buddhakhettamhi cakkavāle  ca m uppari   
 mahantā jotisampannā acchiddā  ratanāmayā  apbud     
 tiṭṭhantu soṇṇapallaṅkā   dīparukkhā jalantu te  
 bhavantu ekapajjotā dasasahassī paramparā   apbud     
 gaṇikā lāsikā c  eva naccantu accharāgaṇā  
 nānāraṅgā padissantu pāsādassa samantato   apbud     
 dumagge pabbatagge vā sinerugirimuddhane   
 ussāpemi dhajaṃ sabbaṃ vicittaṃ pañcavaṇṇikaṃ   apbud     
 nārā nāgā ca gandhabbā sabbe devā upentu te  
 namassantā pañjalikā pāsādaṃ parivārayuṃ   apbud     
 yaṃ kiñci kusalaṃ kammaṃ kattabbaṃ kiriyaṃ mama  
 kāyena vācā manasā tidase sukataṃ kataṃ   apbud     
 ye sattā saññino atthi ye ca sattā asaññino  
 kataṃ puññaphalaṃ  mayhaṃ sabbe bhāgī bhavantu te   apbud     
 yesaṃ  kataṃ suviditaṃ dinnaṃ puññaphalaṃ mayā  
 ye ca tattha  na jānanti devā gantvā nivedayuṃ    apbud     
 sabbe lokamhi   ye sattā jīvantāhārahetukā  
 manuññaṃ bhojanaṃ sabbaṃ labhantu mama cetasā   apbud     
 manasā dānaṃ mayā dinnaṃ manasā pasādam āvahiṃ    
 pūjitā sabba sambuddhā paccekā jinasāvakā   apbud     
 tena kammena sukatena cetanā paṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā   mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsam agañch  ahaṃ   apbud     
 duve bhave pajānāmi devatte atha mānuse  
 aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi manasā patthanāphalaṃ   apbud     
 devānaṃ adhiko homi bhavāmi manujādhipo  
 rūpalakkhaṇasampanno paññāya asamo bhave   apbud     
 bhojanaṃ vividhaṃ seṭṭhaṃ ratanañ ca anappakaṃ  
 nānāvidhāni vatthāni   nabhā   khippam upenti maṃ   apbud     
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi dibbā bhakkhā upenti maṃ   apbud     
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi ratanā sabbe upenti me     apbud

  page      
 buddhāpadānaṃ   
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbe gandhā upenti me    apbud     
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbe yānā upenti me    apbud     
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbe mālā upenti me    apbud     
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi alaṅkārā upenti me    apbud     
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbā kaññā upenti me    apbud     
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi upenti madhusakkharā   apbud     
 puthavyā pabbate c  eva ākāse udake vane  
 yaṃyaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbe khajjā  upenti maṃ   apbud     
  adhane addhikajane yācake ca pathāvino    
 yam me kataṃ  dānavaraṃ sambodhivarapattiyā   apbud     
 nādento pabbataṃ selaṃ gajjento  bahalaṃ  giriṃ  
 sadevalokaṃ hāsento  buddho loke bhavām  ahaṃ   apbud     
 disā dasavidhā loke yāyato n  atthi antakaṃ  
 tasmiñ ca disābhāgamhi buddhakhettā   asaṅkhiyā   apbud     
 pabhāpakittitā mayhaṃ yamakā raṃsivāhanā  
 etth  antare   raṃsijālaṃ āloko vipulo bhave   apbud     
 ettake lokadhātumhi sabbe passantu maṃ janā  
 sabbe ca sumanā hontu sabbe mam anuvattare     apbud     
 visiṭṭhamadhunādena   amataṃ bherim āhane    
 etth  antare janā sabbe suṇantu madhuraṃ giraṃ   apbud     
 dhammameghena vassante sabbe hontu anāsavā  
 ye ttha   pacchimakā sattā sotāpannā bhavantu te   apbud     
 datvā dātabbakaṃ dānaṃ sīlaṃ pūretv  asesato  
 nekkhamme pāramiṃ   patvā patto sambodhim uttamaṃ   apbud

  page      
   apadāna 
 paṇḍite paripucchitvā katvā viriyam uttamaṃ  
 khantiyā pāramiṃ gantvā patto sambodhim uttamaṃ   apbud     
 katvā saccam  adhiṭṭhānaṃ pūretvā saccapāramiṃ  
 mettāya pāramiṃ gantvā  patto sambodhim uttamaṃ   apbud     
 lābhālābhe sukhe dukkhe sammāne ca vimānane  
 sabbattha samako hutvā patto sambodhim uttamaṃ   apbud     
 kosajjaṃ bhayato disvā viriyañ cāpi khemato  
 āraddhavīriyā  hotha esā buddhānusāsanī   apbud     
 vivādaṃ bhayato disvā avivādaṃ ca khemato  
 samaggā sakhilā hotha esā buddhānusāsanī   apbud     
 pamādaṃ bhayato disvā appamādañ  ca khemato  
 bhāveth  aṭṭhaṅgikaṃ maggaṃ esā buddhānusāsanī   apbud     
 samāgatā bahū buddhā arahanto  ca sabbaso  
 sambuddhe arahante ca vandamānā  namassatha   apbud     
 evaṃ acintiyā buddhā buddhadhammā acintiyā  
 acintiyesu  pasannānaṃ vipāko hoti acintiyo ti   apbud     
 itthaṃ sudaṃ bhagavā attano buddhacaritaṃ  sambhāvayamāno buddhānaṃ padāniyaṃ  nāma dhammapariyāyaṃ abhāsitthā ti  
 buddhāpadānaṃ samattaṃ

 ii  
 paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ 
 atha paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ suṇātha  
 tathāgataṃ jetavane vasantaṃ apucchi vedehamuni nataṅgo    
  paccekabuddhā kira nāma honti bhavanti te hetuhi kehi dhīrā    appac    
 tadāha sabbaññuvaro mahesi ānandabhaddaṃ  madhurassarena   
 ye sabbabuddhesu  katādhikārā aladdhamokkhā jinasāsanesu   appac    
 ten  eva  saṃvegamukhena dhīrā  vināpi buddhehi sutikkhapaññā  
 ārammaṇenāpi parittakena paccekabodhiṃ anupāpuṇanti   appac    
 sabbamhi  lokamhi mamaṃ ṭha petvā paccekabuddhehi samo va n  atthi   
 tesaṃ imaṃ vaṇṇapadesamattaṃ vakkhām  ahaṃ sādhu mahāmunīnaṃ   appac    
 sayaṃ eva buddhānaṃ mahāisīnaṃ sādhūni vākyāni madhuñ ca khuddaṃ  
 anuttaraṃ bhesajaṃ patthayantā suṇotha sabbe supasannacittā   appac    
  paccekabuddhānaṃ samāga tānaṃ paramparavyākaraṇāni  yāni  
 ādīnavo yañ ca virāgavatthuṃ yathā ca bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu   appac    
  
                                                                            m  mataṅgo  
   g  anandasaddaṃ  
   g  pubbabuddhesu  
   cy  g  idha  m  ten  idha  
   s  vīrā  
   g  byākaraṇāni  
  
  page      
   apadāna 
 saṃrāgavatthūsu  virāgasaññī rattamhi lokamhi virattacittā  
 hitvā papañcaṃ jitaphanditāni tatth  eva bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu   appac    
 sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ aviheṭhayaṃ aññataram pi tesaṃ  
 mettena cittena hitānukampī eko care khaggavisānakappo   appac    
  sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ aviheṭhayaṃ aññataraṃ pi tesaṃ  
 na puttam iccheyya  kuto sahāyaṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac    
 saṃsaggajātassa bhavanti snehā snehanvayaṃ  dukkhaṃ idaṃ pahoti  
 ādīnavaṃ snehajaṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac     
 mitte suhajje anukampamāno hāpeti atthaṃ paṭibandhacitto  
 etaṃ bhayaṃ santhave  pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac     
 vaṃso visālo va  yathā visatto puttesu dāresu ca yā apekkhā  
 vaṃsakkaḷīro  va asajjamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac     
 migo araññamhi yathā abandho yenicchakaṃ gacchati gocarāya  
 viññu naro seritaṃ  pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac     
 āmantaṇā hoti sahāyamajjhe  vāse ṭhāne  gamane cārikāya  
 anabhijjhitaṃ seritaṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac     
 khiḍḍā ratī   hoti sahāyamajjhe puttesu pemaṃ vipulañ ca hoti    
 piyavippayogaṃ  vijigucchamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac

  page      
 paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ   
  
 catuddiso  appaṭigho ca hoti santussamāno itarītarena  
 parissayānaṃ sahitā achambhī  eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac     
 dussaṅgahā  pabbajitā pi eke atho gahaṭṭhā gharam āvasantā  
 apposukko paraputtesu hutvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac     
 oropayitvā gihibyañjanāni sañchinnapatto yathā koviḷāro  
 chetvāna vīro gihibandhanāni eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   appac     
 sace labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ saddhiṃcaraṃ sādhuvihāri dhīraṃ  
 abhibhūya sabbāni parissayāni careyya ten  attamano satīmā   appac     
 no ce labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ saddhiṃcaraṃ sādhuvihāri dhīraṃ  
 rājā va raṭṭhaṃ vijitaṃ pahāya eko care mātaṅgaraññe va nāgo   appac

 bhajanti sevanti ca kāraṇatthā  nikkāraṇā dullabhā ajja mittā

 uppādesu nimittesu lakkhaṇesu ca kovidā  
 paṭṭhābhummantalikkhe te  mama sissā susikkhitā   aptha         
 appicchā nipakā ete appāhārā aloḷupā   
 lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā parivārenti maṃ sadā   aptha         
 jhāyī jhānaratā dhīrā santacittā samāhitā  
 ākiñcañaṃ patthayantā parivārenti maṃ sadā   aptha         
 abhiññāpāramīpattā pettike gocare ratā  
 antalikkhacarā  dhīrā parivārenti maṃ sadā   aptha         
 saṃvutā chasu dvāresu anejā  rakkhitindriyā  
 asaṃsaṭṭhā ca te dhīrā mama sissā durāsadā   aptha         
 pallaṅkena nisajjāya  thānā caṅkamanena ca  
 vītināmenti te rattiṃ mama sissā durāsadā   aptha         
 rajanīye  na rajjanti dosanīye  na dussare  
 mohanīye na muyhanti mama sissā durāsadā   aptha         
 iddhivīmaṃsamānā te vattanti niccakālikaṃ  
 paṭhaviṃ te pakampenti sārambhena durāsadā   aptha         
 kīḷamānā ca te sissā kīḷanti jhānakīḷitaṃ  
 jambuto  phalam ānenti mama sissā durāsadā   aptha         
 aññe gacchanti goyānaṃ aññe pubbavidehanaṃ   
 aññe uttarakuruṃ ca   mama sissā   durāsadā   aptha         
 purato khāriṃ pesenti   pacchato ca vajanti te

 aggipākī anaggī ca dantodukkhalikā pi ca

 gandhitā sīlagandhena mama sissā durāsadā   aptha

    sāriputta    
 pāto va sannipātetvā jaṭilā uggatāpanā  
 labhālabhaṃ pakittetvā gacchanti ambare tadā   aptha         
 etesaṃ pakkamantānaṃ mahāsaddo pavattati  
 ajinacammasaddena moditā  honti devatā   aptha         
 disodisaṃ  pakkamanti antalikkhacarā isī  
 sakabalen  upatthaddhā  te gacchanti yadicchakaṃ   aptha         
 pathavīkampakā ete sabbe va nabhacārino  
 uggatejā duppasahā sāgaro va akkhobhiyā   aptha         
 ṭhānacaṅkamiyā  keci  keci nesajjikā  isī  
 pavattabhojanā keci mama sissā durāsadā   aptha         
 mettāvihārino  ete hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 anattukkaṃsakā sabbe na te vambhenti kassaci   aptha         
 sīharājā va sambhīto  gajarājā va thāmavā  
 durāsadā vyaggha r iva agacchanti mam antike   aptha         
 vijjādharā ca devatā nāga gandhabba rakkhasā  
 kumbhaṇḍā dānavā garuḷā upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   aptha         
 te jaṭā khāribhārikā  ajinuttaravasino  
 antalikkhacarā sabbe upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   aptha         
 tadānucchavikā ete aññamaññaṃ sagāravā  
 catubbīsaṃsahassānaṃ khittasaddo  na vijjati   aptha         
 pāde pādaṃ nikkhipantā appasaddā susaṃvutā  
 upasaṅkamma sabbe va sirasā vandare mamaṃ   aptha         
 tehi sissehi parivuto santehi ca tapassihi    
 vasāmi assame tattha jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ   aptha         
 isīnaṃ sīlagandhena pupphagandhena cūbhayaṃ  
 phalinaṃ phalagandhena gandhito hoti assamo   aptha         
 rattindivaṃ na jānāmi arati me na vijjati  
 sake sisse ovadanto bhiyyo hāsaṃ   labhām  ahaṃ   aptha         
 pupphānaṃ pupphamānānaṃ phalānaṃ cāpi paccataṃ  
 dibbā gandhā pavāyanti sobhayantā mam  assamaṃ   aptha

 samādhimhā vuṭṭhahitvā ātāpī nipako ahaṃ  
 khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna vanam ajjhogahiṃ ahaṃ   aptha         
 uppāde supine cāpi lakkhaṇe susikkhito  
 pavattamānaṃ mantapadaṃ dharayāmi ahaṃ tadā   aptha         
 anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 vivekakāmo sambuddho himavantam upāgamī   aptha         
 ajjhogahetvā himavantam aggo kāruṇiko muni  
 pallaṅkam ābhujitvāna  nisīdi purisuttamo   aptha         
 tatth  addasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ sappabhāsaṃ manoramaṃ  
 indīvaraṃ va jalitaṃ ādittaṃ va hutāsanaṃ   aptha         
 jalantaṃ dīparukkhaṃ  va vijjuṃ abbhaghane yathā  
 suphullaṃ sālarājaṃ va addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha         
 ayaṃ nāgo mahāvīro dukkhass  antakaro  muni  
 idaṃ  dassanam āgamma sabbe dukkhā  pamuccare   aptha         
 disvān  ahaṃ devadevaṃ lakkhaṇam upadhārayiṃ  
  buddho nu kho na vā buddho  handa passāmi cakkhumaṃ    aptha         
 sahassārāni cakkāni dissanti caraṇuttame  
 lakkhaṇāni ssa disvāna niṭṭhaṃ gacchiṃ tathāgate   aptha         
 sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna sammajjitvān  ahaṃ tadā  
 aṭṭha pupphe samānetva buddhaseṭṭham apūjayiṃ   aptha         
 pūjayitvāna taṃ buddhaṃ  oghatiṇṇaṃ anāsavaṃ  
 ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā namassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha         
 yena ñāṇena sambuddho viharati anāsavo  
 taṃ ñāṇaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇātha mama bhāsato   aptha         
 samuddharas  imaṃ lokaṃ sayambhu amitodaya   
 tava  dassanam āgamma kaṅkhāsotaṃ taranti te   aptha         
 tuvaṃ satthā ca ketu ca dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃ  
 parāyano patiṭṭhā ca dīpo ca dipaduttamo   aptha         
 sakkā samudde udakaṃ pametum āḷhakena vā  
 na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   aptha         
 dhāretuṃ pathaviṃ sakkā ṭhapetvā tulamaṇḍale  
 na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   aptha

 ākāsaṃ minituṃ sakkā rajjuyā aṅgulena vā  
 na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   aptha         
 mahāsamudde udakaṃ paṭhaviṃ cākhilañ jahe   
 buddhañāṇaṃ upādāya upamā te na yujjare   aptha         
 sadevakassa lokassa cittaṃ yesaṃ pavattati  
 antojālagatā  ete tava ñāṇamhi cakkhumā   aptha         
 yena ñāṇena patto si kevalaṃ bodhim uttamaṃ  
 tena ñāṇena sabbaññū maddasi paratitthiye   aptha         
 imā gāthā paṭhitvāna  suruci  nāma tāpaso  
 ajinaṃ pattharitvāna paṭhaviyaṃ nisīdi so   aptha         
 cullāsītisahassāni ajjhogāḷho mahaṇṇave  
 accuggato tāvad eva girirājā pavuccati   aptha         
 tāva accuggato neru āyato vitthato ca so  
 cuṇṇito aṇubhedena koṭisatasahassiyo  aptha         
 lakkhe ṭhapīyamānamhi parikkhayam agacchatha   
 na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   aptha         
 sukhumacchikena jālena udakaṃ yo parikkhipe  
 ye keci udake pāṇā antojālagatā  siyuṃ   aptha         
 tath  eva hi mahāvīra ye keci puthutitthiyā  
 ditthīgahanapakkhannā parāmasena mohitā   aptha         
 tava suddhena ñāṇena anāvaraṇadassinā   
 antojālagatā  ete ñāṇaṃ te nātivattare   aptha         
 bhagavā ca tamhi samaye anomadassī mahāyaso  
 vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā disaṃ olokayī jino   aptha         
 anomadassī munino nisabho nāma sāvako  
 parivuto satasahassehi santacittehi tādihi   aptha         
 khīṇāsavehi suddhehi chaḷabhiññehi tādihi  
 cittam aññāya buddhassa upesi lokanāyakaṃ   aptha         
 antalikkhe ṭhitā tattha padakkhiṇam akaṃsu te  
 namassantā pañjalikā orohuṃ  buddhasantike   aptha         
 anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā sitaṃ pātukarī jino   aptha         
 varuṇo nām  upaṭṭhāko sabbaññussa mahesino  
 ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā apucchi lokanāyakaṃ   aptha

    therāpadāna 
 ko nu kho bhagavā hetu sitakammassa satthuno   
 na hi buddhā ahetuhi sitaṃ pātukaronti te   aptha         
 anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 saṅghamajjhe  nisīditvā imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha   aptha          
 yo maṃ pupphena pūjesi ñāṇañ cāpi anutthunī   
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇātha mama bhāsato   aptha          
 buddhassa giram aññāya sabbe devā samāgatā  
 saddhammaṃ sotukāmā te sambuddham upasaṅkamuṃ   aptha          
 dasasu lokadhātūsu devakāyā mahiddhikā  
 saddhammaṃ sotukāmā te sambuddham upasaṅkamuṃ   aptha          
 hatthī assā rathā pattī senā ca caturaṅginī  
 parivārenti  taṃ  niccaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha          
 saṭṭhiṃturiyasahassāni  bheriyo samalaṅkatā  
 upaṭṭhissanti taṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha          
 soḷasitthisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā  
 vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā  aptha          
 aḷārapamhāhasulā  su soññā tanumajjhimā  
 parivārenti  taṃ  niccaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha          
 kappasatasahassāni devaloke ramissati  
 sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavattī  rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati   aptha          
 sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ     aptha          
 pacchime bhave sampatte manussattaṃ gamissati    
 brāhmaṇī sāriyā nāma dhārayissati kucchinā   aptha          
 mātuyā nāmagottena paññāyissati yaṃ naro  
 sāriputto ti nāmena tikkhapañño bhavissati   aptha          
 asītikoṭī chaḍḍetvā pabbajissati kiñcano  
 gavesanto santipadaṃ carissati mahim imaṃ   aptha          
 aparimeyye ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo    
 gotamo nāmagottena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha          
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sāriputto ti nāmena hessati aggasāvako   aptha

    sāriputta    
 ayaṃ bhāgīrasī gaṅgā himavantā  pabhāvita  
 mahāsamuddaṃ appeti tappayantī  mahodadhiṃ   aptha          
 tath  evāyaṃ sāriputto sāketīsu visārado  
 paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā tappayissati pāṇino   aptha          
 himavantam upādāya sāgarañ ca mahodadhiṃ  
 etthantare yaṃ puliṇaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ    aptha          
 tam pi sakkā asesena saṅkhātuṃ gaṇanā yathā  
 na tveva sāriputtassa paññāy  anto bhavissati   aptha          
 lakkhe ṭhapīyamānamhi  khīye gaṅgāya vālukā  
 na tveva sāriputtassa paññāy  anto bhavissati   aptha          
 mahāsamudde ūmiyo  gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyā  
 tath  eva sāriputtassa paññāy  anto na hessati   aptha          
 ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ  
 paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā hessati aggasāvako   aptha          
 pavattitaṃ dhammacakkaṃ sakyaputtena tādinā  
 anuvattessati sammā  vassanto dhammavuṭṭhiyo   aptha          
 sabbam etam abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavo  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati    aptha          
 aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ anomadassissa satthuno  
 yassāhaṃ kāraṃ katvāna  sabbattha pāramiṅgato   aptha          
 aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha  
 sumutto saravego va  kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ   aptha          
 asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto nibbānaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ  
 vicinaṃ titthiye sabbe esāhaṃ   saṃsariṃ bhave   aptha          
 yathāpi vyādhito   poso pariyeseyya osadhaṃ  
 vicineyyā vanaṃ   sabbaṃ vyādhino parimuttiyā  aptha          
 asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto nibbānaṃ amataṃ padaṃ  
 avyākiṇṇaṃ   pañcasataṃ pabbajiṃ   isipabbajjaṃ  aptha          
 jaṭābhārena bharito ajinuttaranivās  ahaṃ  
 abhiññāpāramiṃ gantvā brahmalokaṃ agacch  ahaṃ  aptha

 n  atthi bāhirake buddhī ṭhapetvā jinasāsanaṃ  
 ye keci buddhimā sattā bujjhanti jinasāsanaṃ    aptha          
 atthakāmaṃ mamam  etaṃ nayidaṃ iti haṃ tadā  
 asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto kutitthaṃ sañcarim ahaṃ   aptha          
 yathā sāratthiko poso kadaliṃ chetvā  phālaye  
 na tattha sāraṃ vindeyyā sārena rittako hi so   aptha          
 tath  eva titthiyā loke nānādiṭṭhī bahujjanā  
 asaṅkhatena rittā va  sārena kadalī yathā   aptha          
 pacchime bhave sampatte brahmabandhu ahos  ahaṃ  
 koṭiyo sataṃ  chaḍḍayitvā pabbajim  anāgāriyaṃ   aptha          
 paṭhamaka bhāṇavāraṃ  
 ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū  
 brāhmaṇo sañjayo nāma tassa mūle vasām  ahaṃ   aptha          
 sāvako te mahāvīra assaji nāma brāhmaṇo  
 durāsado uggatejo piṇḍāya carati sadā   aptha          
 tam addasāsiṃ sappaññaṃ muniṃ mone samāhitaṃ  
 santacittaṃ mahānāgaṃ  suphullaṃ padumaṃ yathā   aptha          
 disvā me cittaṃ uppajji sudantaṃ suddhamānasaṃ  
 usabhaṃ pavaraṃ vīraṃ arahāyaṃ bhavissati   aptha          
 pāsādiko iriyati  abhirūpo susaṃvuto  
 uttame damathe danto amatadassī bhavissati   aptha          
 yannūnāhaṃ uttamatthaṃ puccheyyaṃ tuṭṭhamānasaṃ  
 so me puṭṭho kathessati  paṭipucchām  ahaṃ tadā   aptha          
 piṇḍacāraṃ   carantassa pacchato agamās  ahaṃ  
 okāsaṃ paṭimānento pucchituṃ amataṃ padaṃ   aptha          
 vīthantare   anuppattaṃ upagantvā apucchi haṃ   
 kathaṃ gotto si tvaṃ dhīra    kassa sisso si marisa   aptha          
 so me puṭṭho   vyākāsi asambhīto va kesarī   
 buddho loke samuppanno tassa sisso mhi sāvako   aptha

    sāriputta    
 kīdisaṃ te mahāvīra anujāta mahāyaso  
 buddhassa sāsanaṃ dhammaṃ sādhu me kathayass  ubho   aptha          
 so me puṭṭho kathī  sabbaṃ gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ padaṃ  
 taṇhasallassa hantāraṃ sabbadukkhapanūdanaṃ   aptha          
 ye dhammā hetuppabhavā tesaṃ hetuṃ tathāgato āha  
 tesañ ca yo nirodho evaṃ vādi mahāsamaṇo   aptha          
 so haṃ vissajjite pañhe paṭhamaṃ phalaṃ ajjhagaṃ   
 virajo vimalo āsiṃ  sutvāna jinasāsanaṃ   aptha          
 sutvāna munino vākyaṃ passitvā dhammaṃ uttamaṃ  
 pariyogāḷhasaddhammo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhās  ahaṃ   aptha          
  es  eva dhammo yadi tāvad eva paccavyathā padam asokaṃ  
 adiṭṭham abbhatītaṃ bahukehi kappanahutehi    aptha          
 sāhaṃ dhammaṃ gavesanto kutitthe sañcarim  ahaṃ  
 so me attho anuppatto kālo me na ppamajjituṃ   aptha          
 tosito haṃ assajinā patvāna acalaṃ padaṃ  
 sahāyakaṃ gavesanto assamam agamās  ahaṃ   aptha          
 dūrato va mamaṃ disvā sahāyo me susikkhito  
 iriyāpathasampanno idaṃ vacanam abravī   aptha          
 pasannamukhanetto si muni munibhāvo va  dissati  
 amatādhigato kacci  nibbānaṃ accutaṃ padaṃ   aptha          
 subhānurūpo āyāsi anejjaṅkārito  viya  
 danto ca uttamadamathe upasanto si brāhmaṇa   aptha          
 amataṃ mayā dhigataṃ sokasallavinodanaṃ  
 tuvam pi adhigacche hi  gacchāma buddhasantikaṃ   aptha          
 sādhū ti so paṭissutvā  sahāyo me susikkhito  
 hatthena hatthaṃ gaṇhitvā upāgamī   satthusantikaṃ     aptha          
 ubho pi pabbajissāma sakyaputta tav  antike  
 tava sāsanam āgamma viharāma anāsavā   aptha          
 kolito iddhiyā seṭṭho  ahaṃ paññāya pārago  
 ubho ca ekato   hutvā sāsanaṃ sobhayāmase    aptha

 apariyositasaṅkappo kutitthe sañcarim  ahaṃ  
 tava dassanam āgamma saṅkappo pūrito mama   aptha          
 paṭhaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya pupphanti samaye dumā  
 dibbā gandhā sampavanti tosenti sabbapāṇinaṃ   aptha          
 tath  evāhaṃ mahāvīra sakyaputta mahāyasa   
 sāsane te patiṭṭhāya samay  esāmi pupphituṃ   aptha          
 vimuttipuppham esanto bhavasaṃsāramocanaṃ  
 vimutti pupphalābhena tosemi sabbapāṇinaṃ   aptha          
 yāvatā buddhakhettamhi ṭhapetvāna mahāmuniṃ  
 paññāya sadiso n  atthi tava puttassa cakkhumā   aptha          
 suvinītā ca te sissā parisā ca susikkhitā  
 uttame damathe dantā parivārenti taṃ  sadā   aptha          
 jhāyī jhāna ratā dhīrā santacittā  samāhitā  
 munī moneyya sampannā parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 appicchā nipakā dhīrā appāhārā alolupā  
 lābhālabhena santuṭṭhā parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 āraññakā dhutaratā jhāyino lūkhacīvarā  
 vi vekābhiratā dhīrā parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 paṭipannā phalaṭṭhā ca sekhā phalasamaṅgino  
 āsiṃsakā uttamatthaṃ parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 sotāpannā ca vimalā sakadāgāmino ca ye  
 anāgāmī ca arahā parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
  satipaṭṭhā nakusalā bojjhaṅgābhāvanāratā  
 sāvakā te bahū sabbe parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 iddhipādesu kusalā samādhibhāvanāratā  
 sammappadhānam anuyuktā  parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 tevijjā  chaḷabhiññā ca iddhiyā pārami ṅgatā  
 paññāya pāramīpattā  parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 edisā te mahāvīra tava sissā susikkhitā  
 durāsadā uggatejā parivārenti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 tehi sissehi parivuto saññatehi tapassihi  
 migarājā v  asambhīto  uḷurājā va sobhasi    aptha          
 paṭhaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya ruhanti dharaṇīruhā  
 vepullataṃ papuṇanti phalan ca dassayanti te   aptha

    sāriputta    
 paṭhavī sadiso tvaṃ si  sakyaputta mahāyasa  
 sāsane te patiṭṭhāya labhanti amataṃ phalaṃ   aptha          
 sindhū sarasvatī c  eva nadiyā candabhāgiyo  
 gaṅgā ca yamunā c  eva sarabhū ca atho mahī    aptha          
 etāsaṃ sandamānānaṃ sāgaro sampaṭicchati  
 jahanti purimaṃ nāmaṃ sāgaro te va ñāyati    aptha          
 tath  ev  ime catuvaṇṇā pabbajitvā tav  antike  
 jahanti purimaṃ nāmam buddhaputtā ti ñāyare   aptha          
 yathāpi cando vimalo gacchaṃ ākāsadhātuyā   
 sabbe tārāgaṇe  loke ābhāya atirocati   aptha          
 tath  eva tvaṃ mahāvīra parivuto devamānuse   
 buddhakhettaṃ  atikkamma jalasi sabbadā  tuvaṃ   aptha          
 gambhīre uṭṭhitā ūmi na velam ativattati  
 sabbavelam paphusanti  sañcuṇṇā   vikiranti tā   aptha          
 tath  eva titthiyā loke nānādiṭṭhī bahujjanā  
 dhammaṃ dhāritukāmā   te n  ātivattanti taṃ muniṃ   aptha          
 sac  eva taṃ pāpuṇanti paṭivādehi   cakkhuma  
 tav antikaṃ upāgantvā sañcuṇṇā va bhavanti te   aptha          
 yathāpi udake jātā kumudā mandālakā   bahū  
 upalimpanti toyena kaddamakalalena ca   aptha          
 tath  eva bahukā sattā loke jātā virūhare  
 aṭṭitā rāgadosena kaddame kumudaṃ yathā   aptha          
 yathā padumaṃ jalajaṃ jalamajjhe virūhati    
 na so limpati toyena parisuddho hi kesarī   aptha          
 tath eva tvaṃ mahāvīra loke jāto mahāmuni  
 no palimpasi   lokena   toyena padumaṃ yathā   aptha          
 yathāpi rammake māse bahū pupphanti vārijā  
 nātikkamanti   taṃ māsaṃ samayo pupphanāya so   aptha

    therāpadāna 
 tath  eva tvaṃ sakyaputta  pupphitā te vimuttiyā  
 sāsanaṃ nātivattanti padumaṃ vārijaṃ  yathā   aptha          
 supupphito sālarājā dibbagandhaṃ pavāyati  
 aññasālehi parivuto sālarājā va sobhati   aptha          
 tath  eva tvaṃ mahāvīra buddhañāṇena pupphito  
 bhikkhusaṅghena parivuto sālarājā va sobhasi    aptha          
 yathāpi selo himavā osadho sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 nāgānam asurānañ ca devatānañ ca ālayo   aptha          
 tath  eva tvaṃ mahāvīra osadho viya pāṇinaṃ  
 tevijjā chaḷabhiññā ca iddhiyā pāramiṅgatā   aptha          
 anusiṭṭhā mahāvīra tayā kāruṇikena te  
 ramanti dhammaratiyā vasanti tava sāsane   aptha          
 migarājā yathā sīho abhinikkhamma āsayā   
 catuddisā viloketvā  tikkhattuṃ abhinādayi   aptha          
 sabbe  mi gā uttasanti migarājassa gajjato   
 tathā hi jātimā eso pasu tāseti  sabbadā   aptha          
 gajjato  te mahāvīra vasudhā sampakampati   
 bodhaneyyā va   bojjhanti tasanti mārakāyikā   aptha          
 tasanti titthiyā sabbe nadato te mahāmuni    
 kākasenā va   vibbhantā migaraññā yathā migā   aptha          
 ye keci gaṇino loke satthāro ti pavuccare  
 paramparāgataṃ dhammaṃ desenti parisāya te   aptha          
 na h  eva tvaṃ mahāvīra dhammaṃ desesi pāṇinaṃ  
 samaṃ saccāni bujjhitvā kevalaṃ bodhipakkhikaṃ   aptha          
 āsayānusayaṃ ñatvā indriyānaṃ phalāphalaṃ    
 bhabbābhabbe   viditvāna mahāmegho   va gajjasi   aptha          
 cakkavālapariyantā   nisinnā parisā bhave  
 nānādiṭṭhī vicintenti   vimaticchedanāya taṃ   aptha

    sāriputta    
 sabbesaṃ cittam aññāya opammakusalo muni  
 ekaṃ pañhaṃ kathento va  vimatin chindi  pāṇinaṃ   aptha          
 upadisasadiseh  eva vāsudhā pūritā bhave  
 sabbe va te pañjalikā kittayuṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha          
 kappaṃ vā te kittayantā nānāvaṇṇehi kittayuṃ  
 parimetuṃ na pappeyyum  appameyyo tathāgato   aptha          
 yathā  sakena thāmena  kittito hi mahājino  
 kappakoṭī pakittentā evamevam  akittayuṃ   aptha          
 sace hi koci devo vā manusso vā susikkhito  
 pūritaṃ  parikaḍḍheyya  vighātaṃ va labheyya so   aptha          
 sāsane te patiṭṭhāya sakyaputta mahāyasa  
 paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā viharāmi anāsavo   aptha          
 titthiye sampamaddāmi vattemi jinasāsanaṃ  
 dhammasenāpati ajja sakyaputtassa sāsane   aptha          
 aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha  
 sukhito   saravego va   kilese jhāpayī   mamaṃ     aptha          
 yo koci manujo bhāraṃ dhāreyya matthake sadā  
 bhārena dukkhito assa bhāro hi   bharito tathā   aptha          
 dayhamāno tīhaggīhi   bhavesu saṃsariṃ ahaṃ  
 bharito bhavabhārena girim uccārito   yathā   aptha          
 oropito ca me bhāro  bhavā ugghāṭitā mayā  
 karaṇīyaṃ kataṃ sabbaṃ sakyaputtassa sāsane   aptha          
 yāvatā buddhakhettamhi ṭhapetvā sakyapuṅgavaṃ  
 aham aggo mhi paññāya sadiso me na vijjati   aptha          
 samādhimhi sukusalo iddhiyā pāramiṅgato  
 icchamāno va haṃ   ajja sahāyam   abhinimmine   aptha

    therāpadāna 
 anupubbavihārissa vasībhūto mahāmuni    
 kathesi sāsanaṃ  mayhaṃ  nirodho sayanaṃ mamaṃ    aptha          
 dibbacakkhuṃ  visuddham me samādhikusalo ahaṃ  
 sammappadhānam anuyutto bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato   aptha          
 sāvakena hi pattabbaṃ sabbam eva kataṃ mamaṃ   
 lokanāthaṃ ṭhapetvāna sadiso me na vijjati   aptha          
 samāpattivinayakusalo  jhānavimokkhānaṃ khippalābhī   
 bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato  sāvakaguṇapāramiṅgato  smiṃ   aptha          
 sāvakaguṇenāpi phusena buddhiyā purisuttamagāravā  
 saddhāya saṅgahītaṃ cittaṃ sadā sabrahmacārisu     aptha          
 uddhataviso va sappo chinnavisāno va usabho  
 nikkhittamānadappo upemi garugāravena gaṇaṃ   aptha          
 yadi rūpinī bhaveyya paññā me vasupatīnaṃ   sameyya   
 anomadassissa bhagavato phalam etaṃ ñāṇaṃ thavanāya     aptha          
 pavattitaṃ dhammacakkaṃ sakyaputtena tādinā  
 anuvattem  ahaṃ sammā ñāṇathavanāy   idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha          
 mā me kadāci pāpiccho kusīto hīnavīriyo  
 appassuto anācāro sameto   katthaci ahu   aptha          
 bahussuto ca medhāvī sīlesu susamāhito    
 cetosamathānuyukto   api muddhani tiṭṭhatu   aptha          
 taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddante yāvant  ettha samāgatā  
 appicchā hotha santuṭṭhā jhāyī jhānaratā sadā   aptha

    mahā moggallāna    
 yam ahaṃ paṭhamaṃ disvā virajo vimalo ahuṃ  
 so me ācariyo vīro  assaji nāma sāvako   aptha          
 tassāhaṃ vāhasā ajja dhammasenāpatī ahuṃ  
 sabbattha pāramiṃ patvā  viharāmi anāsavo   aptha          
 yo me ācariyo āsi assaji nāma sāvako  
 yassaṃ disāyaṃ vasati ussīsamhikaro  ahaṃ   aptha          
 mama kammaṃ saritvāna gotamo sakyapuṅgavo  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ   aptha          
 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime  
 chaḍābhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsasanaṃ ti  aptha          
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sāriputto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
 sāriputtattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
     mahā moggallāna   
 anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 vihāsi himavantamhi devasaṅghapurakkhato   aptha        
 varūṇo nāma nāmena nāgarājā ahaṃ tadā  
 kāmarūpī  vikubbāmi mahodadhi nivās  ahaṃ   aptha        
 saṅganiyaṃ gaṇaṃ  hitvā turiyaṃ paṭṭhapes  ahaṃ  
 sambuddhaṃ parivāretvā vādesuṃ accharā tadā  aptha        
 vajjamānesu turiyesu  devā turiyāni  vajjiṃsu  
 ubhiṇṇaṃ saddaṃ sutvāna buddho pi sampabujjhatha   aptha        
 nimantayitvā sambuddhaṃ sakaṃ bhavanam upāgamiṃ   
 āsanaṃ paññapetvāna kālam ārocayim ahaṃ   aptha        
 khīṇāsavasahassehi purato lokanāyako  
 obhāsento   disā sabbā bhavanam me upāgami   aptha

    therāpadāna 
 upaviṭṭhaṃ mahāvīraṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 bhikkhusaṅghaṃ santappesiṃ  annapānen  ahaṃ tadā   aptha        
 anumodi mahāvīro sayambhu aggapuggalo  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha        
 yo  so saṅghaṃ apūjesi buddhañ ca lokanāyakaṃ  
 tena cittappasādena devalokaṃ gamissati   aptha        
 sattasattatikkhattuñ ca devarajjaṃ karissati  
 paṭhavyarajjaṃ  aṭṭhasataṃ vasudham āvasissati   aptha         
 pañcapaññāsakkhattuṃ ca cakkavatti bhavissati  
 bhogā asaṅkhiyā  tassa uppajjissanti  tāvade   aptha         
 aparimeyye ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha         
 nirayā so cavitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati  
 kolito nāma nāmena brahmabandhu bhavissati   aptha         
 so pacchā pabbajitvāna kusalamūlena codito  
 gotamassa bhagavato dutiyo hessati sāvako   aptha         
 āraddhavīriyo pahitatto iddhiyā pāramiṅgato  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo   aptha         
 pāpamittopanissāya kāmarāgavasaṅgato  
 mātaraṃ pitaraṃ cāpi ghātayiṃ  duṭṭhamānaso   aptha         
 yaṃ yaṃ yon  upapajjāmi  nirayaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 pāpakammasamaṅgīnaṃ bhinnasīso bhavām  ahaṃ   aptha         
 idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo  
 idhāpi ca disaṃ  mayhaṃ   maraṇakāle bhavissati   aptha         
 pavivekaṃ anuyutto samādhibhāvanārato  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha         
 dharaṇiṃ pi sugambhīraṃ bahalaṃ duppadhaṃsiyaṃ  
 vāmaṅguṭṭhena   khobheyyam   iddhiyā pāramiṃgato     aptha         
 asmimānaṃ na passāmi māno mayhaṃ na vijjati  
 sāmaṇere   upādāya garucittaṃ karom  ahaṃ   aptha         
 aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ kammaṃ abhinīhariṃ  
 tāhaṃ   bhumiṃ anuppatto patto mhi āsavakkhayaṃ   aptha

     mahā kassapa  
 padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 nibbute lokanāthamhi pūjaṃ kubbanti satthuno  
 udaggacittā janatā āmoditapamoditā   aptha        
 tesu saṃvegajātesu pīti me udapajjatha   
 ñatimitte samānetvā  idaṃ vacanam abraviṃ    
  parinibbuto mahāvīro handa pūjaṃ karomase    aptha        
 sadhū ti te paṭissutvā bhiyyo hāsaṃ  janiṃsu  me  
 buddhasmiṃ lokanāthasmiṃ kāhāma puññasañcayaṃ   aptha        
 agghiyaṃ sukataṃ katvā satahatthaṃ samuggataṃ

    apadāna 
 sahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ  dibbaṃ yānam  adhiṭṭhito  
 ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ sattabhūmi  samuggataṃ  aptha        
 kūṭāgārasahassāni sabbe sovaṇṇayā ahuṃ   
 jalanti sakatejena  disā sabbā pabhāsayaṃ   aptha        
 santi aññe pi  niyyuhā lohitaṅkamayā tadā  
 te pi jotanti ābhāya samantā caturo disā  aptha         
 puññakammābhinibbattā kūṭāgārā sunimmitā  
 maṇimayāpi jotanti disādasa samantato   aptha         
 tesaṃ ujjotamānānaṃ obhāso vipulo  ahu  
 sabbe deve atibhomi  puññakammass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 saṭṭhikappasahassamhi  ubbiddho   nāma khattiyo  
 caturanto vijitāvī puṭhaviṃ āvasiṃ ahaṃ   aptha         
 tamh  eva   bhaddake kappe tiṃsakkhattuṃ   ahos ahaṃ  
 sakakammābhiraddho   mhi cakkavatti mahabbalo     aptha         
 sattaratanasampanno cātudīpamhi issaro  
 tatthāpi bhavanaṃ   mayhaṃ indalaṭṭhi va uggataṃ  aptha         
 āyāmato catubbīsaṃ   vitthārena ca dvādasā   
 rammakaṃ nāma naṅgaraṃ   daḷhapākāratoraṇaṃ   aptha         
 āyāmato pañcasataṃ vitthārena tadaḍḍhakaṃ  
 ākiṇṇaṃ janakāyehi tidasānaṃ puraṃ viya   aptha         
 yathā sucighare sucipakkhittā paṇṇuvīsati  
 aññamaññam saṅghaṭṭhenti ākiṇṇaṃ hoti taṃ tadā     aptha         
 evam pi nagaraṃ mayhaṃ hatthassarathasaṅkulaṃ  
 manussehi tadākiṇṇaṃ rammakaṃ naṅgaruttamaṃ   aptha         
 tattha bhutvā ca pitvā   ca puna devattataṃ gato    
 bhave pacchimake mayhaṃ ahosi kulasampadā   aptha

     anuruddha  
 sumedhaṃ bhagavantāhaṃ  lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 vupakaṭṭhaṃ viharantaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha

 añjalim  paggahetvāna buddhaseṭṭham ayāc  ahaṃ   aptha        
  anukampī  mahāvīra lokajeṭṭha narāsabha   
 padīpan te padassāmi  rukkhamūlamhi jhāyato    aptha        
 adhivāsesi so dhīro   sayambhū vadataṃ varo    
 dumesu vinivijjhitvā yantaṃ yojetv   ahaṃ tadā   aptha

 samantato pajjalati dīpadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

 tiṃsakappāni devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 na maṃ  kec  atimaññanti dīpadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha        
 aṭṭhavīsatikkhattuñ ca cakkavattī ahos ahaṃ  
 divārattiñ ca passāmi samantā yojanaṃ tadā   aptha         
 sahassalokaṃ ñāṇena passāmi satthu sāsane  
 dibbacakkhuṃ anuppatto dīpadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 sumedho nāma sambuddho tiṃsakappasahass  ito  
 tassa dīpo mayā dinno vippasannena cetasā   aptha         
 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime  
 chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   aptha         
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anuruddhatthero imā gāthāyo bhāsitthāti  
 anuruddhattherassa apadānaṃsamattaṃ  
  
     puṇṇa mantāniputta  
 ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragū  
 purakkhato smi  sissehi upagacchiṃ  naruttamaṃ   aptha        
 padumuttaro lokavidū ahutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mama kammaṃ pakittesi saṅkhittena mahāmuni   aptha        
 tāhaṃ dhammaṃ suṇitvāna abhivādetvāna satthuno  
 añjalim  paggahetvāna pakkāmiṃ dakkhiṇāmukho   aptha        
 saṅkhittena suṇitvāna vitthārena adesayiṃ   
 sabbe sissā attamanā sutvāna mama bhāsato   aptha        
 sakadiṭṭhiṃ  vinodetvā buddhe  cittaṃ pasādayuṃ  
 saṅkhittena pi desemi vitthārena tath ev ahaṃ   aptha

 ito pañcasate kappe caturo suppakāsakā

     upāli  
 naṅgare  haṃsavatiyā sujāto  nāma brāhmaṇo  
 asītikoṭinicayo  pahūtadhanadhaññavā   aptha        
 ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragū   
 lakkhaṇe itibhāse  ca saddhamme  pāramiṅgato   aptha        
 paribbājā ekasikhā gotamabuddhasāvakā  
 carakā tāpasā  c  eva caranti mahiyā tadā  aptha        
  te pi maṃ parivārenti  brāhmaṇo vissuto iti   
 bahujjano maṃ pūjeti   nāhaṃ pūjemi   kañcinaṃ     aptha        
 pūjārahaṃ na passāmi mānatthaddho ahaṃ tadā  
 buddho ti vacanaṃ natthi tāva nuppajjate jino   aptha        
 accayena ahorattaṃ   padumuttaranāyako  
 sabbaṃ tamaṃ vinodetvā loke uppajji cakkhumā   aptha        
 vitthārike   bahujaññe puthubhūte   ca sāsane  
 upāgami tadā buddho naṅgaraṃ   haṃsasavhayaṃ     aptha

    apadāna 
 parūpatthā ya  so buddho dhammaṃ desesi cakkhumā  
 tena kālena parisā samantā yojanaṃ  tadā   aptha        
 sammato  manujānaṃ so  sunando nāma tāpaso  
 yāvatā buddhaparisā puppheh  acchādayī  tadā   aptha        
 catusaccaṃ pakāsento seṭṭhe va  pupphamaṇḍape   
 koṭisatasahassānaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu   aptha         
 sattarattindivaṃ buddho vassitvā  dhammavuṭṭhiyā  
 aṭṭhame  divase patte sunandaṃ kittayi jino   aptha         
 devaloke manusse vā saṃsaranto ayaṃ   bhave  
 sabbesaṃ pavaro hutvā bhaveussaṃsarissati   aptha         
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha         
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 mantāṇiputto puṇṇo ti hessati satthu sāvako   aptha         
 evaṃ kittayi sambuddho   sunandaṃ tāpasaṃ tadā  
 hāsayanto   janaṃ sabbaṃ dassayanto sakaṃ balaṃ   aptha         
 katañjalī namassanti sunandaṃ tāpasaṃ tadā  
 buddhe kāraṃ karitvāna sodhesi gatim attano   aptha         
 tattha me ahu saṅkappo sutvāna munino vacaṃ    
 aham pi kāraṃ   karissāmi yathā passāmi gotamaṃ   aptha         
 evāhaṃ cintayitvāna kiriyaṃ cintayiṃ mamaṃ    
 kyāhaṃ   kammaṃ ācarāmi puññakkhette anuttare   aptha         
 ayaṃ ca pāṭhiko bhikkhu sabbapāṭhikasāsane    
 vinaye agganikkhitto taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthaye ahaṃ   aptha         
 idaṃ me amitaṃ bhogaṃ akkhobhaṃ   sāgarūpamaṃ  
 tena bhogena buddhassa ārāmaṃ māpaye ahaṃ   aptha         
 sobhanaṃ nāma ārāmaṃ naṅgarassa   puratthato  
 katvā satasahassena saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ     aptha

 kūṭāgāre ca pāsāde maṇḍape kammiye guhā   
 caṅkame sukate katvā saṅghārāmaṃ  amāpayiṃ   aptha         
 jantāgharaṃ aggisālaṃ adho  udakamālakaṃ  
 nahānagharaṃ  māpayitvā bhikkhusaṅghass  adās  ahaṃ   aptha         
 āsandiyo  pīṭhake ca paribhoge ca bhājane  
 ārāmikañ ca bhesajjaṃ sabbam etaṃ adās  ahaṃ   aptha         
 ārakkhaṃ paṭṭhapetvāna pākāraṃ kārayiṃ  daḷhaṃ  
 mā naṃ koci viheṭhesi santacittāna  tādinaṃ   aptha         
 āvāsasatasahassena  saṅghārāmaṃ  amāpayiṃ  
 vepullataṃ pāpayitvā sambuddhaṃ upanāmayiṃ     aptha         
 niṭṭhāpito mayārāmo   sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ muni  
 niyyātessāmi   te vīra   adhivāsehi cakkhumā   aptha         
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mama saṅkappam aññāya adhivāsesi nāyako   aptha         
 adhivāsanam aññāya sabbaññussa mahesino  
 bhojanaṃ paṭiyādetvā   kālam ārocayiṃ ahaṃ   aptha         
 ārocitamhi kālamhi padumuttaranāyako  
 khīṇāsavasahassehi ārāmaṃ me upāgami   aptha         
 nisinnaṃ kālam   aññāya annapānena tappayiṃ    
 bhuttāviṃkālam   aññāya idaṃ vacanam abraviṃ     aptha         
  kīto satasahassena tattaken  eva kārito  
 sobhano nāma ārāmo sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ mune     aptha         
 iminārāmadānena   cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 bhave nibbattamāno haṃ labhāmi mama patthitaṃ   aptha         
 paṭiggahetvā sambuddho saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃ    
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā idaṃ vacanam abravi     aptha         
  yo so buddhassa pādāsi saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃ  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha

    apadāna 
 hatthī assā rathā pattī senā ca caturaṅginī  
 parivāressant  imaṃ niccaṃ  saṅghārāmass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 saṭṭhiṃ  turiyasahassāni bheriyo  samalaṅkatā  
 parivāressant  imaṃ niccaṃ  saṅghārāmass  idan phalaṃ   aptha         
 chalāsītisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā  
 vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā   aptha         
 āḷārāpamhā  hasulā  susaññā tanumajjhimā  
 parivāressant  imaṃ niccaṃ  saṅghārāmass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati  
 sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati   aptha         
 devarājena pattabbaṃ sabbaṃ paṭilabhissati  
 anūnabhogo hutvāna devarajjaṃ karissati   aptha         
 sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavatti rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati  
 pathavyā rajjaṃ vipulaṃ  gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ    aptha         
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha         
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 upāli nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   aptha         
 vinaye pāramippatto   ṭhānāṭhāne ca kovido  
 jinasāsanaṃ dhārento   viharissat  anāsavo      aptha         
 sabbam etaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavo  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapessati   aptha         
 aparimeyy  upādāya patthemi tava sāsanaṃ  
 so me attho anuppatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo   aptha         
 yathā sūlāvuto poso rājadaṇḍena tajjito  
 sūle sātaṃ na vindanto   parimuttiṃ va icchati   aptha         
 tath  evāhaṃ mahāvīra bhavadaṇḍena tajjito  
 kammasūlāvuto santo pipāsāvedanāṭṭito   aptha         
 bhave sātaṃ na vindāmi ḍayhanto tīhi aggihi  
 parimuttiṃ gavesāmi yathāpi rājadaṇḍito     aptha

 agadaṃ  so gaveseyya visaghātāy  upāyaso    aptha

 tam pivitvā sukhī assa visamhā parimuttiyā   aptha         
 tath  evāhaṃ mahāvīra yathā visahato  naro  
 sampīḷito  avijjāya saddhammāgadaṃ  esahaṃ   aptha

 tassā vassasahassena ekaṃ nibbattate phalaṃ   aptha

 vinaye pāramiṃ patto yathā pi pāṭhiko  isi  
 na me  samasamo atthi  dhāremi sāsanaṃ ahaṃ   aptha         
 vinaye khandhake cāpi tikacchede va pañcake  
 ettha me vimati  n  atthi akkhare vyañjane pi vā    aptha         
 niggahe paṭikamme ca ṭhānāṭhāne ca kovido  
 osāraṇe vuṭṭhāpane sabbaṭṭha pāramiṅgato   aptha         
 vinaye khandhake cāpi nikkhipitvā padaṃ ahaṃ  
 ubhato  viniveṭhetvā rasato osāreyy  ahaṃ   aptha         
 niruttiyā ca kusalo atthānatthe  ca kovido  
 anaññātaṃ mayā n  atthi ekaggo satthu sāsane   aptha         
 rūpadakkho ahaṃ ajja sakyaputtassa sāsane  
 kaṅkhaṃ sabbaṃ  vinodemi chindāmi sabbasaṃsayaṃ   aptha         
 padaṃ anupadañ cāpi akkharañ cāpi vyañjanaṃ  
 nidāne pariyosāne sabbattha kovido ahaṃ   aptha         
 yathāpi rājā balavā niggaṇhitvā paran tape   
 vijinitvāna   saṅgāmaṃ naṅgaraṃ tattha māpaye   aptha         
 pākāraṃ parikhañ   cāpi esikañ dvārakoṭṭhakaṃ  
 aṭṭālake ca vividhe kāraye naṅgare bahū   aptha         
 siṅghāṭakaṃ caccarañ ca suvibhattantarāpaṇaṃ  
 kārayeyya sabhaṃ   tattha atthānatthaṃ vinicchayaṃ   aptha         
 nigghāṭatthaṃ   amittānaṃ chiddāchiddañ ca jānituṃ    
 rakkhāya   balakāyassa senāpaccam ṭhapeti so   aptha         
 ārakkhatthāya bhaṇḍassa nidhānakusalaṃ naraṃ  
  mā me bhaṇḍaṃ vinassī  ti bhaṇḍarakkhaṃ   ṭhapeti   so   aptha         
 māmako   hoti yo rañño vuddhiṃ yassa   ca icchati  
 tassādhikaraṇaṃ deti mittassa paṭipajjituṃ     aptha         
 uppādesu nimittesu lakkhaṇesu ca kovidaṃ  
 ajjhāyakaṃ mantadharaṃ porohicce ṭhapeti   so   aptha

    apadana 
 eteh  aṅgehi sampanno khattiyo ti pavuccati  
 sadā rakkhanti rājānaṃ cakkavāko va dukkhitaṃ    aptha         
 tath  eva tvaṃ mahāvīra hatāmitto va khattiyo  
 sadevakassa lokassa dhammarājā ti vuccati    aptha         
 titthiye nihanitvāna  mārañ cāpi sasenakaṃ  
 tam andhakāraṃ vidhamitvā dhammanaṅgaraṃ amāpayi    aptha         
 sīlaṃ pākārikaṃ tattha ñāṇan te dvārakoṭṭhakaṃ  
 saddhā te esikā dhīra dvārapālo va  saṃvaro   aptha         
 satipaṭṭhānam aṭṭālaṃ  paññā te caccaraṃ mune  
 iddhipādañ ca siṅghāṭaṃ dhammavīthiṃ  sumāpitaṃ   aptha         
 suttantaṃ abhidhammañ ca vinayañ cāpi kevalaṃ  
 navaṅgabuddhavacanaṃ ettha dhammasabhā tava    aptha         
 suññatam animittañ ca  vihārañ cāppanīhitaṃ  
 anejañ  ca  nirodho   ca esā dhammakuṭi tava   aptha         
 paññāya aggo nikkhitto paṭibhāne ca kovido  
 sāriputto ti nāmena dhammasenāpatī tava   aptha         
 cutūpapātakusalo   iddhiyā pāramiṅgato  
 kolito nāma nāmena po rohicco tava mune   aptha          
 po rāṇakavaṃsadharo uggatejo durāsado  
 dhūtavādiguṇen  aggo akkhadasso tavaṃ   mune   aptha          
 bahussuto dhammadharo sabbapāṭhī   ca sāsane  
 ānando nāma nāmena dhammārakkho tavaṃ   mune   aptha          
 ete sabbe atikkamma pihesi   bhagavā mamaṃ    
 vinicchayam me pādāsi vinaye viññūdesitaṃ   aptha          
 yo koci vinaye pañhaṃ   pucchati buddhasāvako  
 tattha me cintanā   n  atthi tañ yev  atthaṃ   kathem  ahaṃ   aptha          
 yāvatā buddhakhettamhi ṭhapetvā taṃ mabāmuni    
 vinaye mādiso n  atthi  kuto bhiyyo bhavissati   aptha

 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā evaṃ gajjati gotamo   
 upālissa samo n  atthi vinaye khandhakesu ca  aptha          
 yāvatā buddhabhaṇitaṃ navaṅgaṃ  satthusāsanaṃ  
 vinayogadhitaṃ  sabbaṃ vinayamūlapassino    aptha          
 mama kammaṃ saritvāna gotamo sakyapuṅgavo  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ   aptha          
 satasahass  upādāya imaṃ ṭhānaṃ apatthayiṃ   
 so me attho anuppatto vinaye pāramiṅgato   aptha          
 sakyānaṃ nandijanano kappako ās  ahaṃ pure  
 vijahitvāna taṃ jātiṃ putto jāto mahesino   aptha          
 ito dutiyake kappe ajaso  nāma khattiyo  
 anantatejo  amitayaso bhūmipālo mahaddhano    aptha          
 tassa rañño ahaṃ putto candano nāma khattiyo  
 jātimaden  upatthaddho yasabhogamadena ca  aptha          
 nāgasatasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 tidhapabhinnā  mātaṅgā parivārenti maṃ sadā   aptha          
 sabalehi pareto  haṃ uyyānaṃ gantukāmako  
 āruyha sirikaṃ nāgaṃ   naṅgarā nikkhamiṃ   tadā   aptha

 devalo   nāma sambuddho āgacchi purato mamaṃ     aptha          
 pesetvā sirikaṃ nāgaṃ   buddhaṃ āsādayiṃ   tadā  
 tato sañjātakopo so nāgo nuddharate padaṃ   aptha

 vihesayitvā   sambuddhaṃ uyyānaṃ a gamās  ahaṃ    aptha          
 sātaṃ   tattha na vindāmi  siro pajjalito yathā  
 parilāhena ḍayhāmi maccho va baḷisādako     aptha

    apadāna 
 sasāgarantā pathavī ādittā viya hoti me  
 pitu santik  upāgamma idaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   aptha          
 āsīvisaṃ va kupitaṃ  aggikkhandham va āgataṃ  
 mattaṃ va kuñjaraṃ  dantiṃ yaṃ sayambhuṃ   asādayiṃ    aptha          
 āsādito mayā buddho ghoro uggatapo jino  
 purā  sabbe vinassāma khamāpessāma taṃ muniṃ   aptha          
 no ce taṃ nijjhapessāma attadantaṃ samāhitaṃ  
 orena sattame divase raṭṭhaṃ me vidhamissati    aptha          
 s umekhalo kosiyo  ca siggavo cāpi sattuko   
 āsādayitvā isayo duggatā te sasenakā    aptha          
 yadā kuppanti  isayo saññatā brahmacāriyo  
 sadevakaṃ vināsenti sasāgaraṃ  sapabbataṃ   aptha          
 tiyojanasahassamhi purise sanni pātayiṃ  
 accayaṃ desana tthāya sayambhuṃ   upasaṅkamiṃ   aptha          
 allavatthā allasirā sabbe va p  añjalīkatā  
 buddhassa pāde   nipatitvā   idaṃ vacanam abravuṃ   aptha          
  khamassu tvaṃ mahāvīra   abhiyācati taṃ jano  
 pariḷāhaṃ vinodehi  mā ca raṭṭhaṃ   vināsāya   aptha          
 sadevā manussā sabbe sadānavā sarakkhasā  
 ayo mayena kūṭena siraṃ   bhiñjeyyuṃ   me sadā   aptha          
 udake aggi na saṇṭhāti bījaṃ selena rūhati  
 agade   kimi na saṇṭhāti kopo buddhe na jāyati   aptha          
 yathāpi bhūmi acalā appameyyo ca   sāgaro  
 anantako ca ākāso evaṃ buddho  akhobhiyo    aptha          
 sadā khantā mahāvīra khamitā ca tapassino  
 khantānaṃ khamitānañ ca gamanaṃ vo na vijjati    aptha          
 idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho pariḷāhaṃ vinodayi    
 mahājanassa purato nabhaṃ abbhuggamī tadā   aptha

 tena  kammen  a haṃ dhīra  hīnattaṃ ajjhupāgato  
 samatikkamma taṃ  jātiṃ pāvisiṃ abhayaṃ puraṃ   aptha          
 tadāpi maṃ mahāvīra ḍayhamānaṃ susaṇṭhitaṃ   
 pariḷāhaṃ vinodesi sayambhuñ ca khamāpayiṃ    aptha          
 ajjāpi maṃ  mahāvīra ḍayhamānaṃ  tīh aggi hi  
 nibbāpesi tayo aggī sītibhāvañ ca pāpayi    aptha          
 yesaṃ sotāvadhān  atthi suṇotha mama bhāsato   
 atthaṃ tuyhaṃ pavakkhāmi yathā diṭṭhapadaṃ mamaṃ    aptha          
  sayambhuṃ  taṃ  vimānetvā santacittaṃ samāhitaṃ  
 tena kammen  a haṃ ajja jāto mhi nīcayoniyam  aptha          
 mā vo khaṇaṃ virādhetha  khaṇātītā hi socare   
 sadatthe vāyameyyātha khaṇo vo paṭipādito   aptha

 visaṃ haḷāhaḷaṃ ete   ekaccānañ ca osadhaṃ   aptha

 dhanapāle rāhule ca   sabbesaṃ samako muni   aptha

    apadāna 
 etesaṃ paṭighaṃ n  atthi  rāgo mesaṃ na vijjati  
 sabbesaṃ samako buddho  vadhakass orasassa ca    aptha          
 panthe disvāna kāsāvaṃ chaḍḍitaṃ mīḷhamakkhitaṃ  
 sirasā añjaliṃ  katvā vanditabbaṃ isiddhajaṃ   aptha          
 abbhātītā ca me buddhā vattamānā anāgatā  
 dhajenānena sujjhanti tasmā ete namassiyā   aptha          
 satthukappaṃ suvinayaṃ dhāremi hadayen  ahaṃ  
 namassamāno vinayaṃ viharissāmi sabbadā   aptha          
 vinayo āsayaṃ mayhaṃ vinayo ṭhānacaṅkamaṃ  
 kappemi vinaye  vāsaṃ vinayo mayhaṃ gocaro   aptha          
 vinaye pāramippatto  samathe cāpi kovido  
 upāli taṃ mahāvīra pāde vandati satthuno   aptha          
 so ahaṃ vicarissāmi gāmāgāmaṃ purāpuraṃ  
 namassamāno sambuddhaṃ dhammassa ca sudhammataṃ   aptha          
 kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā n  atthi dāni punabbhavo  aptha          
 sāgataṃ  vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ   aptha          
 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca atth  ime  
 chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   aptha          
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upālithero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
 upālittherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

 yāvatā bodhiyā mule yakkhā sabbe samāgatā  
 sambuddhaṃ parivāretvā vandanti pañjalīkatā    aptha

    aññākoṇḍañña    
 sabbe devā tuṭṭhamanā ākāse sañcaranti te  
 buddho ayaṃ anuppatto  andhakāratamonudo   aptha        
 tesaṃ hāsaparetānaṃ  mahānādo pavattatha   
 kilese jhāpayissāma  sammāsambuddhasāsane   aptha        
 devānaṃ giram aññāya vācāsabhiṃ udīritaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena ādibhikkham adās  ahaṃ   aptha        
 mamaṃ  saṅkappam aññāya satthā loke anuttaro  
 devasaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha        
  sattāhaṃ abhinikkhamma bodhim ajjhāgamam ahaṃ  
 idaṃ me paṭhamaṃ bhattaṃ brahmacārissa  yāpanaṃ    aptha        
 tusitāhi idhāgantvā yo me bhikkham upānayi  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha        
 tiṃsakappasahassena  devarajjaṃ karissati  
 sabbe deve atibhotvā tidivaṃ āvasissati   aptha        
 devalokā cavitvāna manussattaṃ  gamissati  
 sahassaṃ va   cakkavatti   tattha rajjaṃ karissati   aptha         
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha         
 tidasā so cavitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati  
 agārā pabbajitvāna chabbassāni vasissati   aptha         
 tato sattamake vasse buddho saccaṃ kathessati  
 koṇḍañño nāma nāmena paṭhamaṃ sacchikāhiti    aptha         
 nikkhantenānupabbajjaṃ   padhānaṃ sukataṃ mayā  
 kilese    jhāpanatthāya pabbaj iṃ anagāriyaṃ   aptha         
 abhigantvāna sabbaññū buddho loke sadevake  
 iminā me migāraññe amataṃ bherim āhani     aptha         
 so dāni patto amataṃ santaṃ padam   anuttaraṃ  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha

 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime

     piṇḍola bhāradvāja   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sayambhū aggapuggalo  
 purato himavantassa cittakūṭe  vasī tadā   aptha        
 abhītarūpo  tatthāsiṃ  migarājā catukkamo  
 yassa saddaṃ suṇitvāna vikkhambhanti bahū janā   aptha        
 suphullam padumaṃ gayha upagañchiṃ  narāsabhaṃ  
 vuṭṭhitassa samādhimhā buddhassa abhiropayiṃ    aptha        
 catuddisaṃ  namassitvā buddhaseṭṭhaṃ naruttamaṃ  
 sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā sīhanādam adās  ahaṃ    aptha        
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 sakāsane nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha        
 buddhassa giram aññāya sabbe devā samāgatā  
 āgato vadataṃ  seṭṭho dhammaṃ sossāma taṃ mayaṃ   aptha        
 tesaṃ hāsaparetānaṃ  purato lokanāyako  
 mama saddaṃ pakittesi dīghadassī mahāmuni   aptha        
  yen  idaṃ padumaṃ dinnaṃ sīhanādo ca nādito  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha   mama bhāsato   aptha        
 ito aṭṭhamake kappe cakkavatti bhavissati  
 sattaratanasampanno cātuddīpamhi   issaro   aptha        
 kārayissati issaraṃ mahiyā catusaṭṭhiyā  
 padumo nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahābalo   aptha

    khadiravaniya revata    
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha         
 pakāsite pāvacane brahmabandhu bhavissati  
 brahmaññā abhinikkhamma pabbajissati tāvade   aptha         
 padhānapahitatto  so upasanto nirūpadhi  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo   aptha         
 vipine  pantaseyyamhi vāḷamigasamākule  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo    aptha         
 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime  
 chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   aptha

     khadiravaniya revata   
 gaṅgā bhāgīrasī nāma himavantā pabhāvitā  
 kutitthe nāviko āsiṃ orime ca tariṃ ahaṃ   aptha        
 padumuttaranāyako sambuddho dīpaduttamo  
 vasīsatasahassehi gaṅgāsotaṃ tarissati   aptha        
 bahū nāvā samānetvā vaḍḍhakīhi susaṅkhataṃ  
 nāvāya chadanaṃ katvā paṭimānin  narāsabhaṃ   aptha        
 āgantvāna ca  sambuddho ā ruhi nāvalañcakaṃ   
 vārimajjhe ṭhi to satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha        
  yo so tāresi sambuddhaṃ saṅghaṃ cāpi anāsavaṃ  
 tena cittappasādena devaloke ramissati   aptha        
 nibbattissati te  vyamhaṃ  sukataṃ nāvasaṇṭhitaṃ  
 ākāse pupphachadanaṃ dhārayissati sabbadā   aptha        
 aṭṭhapaññāsakappamhi tāraṇo nāma khattiyo  
 cāturanto vijitāvī cakkavatti bhavissati   aptha

    therāpadāna 
 sattapaññāsakappamhi campako nāma khattiyo  
 uggacchanto va suriyo jotissati mahābalo   aptha        
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha        
 tidasā so cavitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati  
 revato nāma nāmena brahmabandhu bhavissati   aptha         
 agārā nikkhamitvāna sukkamūlena  codito  
 gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissati   aptha         
 so pacchā pabbajitvāna yuttayogo vipassako  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissati nāsavo    aptha         
 viriyam me dhuradhorayhaṃ yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ  
 dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane   aptha         
 paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime  
 chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   aptha         
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā khadiravaniyo revato thero imā 
 gāthāyo abhāsitthati  
 khadiravaniyo revatattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
      ānanda   
 ārāmādvārā nikkhamma padumuttaro mahāmuni  
 vassanto amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ  nibbāpesi  mahājanaṃ   aptha         
 satasahassāni  vīrā  chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā  
 parivārenti sambuddhaṃ chāyā va anapāyinī   aptha         
 hatthikkhandhagato āsiṃ setacchattam varuttamaṃ  
 sucārurūpaṃ disvāna vitti  me udapajjatha    aptha         
 oruyha hatthikkhandhamhā upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 ratanāmayachattam  me buddhaseṭṭhassa dhārayiṃ   aptha

     ananda    
 mama saṅkappam aññāya padumuttaro mahāisi  
 taṃ kathaṃ ṭhapayitvāna imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha         
  yo so chattaṃ adhāresi soṇṇalaṅkārabhūsitaṃ  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha         
 ito gantvā ayaṃ poso tusitaṃ āvasissati  
 anubhossati sampattiṃ  accharāhi purakkhato   aptha         
 catutiṃsatikkhattuñ  ca devarajjaṃ karissati  
 balādhipo aṭṭhasataṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati   aptha         
 aṭṭhapaññāsakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti bhavissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ mahiyā kā rayissati    aptha         
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha          
 sakyānaṃ kulaketussa ñātibandhu  bhavissati  
 ānando nāma nāmena upaṭṭhāko mahesino   aptha          
 ātā pī ni pako cāpi bāhusaccesu kovido  
 nivātavutti athaddho  sabbapāṭhī  bhavissati   aptha          
 padhānapahitatto  so upasanto nirūpadhi  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo    aptha          
 santi āraññakā nāgā kuñjarā saṭṭhihāyanā  
 tidhāppabhinnā mātaṅgā r īsādantā  urūḷhavā   aptha          
 anekasatasahassā paṇḍitā  pi mahiddhikā  
 sabbe te buddhanāgassa   na honti parivimhitā     aptha          
 ādiyāme   namassāmi majjhime atha pacchime  
 pasannacitto sumano buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ   aptha          
 ātāpī nipako cāpi sampajāno patissato  
 sotāpattiphalaṃ patto sekhabhūmisu   kovido   aptha          
 kappe to satasahasse   yaṃ kammam abhinīhariṃ  
 tāhaṃ   bhūmim anuppatto   ṭhito   saṅgama m ācalo     aptha

 sāgataṃ  vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike  
 tisso vijjā anuppatto kataṃ buddhassasāsanaṃ   aptha          
 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime  
 chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   aptha

     sīhāsanadāyaka    
  ii  sīhāsanavaggo   
  
      sīhāsanadāyaka   
 nibbute lokanāthamhi siddhatthe dipaduttame  
 vitthārite  pāvacane bāhujaññamhi sāsane  aptha         
 pasannacitto sumano sīhāsanam akās  ahaṃ  
 sīhāsanaṃ karitvāna pādapīṭhaṃ akās  ahaṃ   aptha         
 sīhāsane ca vassante  gharaṃ tattha akās  ahaṃ  
 tena cittappasādena tusitaṃ upapajj  ahaṃ   aptha         
 āyāmena catubbīsā yojanāsiṃsu tāvade  
 vimānaṃ sukataṃ mayhaṃ vitthārena catuddasaṃ  aptha         
 sattakaññā  sahassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā  
 soṇṇamayañ  ca pallaṅkaṃ vyamhe  āsi  sunimmitaṃ   aptha         
 hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ dibbayānaṃ  upaṭṭhitaṃ  
 pāsādā sivikā c  eva nibbattanti yadicchakaṃ   aptha         
 maṇimayā ca palla ṅkā aññe  sāramayā bahū  
 nibbattanti mamaṃ sabbe sīhāsanass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 soṇṇamayā rūpimayā phalikā veḷuriyāmayā  
 pādukā abhirūhāmi pādapīṭhass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 catunavute ito kappe yaṃ kammam akariṃ  tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi puññakammass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 tesattati ito kappe indanāmā tayo janā  
 dvesattati ito kappe tayo sumana nāmakā   aptha          
 samasattat  ito   kappe tayo varuṇa nāmakā  
 sattaratanasampannā catuddīpamhi issarā   aptha          
 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime  
 chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   aptha          
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sīhāsanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
 sīhāsanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

      ekatthambhika   
 siddhatthassa bhagavato mahāpūgagaṇo ahu  
 saraṇaṅgatā  ca te buddhaṃ saddahanti tathāgataṃ   aptha         
 sabbe saṅgamma  mantetvā māḷaṃ kubbanti satthuno  
 ekatthambhaṃ alabhantā vicinanti brahāvane   aptha         
 te  haṃ araññe disvāna upagamma gaṇaṃ tadā  
 añjalim  paggahetvāna paṭipucchiṃ  gaṇaṃ ahaṃ   aptha         
 te me puṭṭhā viyākaṃsu  sīlavanto upāsakā  
 mālaṃ  mayaṃ kattukāmā ekatthambho na labbhati    aptha         
 ekatthambhaṃ mamaṃ  detha ahaṃ dassami satthuno  
 āharissām  ahaṃ thambhaṃ appossukkā bhavantu te     aptha         
 te me thambhaṃ pavecchiṃsu   pasannā tuṭṭhamānasā  
 tato paṭinivattitvā   āgamaṃsu sakaṃ gharaṃ   aptha         
 aciraṃ gate   pūgagaṇe   thambhaṃ adās  ahaṃ tadā  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena paṭhamaṃ ussāpes  ahaṃ   aptha         
 tena cittappasādena vimānaṃ upapajj  ahaṃ  
 ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ satabhūmisamuggataṃ     aptha         
 vajjamānāsu bherisu parivārem   ahaṃ tadā  
 pañcapaññāsakappamhi rājā āsiṃ   yasodharo   aptha         
 tatthāpi bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ satabhūmisamuggataṃ    
 kūṭāgāravarūpetaṃ ekatthambhaṃ manoramaṃ   aptha          
 ekavīsatikappamhi udeno nāma khattiyo  
 tatrāpi bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ satabhūmisamuggataṃ     aptha          
 yaṃ yaṃ yon  upapajjāmi devattaṃ   atha mānusaṃ  
 anubhomi   sabbam etaṃ ekatthambhass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

      nanda   
 padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 vatthuttamaṃ mayā dinnaṃ sayambhussa mahesino   aptha         
 tam me buddho viyākāsi  jalajuttamanāyako    
  iminā vatthadānena hemavaṇṇo bhavissasi   aptha         
 dve sampattī anubhotvā kusalamūlehi codito  
 gotamassa bhagavato kaniṭṭho tvaṃ  bhavissasi   aptha         
 rāgaratto sukhasīlo kāmesu gedham āyuto  
 buddhena codito santo tato tvaṃ pabbajissasi   aptha         
 pabbajitvāna tvaṃ tattha kusalamūlena codito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissasi  nāsavo    aptha         
 sattakappasahassamhi  caturo celanāmakā  
 saṭṭhiṃ kappasahassāni  upacelā catujjanā   aptha         
 pañcakappasahassamhi celā  caturo janā  
 sattaratanasampannā catuddīpamhi issarā   aptha         
 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime  
 chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   aptha         
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nanda thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti  
 nandatherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

      culla panthaka   
 padumuttaro nāma jino āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 gaṇamhā vupakaṭṭho so himavante vasī tadā   aptha         
 aham pi himavantamhi vasāmi assame tadā  
 acirāgataṃ  mahāvīraṃ upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha         
 pupphacchattaṃ gahetvāna upagañchiṃ  narāsabhaṃ  
 samādhiṃ samāpajjantaṃ antarāyam akās  ahaṃ   aptha         
 ubho hatthehi paggayha pupphachattaṃ adās  ahaṃ  
 paṭiggahesi bhagavā padumuttaro mahāmuni   aptha         
 sabbe devā attamanā himavantam upenti te  
 sādhukāraṃ pavattiṃsu   anumodissati cakkhumā    aptha         
 idaṃ vatvāna te devā upagañchuṃ  naruttamaṃ  
 ākāse dhārayant  assa padumacchattam  uttamaṃ  aptha         
 padumachattaṃ  paggayha adāsi tāpaso mamaṃ  
  tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha         
 pañcavīsatikappāni devarajjaṃ karissati  
 catuttiṃsatikkhattuñ ca cakkavatti bhavissati   aptha         
 yaṃ yaṃ yoniṃ saṃsarati devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 abbhokāse patiṭṭhan taṃ padumaṃ dhārayissati   aptha         
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha          
 pakāsite pāvacane manussattaṃ labhissati  
 manomayamhi kāyamhi uttamo so bhavissati   aptha          
 dve bhātaro bhavissanti ubho pi  panthasavhayā   
 anubhotvā uttamatthaṃ jotayissanti sāsanan    aptha          
 aṭṭhārasañ ca vasso haṃ pabbajiṃ  anagāriyaṃ  
 visesāhaṃ na vindāmi sakyaputtassa sāsane   aptha          
 dandhā mayhaṃ gati āsi paribhūto  pure ahaṃ   
 bhā tā ca maṃ paṇāmesi   gaccha dāni sakaṃ gharaṃ    aptha          
 so haṃ paṇāmito santo saṅghārāmassa koṭṭhake  
 dummano tattha aṭṭhāsiṃ sāmaññasmiṃ apekhavā     aptha

     pilindavaccha    
 ath  ettha satthā āgañchi sīsaṃ mayhaṃ parāmasi  
 bāhāya maṃ gahetvāna  saṅghārāmaṃ pavesayi    aptha          
 anukampāya me satthā adāsī pādapuñchaniṃ   
 evaṃ suddhaṃ adhiṭṭhehi ekamantam adhiṭṭhitaṃ   aptha          
 hatthehi tam  ahaṃ gayha  sariṃ kokanadaṃ ahaṃ  
 tattha  cittaṃ vimuccī me arahattaṃ apāpuniṃ    aptha          
 manomayesu kāyesu sabbattha pāramiṅga to  
 sabbāsave pariññā ya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha

 cullapanthakassatherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
      pilindavaccha   
 nibbute lokanāthamhi sumedhe aggapuggale  
 pasannacitto sumano thūpapūjaṃ akās ahaṃ   aptha         
 ye ca khīṇāsavā tattha chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā  
 te saṃ tattha samānetvā  saṅghabhattaṃ akās  ahaṃ   aptha         
 sumedhassa bhagavato upaṭṭhāko tadā ahu  
 sumedho nāma nāmena anumodittha so tadā   aptha         
 tena cittappasādena vimānaṃ upapajj  ahaṃ  
 chaḷāsītisahassāni a ccharāyo ramiṃsu me   aptha         
 mam  eva anuvattanti sabbakāmehi tā sadā  
 aññe deve atibhomi puññakammass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 pañcavīsatikappamhi varuṇo nāma khattiyo  
 susuddhabhojano  āsiṃ  cakkavatti ahaṃ tadā   aptha         
 na te bījaṃ pavapanti  na pi nīyanti  naṅgalā  
 akaṭṭhapākimaṃ sāliṃ   paribhuñjanti mānusā   aptha

    therāpadāna 
 tattha rajjaṃ karitvāna devattaṃ puna gacch  ahaṃ   
 tadāpi edisā mayhaṃ nibbattā bhogasampadā   aptha         
 na maṃ mittā amittā vā  hiṃsanti sabbapāṇi no  
 sabbesam pi  piyo homi puññakammass idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha         
 tiṃsakappasahassamhi yaṃ dānam adadiṃ  tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi gandhālepass idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha          
  imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe eko āsi janādhipo  
 mahānubhāvo rājā si  cakkavatti mahābalo   aptha          
 so haṃ pañcasu sīlesu ṭhapetvā janataṃ bahuṃ  
 pāpetvā sugatiṃ yeva devatānaṃ piyo ahuṃ    aptha

      rāhula   
 padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
  sattabhūmimhi pāsā de adāsiṃ  santharaṃ  ahaṃ   aptha         
 khīṇāsavasahassehi parikiṇṇo mahāmuṇi  
 upāgami gandhakuṭim dipadindo  narāsabho   aptha         
 virocantaṃ  gandhakuṭiṃ devadevo narāsabho  
 bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā ima gāthā abhāsatha   aptha         
  yenāyaṃ jotito siyā ādāso va susanthato  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha         
 soṇṇamayā rūpimayā  atho veḷuriyāmayā  
 nibbattissanti ākāse ye keci manaso piyā   aptha

   s  adadī  
   g  rājāpi  
   g  s  adāsi  
   s  sapariṃ  s  gocaraṃ  cy  reads ādāsaṃ santharim ahaṃ  
   g  dvipadindo  
   s  virocanti  
   s  g  maṇimayā  
  
  page      
     rāhula    
 catusa ṭṭhi kkhattuñ de vindo devarajjaṃ karissa ti  
 sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavatti bhavissati anantarā    aptha         
 ekavīsatikappamhi vimalo nāma khattiyo  
 cāturanto vijitāvī cakkavatti bhavissati   aptha         
 naṅgaraṃ reṇuvatī  nāma iṭṭhakāhi sumāpitaṃ  
 āyāmato   tīṇisataṃ  caturassaṃ  samāyutaṃ    aptha         
 sudassano nāma pāsādo vissakammena  māpito  
 kūṭāgāravarūpeto sattaratanabhūsito   aptha         
 dasa saddā avivittaṃ vijjādharasamākulaṃ  
 sudassanaṃ va naṅgaraṃ devatānaṃ bhavissati   aptha          
 pabhā nigga cchate tassa ugga cchante va sūriye  
 virocissati taṃ niccaṃ samantā aṭṭhayojanaṃ   aptha          
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha          
 tusitāhi cavi tvāna su kkamūlena codito  
 gotamassa bhagavato atrajo so bhavissati   aptha          
 sace vaseyya āgāraṃ cakkavattī bhaveyya so   
 aṭṭhānaṃ etaṃ yaṃ tādi agāre ratim ajjhagā   aptha          
 ni kkhamitvā agāramhā  pabbajissati subbato  
 rāhulo nāma nāmena arahā so bhavissati   aptha          
 kikī va aṇḍaṃ rakkheyya camarī r iva  vāladhiṃ  
 nipako sīlasampanno mamaṃ rakkhi mahāmuni   aptha          
 tassāhaṃ dhamma m aññāya vihāsiṃ sāsa ne rato  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha          
 paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh  ime  
 chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   aptha          
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā rāhulo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthā ti  
 rāhuḷatherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

      upasena  vaṅgantaputta    
 padumuttaraṃ bhagavantaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 pabbhāramhi  nisinnaṃ taṃ  upagañchiṃ naruttamaṃ   aptha         
 kaṇikā raṃ  pupphitaṃ disvā vaṇṭaṃ  chetvān  ahaṃ tadā  
 alaṅkaritvā chattamhi buddhassa abhiropayiṃ   aptha         
 piṇḍapātañ ca pādāsiṃ  paramannaṃ subhojanaṃ  
 buddhena navame tattha samaṇe  aṭṭha bhojayiṃ   aptha         
 anumodi mahāvīro sayambhū aggapuggalo   
   iminā chattadā nena paramannappavecchanā    aptha         
 tena cittappasādena sampattim anubhossati   
 tiṃsakhattun ca devindo devarajjaṃ karissati   aptha         
 ekavīsatikhattuñ ca cakkavatti bhavissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha         
 yaṃ vadanti sumedho ti bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ    
 kappe to   satasahasse eso buddho bhavissati   aptha         
 sāsane dippamānamhi   manussattaṃ gamissati    
 upaseno ti nāmena hessati satthu sāvako    aptha         
 carimaṃ vat tate mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe sa mūhatā

     ratthapāla    
  
      ratthapāla   
 padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 varanāgo mayā  dinno r īsādanto  urūḷhavo   aptha         
 setacchattopasevito  sāthabbaṇo  sahatthipo   
 agghāpetvāna  taṃ sabbaṃ saṅghārāmam akārayiṃ   aptha         
 catupaññāsasahassāni  pāsāde kārayim  ahaṃ  
 mahābhattaṃ  karitvāna  niyyātesiṃ mahesino    aptha         
 anumodi mahāvīro sayambhū aggapuggalo  
 sabbe jane hāsayanto deseti  amataṃ padaṃ   aptha         
 tam me buddho viyākāsi jaladuttamanāyako    
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha         
   catupaññāsasahassāni pāsāde kārayiṃ ahaṃ   
 kathayissāmi vipākaṃ  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha         
 aṭṭhārasasahassāni kūṭāgārā bhavissare  
 vyamhuttamamhi   nibbattā sabbasoṇṇamayā ca te   aptha         
  paññāsakhat tuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  
 aṭṭhapaññāsakhattuñ ca cakkavatti bhavissati   aptha         
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha         
  devalokā  cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito  
 aḍḍhe   kule mahābhoge nibbattissati tāvade   aptha          
 so pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito  
 raṭṭhapālo ti nāmena hessati satthu sāvako  aptha          
 padhānapahitatto so upa santo nirūpa dhi  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo      aptha          
 uṭṭhāya abhinikkhamma jahitvā bhogasampadā  
 kheḷapiṇḍo va   bhogamhi pemaṃ mayhaṃ na vijjati   aptha

 viriyam me dhuradhorayhaṃ yogakkhemādivāhanaṃ

      sopāka   
 abbhāraṃ sodhayantassa  pavare pabbatuttame  
 siddhattho nāma bhagavā āgacchi mama santikaṃ   aptha         
 buddhaṃ upagataṃ disvā  lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 santharaṃ paññāpet vāna pupphāsanam adās  ahaṃ   aptha         
 pupphāsane nisīditvā siddhattho lokanāyako  
 mamañ ca gatim aññāya aniccattam  udāhari   aptha         
  aniccā vata saṅkhārā uppādavayadhammino  
 uppajjitvā nirujjhanti  tesaṃ vūpasamo sukho    aptha         
  idaṃ vatvāna sa bbaññū lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 nabham  abbhuggamī vīro  haṃsarājā va ambare   aptha         
 sakaṃ diṭṭhiṃ jahitvāna bhāvayāniccasaññ  ahaṃ  
 ekāhaṃ bhāvayitvāna tattha kālakato  ahaṃ   aptha         
 dvesampattī anubhotvā sukkamūlena codito  
  pacchime bhave  sampatte sapākaṃ yonupāgamiṃ    aptha         
 agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ  anagāriyaṃ  
 jātiyā sattavasso haṃ arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   aptha         
 āraddhaviriyo pahitatto sīlesu susamāhito  
  tosetvāna mahā nāgaṃ alatthaṃ upasampadaṃ   aptha

       sumaṅgala    
 āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmo haṃ paṭiyādetvāna  bhojanaṃ

 aṭṭhannaṃ payirupāsataṃ  bhuñjaṃ khīṇāsavā bahū

     subhūti    
  iii  subhutivaggo   
  
      subhūti   
 himavantass  avidūre nisabho nāma pabbato  
 assamo sukato mayhaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā   aptha         
 kosiyo nāma nāmena jaṭilo uggatāpano  
 ekākiko adutiyo vasāmi nisabhe tadā   aptha         
 phalaṃ mūlaṃ ca paṇṇañ  ca na bhuñjāmi ahaṃ tadā  
 pavattapaṇḍupattāhaṃ  upajīvāmi tāvade   aptha         
 nāhaṃ kopemi ājīvaṃ cajamāno pi jīvitaṃ  
 ārādhemi sakaṃ cittaṃ vivajjemi anesanaṃ   aptha         
 rāgupasaṅhitaṃ cittaṃ yadā uppajjate mamaṃ  
 sayaṃ va paccavekkhāmi ekaggo naṃ  damem  ahaṃ   aptha         
 rajjasi rajanīye ca dosanīye ca dussase  
 muyhase mohanīye ca nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ   aptha         
 visuddhānaṃ ayaṃ vāso nimmalānaṃ tapassinaṃ  
 mā kho visuddhaṃ dusesi nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ   aptha         
 āgāriko bhavitvāna sadā yuttaṃ  labhissasi  
 ubho pi mā  virādhesi nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ   aptha         
 chavālātaṃ yathā kaṭṭhaṃ  na kvaci kiccakārakaṃ   
 n  eva gāme araññe vā na hi taṃ  kaṭṭhasammataṃ   aptha         
 chavālātūpamo tvaṃ si gihinā nāpi paññatto   
 ubhato muttako ajja nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ   aptha          
 siyā nu kho tava   etaṃ  ko pajāni hi te idaṃ    
 saddhā dhuraṃ   pāhisi   me kosajjabahulāya ca   aptha          
 jigucchissanti taṃ viññū asucim āgāriko  yathā  
 ākaḍḍhitvāna isayo  codayissanti taṃ sadā   aptha          
 taṃ viññū pavadissanti samatikkanta sāsanaṃ    
 saṃvāsaṃ alabhanto hi kathaṃ jīvihisī   tuvaṃ   aptha

 tidhappabhinnaṃ  mātaṅgaṃ kuñjaraṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃ  
 balināgo upāgantvā yūthā  niha rate gajaṃ   aptha          
 yūthā vinissaṭo santo sukhaṃ  sātaṃ  na vindati  
 dukkhito vimano  hoti ojjhāyanto  padhāvati    aptha          
 tath  eva jaṭilā tam pi nīharissanti dummatī

 siṅgīnikkhasuvaṇṇābho   khadiraṅgārasannibho  
 maṇi yathā jotiraso ākāse caṅkamī tadā   aptha

     subhūti    
 visuddhakelāsaṇṇibho puṇṇamāse va candimā  
 majjhantiko  va suriyo ākāse caṅkamī tadā   aptha          
 disvā nabhe caṅkamantaṃ evaṃ cintes  ahan tadā   
 devo nu kho ayaṃ satto udāhu manujo ayaṃ   aptha          
 na me suto vā diṭṭho vā mahiyā ediso naro  
 api mantapadaṃ atthi  ayaṃ satthā bhavissati   aptha          
 evāhaṃ cintayitvāna sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 nānāpupphañ ca gandhañ ca sannipātetv  ahaṃ tadā   aptha          
 pupphāsanaṃ paññāpetvā sādhucittaṃ manoramaṃ  
 narasārathīnaṃ  aggaṃ idaṃ vacanam abraviṃ    aptha          
  idam me āsanaṃ vīra paññattaṃ tav  anucchavaṃ   
 hāsayanto mamaṃ  cittaṃ nisīda kusumāsane    aptha          
 nisīdi tattha bhagavā asambhīto va kesarī  
 sattarattindivaṃ buddho pavare kusumāsane   aptha          
 namassamāno aṭṭhāsiṃ  sattarattindivaṃ ahaṃ  
 vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā satthā loke anuttaro  aptha          
 mama kammaṃ pakittento idaṃ  vacanaṃ abravi   
  bhāvehi buddhānussatiṃ  bhāvanānaṃ anuttaraṃ  aptha          
 imaṃ satiṃ bhāvayitvā pūrayissasi mānasaṃ  
 tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissasi   aptha          
 asītikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissasi  
 sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavattī  rājāraṭṭhe bhavissa si   aptha          
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyam   
 anubhossasi taṃ sabbaṃ buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ   aptha          
 bhavābhave saṃsaranto mahābhogaṃ labhissasi  
 bhoge te ūnatā n  atthi buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ   aptha          
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha          
 asītikotiṃ chaḍḍetvā dāse   kammakare bahū    
 gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissasi   aptha          
 ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sākyapuṅgavaṃ  
 subhūti nāma nāmena hessasi satthu sāvako   aptha

 devā tattha samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ  tadā  
 mayaṃ pi thūpaṃ karissāma lokanāthassa tādino   aptha         
 dhātu āveṇikā n  atthi sarīraṃ ekapiṇḍitaṃ    
 imamhi   buddhathūpamhi   karissāma kañcukaṃ mayaṃ   aptha         
 devā sattaratanehi aññaṃ vaḍḍhesuṃ yojanaṃ  
 thūpo dviyojanu bbi ddho timiraṃ vyapahanti so     aptha         
 nāgā tattha samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā  
 manussā c  eva devā ca buddhathūpaṃ akaṃsu te   aptha          
 mā no pamattā assumhā appamattā sadevatā    
 mayam pi thūpaṃ karissāma lokanāthassa tādino   aptha          
 indanīlaṃ mahānīlaṃ atho jotirasaṃ maṇiṃ  
 ekato sannipātetvā buddhathūpaṃ acchādayuṃ   aptha          
 sabbaṃ maṇimayaṃ āsi tāvatā buddhacetiyaṃ  
 tīṇi yojanam ubbiddhaṃ ālokakaraṇaṃ   tadā   aptha          
  kumbhaṇḍā  ca samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā  
 manussā devā nāgā ca buddhathūpaṃ akaṃsu te   aptha          
 mā no pamattā assumhā appamattā sadevakā  
 mayam pi thūpaṃ karissāma lokanāthassa tādino   aptha          
 sabbamaṇimayaṃ thūpaṃ akar  uttarakañcukaṃ    
 yojanan te pi vaḍḍhesuṃ āyataṃ   buddhacetiyaṃ   aptha          
 catuyojanam ubbiddho buddhathūpo virocati  
 obhāseti disā sabbā sataraṃsīva   uggato   aptha
