       saparivārachattadāyaka   
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 ākāse jalavuṭṭhīva  vassati dhammavuṭṭhiyā   aptha           
 tam addasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ desentam amataṃ padaṃ  
 sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā agamāsiṃ  sakaṃ gharaṃ  aptha           
 chattam alaṅkataṃ  gayha upagacchiṃ  naruttamaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena ākāse ukkhipim ahaṃ    aptha           
 susaṅgahītayānaṃ va danto va sāvakuttamo  
 upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ matthake sampatiṭṭhahi   aptha           
 anukampako kāruṇiko buddho lokagganāyako  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha           
  yena chattam idaṃ dinnam alaṅkataṃ manoramaṃ   
 tena cittappasādena duggatiṃ so na gacchati   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 sattakkhattuñ ca devesu devarajjaṃ karissati  
 chattiṃsakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   aptha           
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha           
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo    aptha           
 buddhassa giram aññāya vācāsabhim  udīritaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano bhiyyobhāsaṃ janes  ahaṃ   aptha            
 jahitvā mānusaṃ yoniṃ devayoniṃ  samajjhagaṃ  
 vimānam uttamaṃ mayham abbhuggataṃ manoramaṃ    aptha            
 vimānā nikkhamantassa setacchattaṃ dhāriyati  tadā  
 saññaṃ paṭilabhāmi pubbakammass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 devalokā cavitvāna manussattañ ca āgacchiṃ   
 chattiṃsakkhattuñ cakkavattī sattakappasatamhi to   aptha            
 tamhā kāyā cavitvāna āgacchaṃ  tidasaṃ puraṃ  
 saṃsaritvānupubbena  mānussaṃ punar āgamaṃ    aptha            
 okkantam mātukucchiṃ maṃ setacchattam adhārayuṃ  
 jātiyā sattavassā haṃ   pabbajim   anagāriyaṃ   aptha            
 sunando nāma nāmena brāhmaṇo mantapāragū  
 phalitaṃ   chattam ādāya sāvakaggassa so   adā   aptha            
 anumodi mahāvīro sāriputto mahākathī  
 sutvānumodanaṃ tassa pubbakammam anussariṃ   aptha            
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ    
 saritvā pūrimaṃ kammam arahattam apāpuṇiṃ   aptha            
 uṭṭhāya āsanā tamhā sīre katvāna añjaliṃ  
 sambuddham abhivādetvā imaṃ vācam udīrayiṃ   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe buddho loke anuttaro  
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho   aptha            
 tassa chattaṃ mayā dinnaṃ vicittaṃ samalaṅkataṃ  
 ubho hatthehi paggaṇhi sayambhū aggapuggalo   aptha

       phussitakammiya   
 vipassī nāma sambuddho lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 khīṇāsavehi sahito saṅghārāme vasī  tadā   aptha           
 ārāmadvārā nikkhamma vipassī lokanāyako  
 sahasatasahassehi aṭṭha khīṇāsavehi tu    aptha           
 ajinena  nivattho  haṃ vāka ciradharo pi ca  
 kusumbhodakam  ādāya sambuddham upasaṅkamiṃ   aptha           
 sakaṃ  cittaṃ pasādetvā vedajāto  katañjali  
 kusumbhodakam ādāya buddham abbhukkirim ahaṃ  aptha           
 tena kammena sambuddho jalajuttamanāmako  
 mama kammaṃ pakittetvā   agamā ye na patthitaṃ   aptha           
 phussitā pañcasahassā yehi pūjes  ahaṃ jinaṃ  
 aḍḍhateyyasahassehi devarajjam akārayiṃ   aptha           
 aḍḍhateyyasahassehi cakkavattī ahos  ahaṃ  
 avasesena kammena arahattam apāpuṇiṃ    aptha           
 devarājā yadā  homi   manujādhipati   yathā    
 tam yeva nāmadheyyam me phussito   nāma hom   ahaṃ   aptha           
 devabhūtassa santassa athāpi mānusassa vā  
 samantāvyāmato   mayhaṃ phussitaṃ va pavassati    aptha           
 bhavā ugghāṭitā mayhaṃ kilesā jhāpitā mama  
 sabbāsave   parikkhīṇo phussitassa idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 candanass  eva me vasso   tathā gandho pavāyati  
 sārīriko mamaṃ   gandho aḍḍhakose   pavāyati   aptha            
 dibbagandhaṃ   sampavantaṃ   puññakammasamaṅginaṃ    
 gandhaṃ ghatvāna jānanti   phussito āgato idha   aptha

 sākhā phalā  sakaṭṭhāni tiṇāni pi va sabbaso

       pabhaṅkara   
 padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  
 pavane cetiyam āsi vāḷamigasamākule   aptha           
 na koci visahī gantuṃ cetiyam abhivandituṃ  
 tiṇakaṭṭhalatonaddhaṃ paluggam āsi  cetiyaṃ   aptha           
 vanakammiko tadā āsiṃ pitupetāmahen  ahaṃ  
 addasaṃ pavane thūpaṃ luggaṃ tiṇalatākulaṃ   aptha           
 disvān  ahaṃ buddhathūpaṃ garucittam upaṭṭhahiṃ   
 buddhaseṭṭhassa thūpo yaṃ paluggo acchatī  vane   aptha           
 nacchannaṃ nappatirūpaṃ jānantassa guṇāguṇaṃ  
 buddhathūpam asodhetvā aññakammaṃ payojaye   aptha           
 tiṇakaṭṭhañ ca vallin ca   sodhayitvāna cetiye  
 vanditvā  aṭṭha  vā rāni paṭikuṭiko  agacch  ahaṃ    aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ  sovaṇṇaṃ sappabhassaraṃ  
 saṭṭhiyojanam ubbedhaṃ   tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ   aptha           
 tisatāni ca vārāni devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 pañcavīsatikkhattuñ ca cakkavattī ahos  ahaṃ   aptha           
 bhavābhave saṃsaranto mahābhogaṃ labhām  ahaṃ  
 bhoge me ūṇatā n  atthi sodhanāya idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

 siviyā hatthikkhandhena pavane gacchato mamaṃ

 khāṇuṃ vā kaṇṭakaṃ vāpi nāhaṃ passāmi cakkhunā

      tiṇakuṭidāyaka     
 kālo gatiṃ me sodhetuṃ khaṇo me paṭipādito  
 dukkho nirayasamphasso  apuññānaṃ hi pāṇinaṃ   aptha           
 evāhaṃ cintayitvāna kammasāmim upāgamiṃ  
 ekāhaṃ kammaṃ  yācitvā pavanaṃ pāvisim ahaṃ   aptha           
 tiṇakaṭṭhañ ca  valliñ  ca āharitvān  ahan tadā  
 tidaṇḍake ṭhapetvāna akaṃ tiṇakuṭim ahaṃ   aptha           
 saṅghassatthāya kuṭikaṃ niyyātetvāna  tam ahaṃ   
 tadahe yeva āgantvā kammasāmim upāgamiṃ   aptha           
  tena kammena sukatena tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ  
 tattha me  sukataṃ vyamhaṃ  tiṇakuṭikāya nimmitaṃ   aptha           
 sahassakaṇḍo  satageṇḍu  dhajālu haritāmayo  
 satasahassaniyyūhā vyamhe  pātubhaviṃsu me   aptha           
 yaṃ yaṃ yonūpapajjāmi devattam atha mānusaṃ  
 mama saṅkappam aññāya  pāsādo upatiṭṭhati    aptha           
 bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso na vijjati  
 tāsaṃ mamaṃ  na jānāmi tiṇakuṭikāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 sīhavyagghā ca dīpī ca acchakokataracchayo   
 sabbe maṃ parivajjenti tiṇakuṭikāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 siriṃsapā ca bhūtā  ca ahi kumbhaṇḍa ra kkhasā  
 te pi maṃ parivajjenti tiṇakuṭikāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 na pāpasupinassāhaṃ   sarāmi dassanaṃ mama  
 upaṭṭhitā sati mayhaṃ tiṇakuṭikāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 tāy  eva   tiṇakuṭikāya anubhotvāna sampadā  
 gotamassa bhagavato dhammaṃ sacchikarim ahaṃ   aptha            
 ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammam akariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tiṇakuṭikāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudam āyasmā tiṇakuṭidāyako th  i  g  a ti  
 tiṇakuṭidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

       uttareyyadāyaka   
 nagare  haṃsavatiyā āhosiṃ  brāhmaṇo tadā  
 ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū   aptha           
 purakkhato sasissehi jātimā ca susikkhito  
 toyābhisecanatthāya nagarā  nikkhamiṃ  tadā   aptha           
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  
 khīṇāsa vasa hassehi nagaraṃ pāvisi jino   aptha           
 sucārurūpaṃ  disvāna anejaṃ kāritaṃ viya   
 parivutam  arahantehi disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ   aptha           
 sirasi añjaliṃ katvā namassitvāna subbataṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano uttarīyam adās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 ubho hatthehi paggayha sāṭakam ukkhipim ahaṃ  
 yāvatā buddhaparisā tāva cchādesi  sāṭakaṃ   aptha           
 piṇḍacārañ  caran tassa mahābhikkhugaṇādinaṃ   
 chadaṃ   karonto aṭṭhāsi hāsayanto   maman tadā   aptha           
 gharato nikkhamantassa sayambhū aggapuggalo  
 vīṭhiyaṃ va   ṭhito satthā akā me anumodanaṃ   aptha           
 pasannacitto sumano yo me  pādāsi sāṭa kaṃ  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha           
  tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati  
 paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati   aptha            
 devaloke vasantassa puññakammasamaṅgino  
 samantāyojanasataṃ  dussacchannaṃ  bhavissati   aptha            
 chattiṃsakkhattuṃ rājā  ca  cakkavatti bhavissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ     aptha            
 bhave saṃsāramāṇassa puññakammasamaṅgino

 koseyyakambalāni ca khomakappāsikāni ca  
 mahagghāni ca dussāni paṭilacchati   yaṃ naro   aptha

      uttareyyadāyaka     
 manasā patthitaṃ sabbaṃ paṭilacchati  yaṃ naro  
 ekadussassa vipākam anubhossati  sabbadā   aptha            
 so pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito  
 gotamassa bhagavato dhammaṃ sacchikarissati    aptha            
 aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ sabbaññussa mahesino  
 ekāhaṃ sāṭakaṃ datvā  patto mhi amataṃ  padaṃ   aptha            
 maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā vasato suññake ghare   
 dhāreti dussacchadanaṃ samantāvyāmato mamaṃ   aptha            
 aviññatti  nisevāmi cīvaraṃ paccayañ ca haṃ   
 lābhī hi annapānassa  uttareyyass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammam akariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vatthadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudam āyasmā uttareyyadāyako thero i  g  a ti  
 uttareyyadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       dhammasavaniya   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū   
 catusaccaṃ pakāsento santāreti bahuṃ janaṃ     aptha           
 ahaṃ tena samayena jaṭilo uggatāpaṇo    
 dhunanto vākacīrāni gacchāmi ambare tadā   aptha           
 buddhaseṭṭhassa upari gantuṃ na visahām  ahaṃ  
 pakkhī va selam āsajja gamanaṃ na labhe   tadā   aptha           
 na me idaṃ bhūtapubbam iriyassa vikopanaṃ    
 dake yathā ummisitvā   evaṃ gacchāmi ambare   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 ulārabhūto  manujo heṭṭhāsīno  bhavissati  
 handa me naṃ  gavesissam  api atthaṃ labheyy  ahaṃ   aptha           
 orohanto antalikkhā saddam assosi satthuno  
 aniccataṃ kathentassa tam aham uggahiṃ tadā   aptha           
 aniccasaññam uggayha agamāsiṃ mam  assamaṃ  
 yāvatā yu vasitvā na tattha kālakato ahaṃ   aptha           
 carime vattamānamhi taṃ dhammasavanaṃ sariṃ   
 tena kammena sukatena tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ  
 ekapaññāsakkhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ   aptha           
  ekasattatikkhattuñ ca  cakkavattī ahos ahaṃ  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ    aptha            
  pi tu ghare nisīditvā samaṇo bhāvitindriyo  
 kathāya  paridīpento aniccavatthudāhari   aptha            
 anussarāmi  taṃ saññaṃ saṃsaranto bhavābhave  
 na koṭipaṭivijjhāmi  ni bbānam accutaṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 aniccā vata saṅkhārā uppādāvayadhammino    
 uppajjitvā nirujjhanti tesaṃ vupasamo sukho   aptha            
 saha gāthaṃ   suṇitvāna pubbasaññam anussariṃ  
 ekāsane nisīditvā arahattam apāpuṇiṃ   aptha            
 jātiyā  sattavasso ham arahattam apāpuṇiṃ  
 upasampādayi   buddho guṇam aññāya cakkhumā   aptha            
 dārako va   ahaṃ santo karaṇīyaṃ samāpayiṃ    
 kim me karaṇiyam ajja sakyaputtassa sāsane   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammam akariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saddhammasavane phalaṃ   aptha

      ukkhittapadumiya     
  
       ukkhittapadumiya   
 nagare haṃsavatiyā āhosiṃ  māliko tadā  
 ogahetvā padumasaraṃ  satapatte  ocinām  ahaṃ   aptha           
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  
 sahasatasahassehi santacittehi tādihi  aptha           
 khīṇāsavehi suddhehi chaḷābhiññāhi so saha   
 mama vuddhiṃ  samannesaṃ  āgacchi  purisuttamo   aptha           
 disvān  ahaṃ  devadevan sayambhuṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 vaṇṭe  chetvā   satapattam ukkhipim   ambare tadā   aptha           
  yadi buddho tuvaṃ vīra lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 sayaṃ   gantvā   satapattā matthake dhārayantu te    aptha           
 adhiṭṭhahi mahāvīro lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 buddhassa ānubhāvena matthake dhārayiṃsu te   aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā   mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ   satapattan   ti vuccati  
 saṭṭhiyojanamubbiddhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ   aptha           
 sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 pañcasattatikkhattuñ ca cakkavattī ahos  ahaṃ  aptha           
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ    
 anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe sukatam attano  aptha            
 ten  eva ekapadumena anubhotvāna   sampadā  
 gotamassa bhagavato dhammaṃ sacchikarim ahaṃ   aptha            
 kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ puppham abhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ekapadumass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       ekapadumiya   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  
 bhavābhave vibhāvento tāreti janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 haṃsarājā tadā homi dijānaṃ pavaro ahaṃ  
 jātassaraṃ samoggayha kīḷāmi haṃsakīḷitaṃ   aptha           
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 jātassarassa upari āgacchi  tāvade jino   aptha           
 disvān  ahaṃ devadevaṃ sayambhuṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 vaṇṭe chetvāna padumaṃ satapattaṃ manoramaṃ   aptha           
 mukhatuṇḍena paggayha pasanno lokanāyake    
 ukkhipitvāna gagane   buddhasettham apūjayiṃ   aptha           
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 antalikkhe ṭhito satthā akā me anumodanaṃ   aptha           
  iminā ekapadumena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ vinipātaṃ na gacchasi     aptha           
 idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho jalajuttamanāmako    
 mama kammaṃ pakittetvā agamā yena patthitaṃ   aptha

       tiṇamuṭṭhidāyaka   
 himavantass  avidūre lambako nāma pabbato  
 upatisso nāma sambuddho abbhokāsamhi caṅkami   aptha           
 migaluddo pure āsim  araññe kānane ahaṃ

 datvāna devadevassa bhiyyo cittaṃ pasādayiṃ

       ekañjaliya   
 romaso  nāma sambuddho nadīkūle  vasī  tadā  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ vītaraṃsīva  bhāṇumaṃ   aptha           
 ukkāmukhaṃ pahaṭaṃ  va khadiraṅgārasannibhaṃ  
 osadhī viya rocantam ekañja lim  akās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 catunavute ito kappe yam añjalim akās  ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi añjaliyā idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe        aptha           
 itthaṃ sudam āyasmā ekañjaliyo thero i  g  a ti  
 ekañjaliyattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
 uddānaṃ  
 padum  uppalahatthā ti  dhajo kiṅkhaṇiko   nalo 
 campako paduma muṭṭhī tinduk  ekañjalī tathā 
 cha ca saṭṭhi ca gāthāyo gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi    
 ekapadumiyavaggo pañcatiṃso

       saddasaññaka   
 migaluddo pure  āsim araññe kānane ahaṃ  
 tatth  addasāsiṃ  sambuddhaṃ devasaṅghapurakkhataṃ  aptha           
 catusaccaṃ pakāsentam uddharantaṃ mahājanaṃ  
 assosiṃ madhuraṃ vācaṃ karavīkarudopamaṃ   aptha           
 brahmassarassa munino sikhino lokabandhuno  
 ghose cittaṃ pasādetvā patto mhi āsavakkhayaṃ   aptha

 anukampako  kāruṇiko sikhī lokagganāyako  
 mama saṅkappam aññāya nisīdi ya vasanthare   aptha           
 disvā nisinnaṃ vimalaṃ mahājhāyivināyakaṃ   
 pāmujjaṃ  janayitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ   aptha

       bodhivandaka   
 pāṭaliṃ haritaṃ  disvā pādapaṃ dharaṇīruhaṃ  
 ekaṃsam añjaliṃ katvā avandiṃ pāṭalim ahaṃ   aptha           
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna garuṃ katvāna mānasaṃ  
 antosuddhaṃ bahiṃ suddhaṃ  suvimuttam anāsavaṃ  aptha           
 vipassiṃ lokamahitaṃ karuṇāñāṇasāgaraṃ  
 sammukhā viya  sam buddham avandiṃ pāṭalim ahaṃ   aptha           
 ekanavut  ito kappe yaṃ bodhim abhivand  ahaṃ   
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       pāṭalipupphiya   
  vipassī nāma bhagavā  sayambhū aggapuggalo  
 purakkhato sasissehi bandhumaṃ pavisī  jino   aptha           
 tīṇi pāṭalipupphāni ucchaṅge ṭhapitāni me  
 sīsaṃ nahāyitukāmo  haṃ nadītittham agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 nikkhamma bandhumatiyā addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 indīvaraṃ va jalitam ādittaṃ va hutāsanaṃ  aptha           
 vyagghusabhaṃ va pavaram abhijātaṃ va kesariṃ  
 gacchantaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ   aptha           
 tasmiṃ pasanno sugate  kilesamaladhovane   
 gahetvā tīṇipupphāni buddhaseṭṭham apūjayiṃ   aptha           
 ekanavut  ito kappe yaṃ puppham abhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe        aptha           
 itthaṃ sudam āyasmā pāṭalipupphiyo th  i  g  a ti  
 pāṭalipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

      tīṇuppalamāliya     
  
       tīṇuppalamāliya   
 candabhāgānadītīre ahosiṃ vānaro tadā  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare   aptha           
 obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā sāla  rājaṃ  va phullitaṃ   
 lakkhaṇavyañjanūpetaṃ disvā attamano ahaṃ   aptha           
 udaggacitto sumano pītiyā haṭṭhamāṇaso  
 tīṇi uppaḷapupphāni matthake abhiropayiṃ   aptha           
 pūjayitvāna pupphāni phussassātha  mahesino  
 sagāravo bhavitvāna pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho   aptha           
 gacchanto paṭikuṭiko vippasannena cetasā  
 selantare patitvāna pāpuṇiṃ jīvitakkhayaṃ   aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā purimaṃ jātiṃ tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 satānaṃ tīṇikhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 satānaṃ pañcakhattuñ ca cakkavatti  ahos  ahaṃ   aptha

       pattipupphiyo

 pasannacitto sumano pattipuppham  apūjayiṃ   aptha           
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ puppham abhipūjayiṃ

 nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo   aptha

       soṇakoṭivīsa   
 vipassino pāvacane ekaṃ leṇaṃ mayā kataṃ  
 cātuddisassa saṅghassa bandhumā rājadhāniyā    aptha           
 dussehi bhūmileṇassa  santharitvā  pariccajiṃ  
 udaggacitto sumano akāsiṃ paṇidhiṃ tadā   aptha           
  ārādhayeyyaṃ sambuddhaṃ pabbajjañ ca labheyy  ahaṃ  
 anuttarañ ca nibbānaṃ phuseyyaṃ santim uttamaṃ    aptha           
 ten  eva sukkamūlena kappaṃ navuti saṃsariṃ  
 devabhūto manusso va  katapuñño viroc  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tato kammāvasesena idha pacchimake bhave  
 campāyam aggaseṭṭhissa jāto mhi ekaputtako   aptha           
 jāta mat tassa  me sutvā pitucchando  ayam ahu  
 dadām  ahaṃ  kumārassa vīsakoṭianūnakā   aptha           
 caturaṅgulā ca me lomā jātā pādatale ubho  
 sukhumā mudusamphassā tulāpi ca mahāsubhā   aptha           
 atītā navutī kappā   ay am eko va uttariṃ   
 nābhijānāmi nikkhitte pāde bhume   asanthate   aptha           
 ārādhito me sambuddho pabbajim anagāriyaṃ  
 arahattañ ca me pattaṃ sītibhūto mhi nibbuto     aptha           
 aggo āraddhaviriyānaṃ   niddiṭṭho  sabbadassinā   
 khīṇāsavo ca arahā chaḷabhiññāmahiddhiko     aptha            
 ekanavut  ito kappe yaṃ dānam adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi leṇadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe        aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe        aptha            
 koṭivīso ti so soṇo bhikkhu  saṅghassa aggato  
 pañhaṃ   puṭṭho viyākāsi anotatte mahāsare ti  
 itthaṃ sudam āyasmā soṇo koṭivīso thero i  g  a ti  
 soṇakoṭivīsattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

      pubbakammapiloti     
  
       pubbakammapiloti   
 anota ttasarāsanne ramaṇīye silā tale  
 nānāratanapajjote nānāgandhavanantare  aptha           
 mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena pareto lokanāyako  
 āsīno vyākari tattha pubbakammāni attano   aptha           
  suṇotha  bhikkhavo mayham yaṃ kammaṃ pakatam mayā  
  pilotiyassa  kammassa buddhatthe   pi vipaccati   aptha           
 munāli  nām  ahaṃ dhutto  pubbe aññāsu jātisu  
 paccekabuddhaṃ surabhim abbhācikkhim  adūsakaṃ   aptha           
 tena kammavipākena niraye saṃsariṃ ciraṃ  
 bahū vassasahassāni dukkhaṃ vedesiṃ vedanaṃ   aptha           
 tena kammāvasesena idha pa cchimake bhave  
 abbhakkhā naṃ mayā laddhaṃ sundarīkāya kāraṇā   aptha           
 sabbābhibhussa buddhassa nando nām  āsi sāvako  
 tam  abbhakkhāya  niraye ciraṃ saṃsaritam mayā   aptha           
 dasavassasahassāni niraye saṃsariṃ ciraṃ  
 manussabhāvaṃ laddhāham  abbhakkhānaṃ bahuṃ labhiṃ   aptha           
 tena kammā vasesena ciñca  mānavikā mamaṃ  
 abbhakkhāsi   abhūtena janakāyassa aggato   aptha           
 brāhmaṇo sutavā āsim ahaṃ sakkatapūjito  
 mahāvane pañcasate  mante  vācemi māṇave   aptha            
 tatthāgato isigaṇo   pañcābhiññāmahi ddhiko     
 tañ cāham   ā gataṃ disvā abbhācikkhim adūsakaṃ   aptha            
 tato ham avacaṃ sisse  kāmabhogī   ayaṃ isi  
 mayhaṃ vibhāsamānassa anumodiṃsu māṇavā   aptha            
 tato māṇavakā sabbe bhikkhamānā kulākule    
 mahājanassa ahaṃsu   kāma bhogī   ayaṃ isi   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 tena kammavipākena pañcabhikkhusatā ime  
 abbhakkhānaṃ labhuṃ sabbe sundarīkāya kāraṇā   aptha            
 dvemātā  bhātaro pubbe  dhanahetu haniṃ ahaṃ   
 pakkhipiṃ giriduggesu silāya  ca apiṃsayiṃ   aptha            
 tena kammavipākena devadatto silaṃ khipi  
 aṅguṭṭhaṃ piṃsayī  pāde mama pāsānasakkharā   aptha            
 pure haṃ dārako hutvā kīḷamāno mahāpathe  
 paccekabuddhaṃ disvāna magge sakalikaṃ dahiṃ    aptha            
 tena kammavipākena idha pacchimake bhave  
 vadhatthaṃ maṃ devadatto abhimāre  payojayi   aptha            
 hatthāroho pure āsiṃ paccekamunim uttamaṃ  
 piṇḍāya vicarantaṃ  tam  āsādesiṃ  gajen  ahaṃ   aptha            
 tena kammavipākena bhanto  nāḷāgirī   gajo  
 giribbaje puravare   dāruṇo mam upāgamī     aptha            
 rājāhaṃ patthivo   āsiṃ sattiyā purisaṃ haniṃ  
 tena kammavipākena niraye paccasiṃ   bhusaṃ   aptha            
 kammuṇo   tassa sesena cādiṇṇaṃ   sakalaṃ mama  
 pāde chaviṃ pakopesi   na hi kammaṃ panassati     aptha            
 ahaṃ kevaṭṭagāmasmim   ahuṃ kevaṭṭadārako  
 macchake ghātite disvā janayiṃ somanassakaṃ   aptha            
 tena kammavipākena sīsadukkham ahu mama  
 sakkesu haññamānesu yadā hani viḍuḍabho     aptha            
 phussassāhaṃ   pāvacane sāvake paribhāsayiṃ    
 yavaṃ khādatha bhuñjatha mā ca bhuñjatha sāliyo   aptha

      pubbakammapiloti

 sītaṃ uṇhaṃ na jānāmi rajojallaṃ na lippati

 yaṃ so desesi saddhammaṃ khemaṃ nibbānapattiyā  
 tam ev  atthaṃ nisāmetha saddhammasavanaṃ sukhaṃ    aptha            
 upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ sammodiṃ  muninā ahaṃ  
 taṃ kathaṃ vītisāretvā lakkhaṇe upadhārayiṃ   aptha            
 lakkhaṇe dve va  kaṅkhāmi passāmi tiṃsalakkhaṇe

 kanikāraṃ va jalitaṃ dīparukkhaṃ  va jotitaṃ  
 osadhiṃ va virocantaṃ vijjuṃ  abbhaghane  yathā  aptha           
 asambhītam anuttāsiṃ  migarājaṃ va kesariṃ

 uddharantam imaṃ lokaṃ chindantaṃ sabbasaṃsayaṃ  
 lasantaṃ  migarājaṃ va addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha

  vā kacīraṃ gahetvāna pādamūle apatthariṃ    aptha           
 kāḷānusārikaṃ gayha anulimpin   tathāgataṃ  
 sambuddham anulimpitvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha

 usabho jitasaṅgāme   sampakampesi mediniṃ   aptha

 tath  eva tava ñāṇamhi sabbā diṭṭhī pabhijjare     aptha           
 sukhumacchikajāle va saramhi sampatānite

 tath  eva titthiyā loke phuṭā saccavinissitā    
 anto ñāṇavare tuyhaṃ parivattanti mārisa   aptha            
 patiṭṭhā vuyhataṃ oghe tvam hi nātho abandhanaṃ  
 bhayāṭṭitānaṃ saraṇo muttatthīnaṃ parāyano   aptha            
 ekavīro asadiso mettākāruṇādisañcayo  
 susīlo asamo santo vasitavijitañjayo     aptha

 dhīro vigatasammoho  anejo akathaṃ kathī  
 vusito  vantadoso si nimmalo payato suci   aptha            
 saṅgh  ātīto  gatamado tevijjo tibhavantago  
 sīmātigo dhammagarū katattho  hitadhammato    aptha            
 tārako tvaṃ yāthā nāvā  nidhi v  assāsakārako   
 asambhīto yathā sīho gajarājā  va dammito   aptha            
 thometvā dasagāthāhi padumuttaraṃ mahāyasaṃ  
 vanditvā satthuno pāde tuṇhī aṭṭhās  ahaṃ tadā   aptha            
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
 yo me sīlañ ca ñāṇañ ca dhamman cāpi pakittayi   
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 saṭṭhiṃ kappasahassāni   devaloke ramissati  
 aññe deve adhibhotvā   isseraṃ   kārayissati   aptha            
 so pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito  
 gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissati   aptha

 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo   aptha            
 yathāpi megho thanayaṃ   tappeti medinim imaṃ  
 tath  eva tvaṃ mahāvīra thanena   tappayī   mamaṃ   aptha            
 sīlaṃ paññaṃ ca dhamman ca thavitvā lokanāyakaṃ  
 patto mhi paramaṃ santiṃ nibbānaṃ padaṃ accutaṃ   aptha            
 api nūn  esa   bhagavā ciraṃ tiṭṭheyya cakkhumā  
 aññātañ ca vijāneyyaṃ   phasseyyam   amataṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 ayaṃ me pacchimā jāti bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ buddham abhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       madhudāyaka   
  sindhuyā nadiyā tīre sukato assamo mama  
 tassa vācem  ahaṃ  sisse itihāsaṃ salakkhaṇaṃ   aptha           
 dhammakāmā vinītā te sotukāmā pi sāsanaṃ   
 chalaṅge pāramiṃ pattā sindhukūle vasanti te   aptha           
 uppādāgamane c  eva lakkhaṇesu ca kovidā  
 uttamatthaṃ gavesantā vasanti pavane tadā    aptha           
 sumedho nāma sambuddho loke uppajji tāvade  
 amhākam anukampanto upagacchi vināyako   aptha           
 upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 tiṇasantharakaṃ  katvā lokajeṭṭhass  adās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 pavanāto madhuṃ gayha buddhaseṭṭhass  adās  ahaṃ  
 sambuddho paribh uñjitvā idaṃ vacanam abravi    aptha           
 yan taṃ adāsi madhuṃ me pasanno sehi pānihi  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha           
 iminā madhudānena tiṇasanthārakena ca  
 tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati   aptha           
 tiṃsakappasahassāni  okkākakula sambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā  loke bhavissati   aptha           
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissati nāsavo   aptha            
 devalokā idhāgantvā mātukucchim upāgato  
 madhuvasso pavassittha chādayaṃ  madhunā mahiṃ   aptha            
 mama nikkhantamattamhi  kumbhiyā vasuduttarā   
 tatrāpi madhuvasso me vassate niccakālikaṃ   aptha

 agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajjim anagāriyaṃ

 ten  eva madhudānena patto mhi āsavakkhayaṃ   aptha            
 vuṭṭhamhi  deve caturaṅgule tiṇe

       padumakūṭāgāriya   
 piyadassī nāma bhagavā sayambhū lokanāyako  
 vivekakāmo sambuddho samādhikusalo muni   aptha           
 vanasaṇḍaṃ samoggayha piyadassī mahāmuni  
 paṃsukūlaṃ pattharitvā nisīdi purisuttamo   aptha           
 migaluddo pure āsiṃ iriṇe  kānane ahaṃ  
 pasadaṃ migam esanto  ahiṇḍāmi ahaṃ tadā   aptha           
 tatth  addasāsiṃ sambuddham oghatiṇṇam anāsavaṃ  
 pupphitaṃ sālarājaṃ va sataraṃsīva uggataṃ   aptha           
 disvān  ahaṃ devadevaṃ piyadassi mahāyasaṃ

 āharitvāna padumaṃ satapattaṃ manoramaṃ  
 kūṭāgāraṃ karitvāna chādayiṃ padumen  ahaṃ   aptha

      padumakūṭāgāriya     
 anukampako kāruṇiko piyadassī mahāmunī  
 sattarattindivaṃ buddho kūṭāgāre vasī jino   aptha           
 purāṇaṃ chaḍḍayitvāna navena cchādayim ahaṃ  
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna aṭṭhāsiṃ tāvade ahaṃ   aptha           
 vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā piyadassī mahāmuni  
 disā anuvilokento nisīdi lokanāyako   aptha           
 tadā sudassano nāma upaṭṭhāko mahiddhiko  
 cittam aññāya buddhassa piyadassissa satthuno  aptha            
 asītiyā sahassehi bhikkhūhi parivārito  
 vanante sukham āsīnam upesi lokanāyakaṃ   aptha            
 yāvatā vanasaṇḍamhi  adhivatthā ca devatā  
 buddhassa cittam aññāya sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā   aptha            
 samāgatesu yakkhesu kumbhaṇḍe saha rakkhase  
 bhikkhusaṅghe ca sampatte gāthā m  avyāharī jino   aptha            
 yo maṃ sattāhaṃ pūjesi āvāsañ ca akāsi me  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 sududdasaṃ sunipuṇaṃ gambhīraṃ suppakāsitaṃ  
 ñāṇena kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 catuddasāni kappāni devarajjaṃ karissati  
 kūṭāgāraṃ brahan tassa padumapupphehi chāditaṃ  
 ākāse dhārayissanti pubbakammass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 catubbise kappasate vokiṇṇaṃ  saṃsarissati  
 tattha pupphamayaṃ vyamham  ākāse dhārayissati   aptha            
 yathā padumapattamhi toyaṃ na upalippati   
 tath  ev  imassa ñāṇamhi kilesā nopalippare   
 manasā vinivaṭṭetvā pañcanīvaraṇe ayaṃ  aptha            
 cittaṃ janetvā  nikkhamma agārā pabbajissati  
 tato pupphamayaṃ vyamhaṃ  dhārentaṃ nikkhamissati   aptha            
 rukkhamūle vasantassa nipakassa satīmato   
 tattha pupphamayaṃ vyamhaṃ matthake dhārayissati   aptha            
 cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ  
 daditvā bhikkhusaṅghassa nibbāyissat  anāsavo   aptha            
 kūṭāgārena caraṇā  pabbajjaṃ abhinikkhamiṃ    
 rukkhamūle vasantamhi   kūṭāgāraṃ dhariyyati     aptha

      bakkula     
 kosumbhā salaḷā nīpā nigrodhā ca kapitthanā   
 ediso assamo mayhaṃ sasisso haṃ tadā vasiṃ   aptha           
 anomadassī bhagavā sayambhū lokanāyako  
 gavesaṃ paṭisallāṇaṃ mam assamam  upāgami   aptha           
 upetañ ca mahāvīram anomadassi mahāyasaṃ  
 khaṇena  lokanāthassa vātābādho samuṭṭhahi  aptha           
 vicaranto araññamhi addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ cakkhumantam mahāyasaṃ  aptha           
 iriyañ cāpi disvāna upalakkhes  ahan tadā  
 asaṃsayaṃ hi buddhassa vyādhino udapajjatha   aptha           
 khippam assamam āgacchiṃ  mama sissāna santike  
 bhesajjaṃ kattukāmo haṃ sisse āmantayiṃ  tadā   aptha            
 paṭissutvāna me vākyaṃ sissā sabbe sagāravā  
 ekajjhaṃ sannipātiṃsu  satthu gāravatā mama   aptha            
 khippaṃ pabbatam āruyha sabbosadham akās ahaṃ  
 pānīyayogaṃ katvāna buddhaseṭṭhass  adās  ahaṃ   aptha            
 paribhutto mahāvīro sabbaññū lokanāyako   
 khippaṃ vāto vūpasami sugatassa mahesino   aptha            
 passaddhadarathaṃ  disvā anomadassī mahāyaso  
 sakāsane nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
 yo me pādāsi bhesajjaṃ vyādhiñ ca samayī mayī    
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 kappasatasahassāni devaloke ramissati  
 vādite turiye tattha modissati sadā ayaṃ   aptha            
 manussalokam āgantvā sukkamūlena codito  
 sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   aptha            
 pañcapaññāsakappamhi anoma   nāma khattiyo  
 cāturanto vijitāvī jambusaṇḍassa issaro   aptha            
 sattaratanasampanno cakkavattī mahabbalo  
 tāvatiṃse to   khobhetvā   isseraṃ   kārayissati   aptha

 sokasallapareto haṃ vanantam upasaṅkamiṃ

     therāpadāna 
 saṭṭhiṃ turiyasahassāni  sāyapāto  pavajjare   
 soḷasitthisahassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā   aptha           
 abhinikkhamma bhavanā sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano vandissan  taṃ mahāyasaṃ   aptha           
 sambuddham abhivādetvā sasissaṃ taṃ nimantayiṃ   
 adhivasesi so vīro  sumedho lokanāyako   aptha           
 mamaṃ dhammakathaṃ katvā uyyojesi mahāmuni   
 sambuddham abhivādetvā bhavanam me upāgamiṃ   aptha            
 āmantayiṃ  parijanaṃ sabbe sannipatātha vo   
 pubbaṇhasamayaṃ buddho bhavanam āgamissati   aptha            
 lābhā amhaṃ   suladdhaṃ no   y  esāma   tava sa ntike   
 mayam pi buddhaseṭṭhassa pūjaṃ karissāma satthuno   aptha            
 annaṃ pānaṃ paṭṭhapetvā kālam arocayim ahaṃ  
 vasīsatasahassehi upesi lokanāyako   aptha            
 sataṅgikehi   turiyehi paccuggaman akās  ahaṃ  
 sabbasovaṇṇaye pīṭhe nisīdi purisuttamo   aptha            
 uparicchannam akāsiṃ   sabbasovaṇṇayaṃ tadā  
 vījanīyā   pavāyanti bhikkhusaṅghassa antare   aptha            
 bahuken  annapānena   bhikkhusaṅgham atappayiṃ   
 paccekadussayugale bhikkhusaṅghass adās  ahaṃ   aptha            
 yaṃ vadanti samedho ti lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃ  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā  imā gāthā abhāsatha    aptha            
 yo me annañ ca pānañ ca saṅgham   etena tappayi  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissati  
 sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   aptha            
 upapajjati yaṃ yo niṃ devattam atha mānusaṃ  
 sabbadā  sabbasovaṇṇaṃ chadanaṃ dhārayissati   aptha            
 tiṃsakappasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena   satthā loke bhavissati   aptha

       ajita   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  
 ajjhogāhetvā himavantaṃ nisīdi lokanāyako   aptha           
 nāham addakkhiṃ sambuddhaṃ na pi saddaṃ suṇom  ahaṃ  
 mamaṃ bhikkhaṃ gavesanto āhiṇḍāmi  vane ahaṃ   aptha           
 tatth  addasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ  
 disvāna cittam āpajjiṃ   satto  ko nām  ayaṃ bhave   aptha           
 lakkhaṇāni viloketvā mama vijjam anussariṃ  
 sutaṃ hi me taṃ buddhānaṃ paṇḍitānaṃ subhāsitaṃ   aptha           
 tesaṃ tathā taṃ  vacanam  ayaṃ buddho bhavissati  
 yannunāhaṃ sakkareyyaṃ gatiṃ  me sodhayissati   aptha           
 khippam assamam āgantvā dumatelaṃ gahim ahaṃ  
 kolambakaṃ gahetvāna upagacchiṃ  vināyakaṃ   aptha           
 tidaṇḍake gahetvāna abbhokāse ṭhapes  ahaṃ  
 padīpaṃ pajjaletvāna   aṭṭhakkhattum avand  ahaṃ     aptha

     therāpadāna 
 sattarattindivaṃ buddho nisīdi purisuttamo  
 tato ratyā vivasane  vuṭṭhāsi lokanāyako   aptha           
 pasannacitto sumano sabbarattindivam ahaṃ  
 dīpaṃ buddhassa pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pānihi   aptha           
 sabbe vanā gandhamayā  pabbate gandhamādane  
 buddhass  ānubhāvena upagacchuṃ tadā jinaṃ   aptha            
 ye keci pupphagandhā ye  pupphitā dharaṇīruhā  
 buddhass  ānubhāvena sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā   aptha            
 yāvatā himavantamhi nāgā ca garuḷā ubho  
 dhammañ va sotukāmā te  āgacchuṃ  buddhasantike   aptha            
 devalo nāma samaṇo buddhassa aggasāvako  
 vasīsatasahassehi buddhasantik  upāgami    aptha            
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
 yo me dīpaṃ padīpesi pasanno sehi pānihi  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 saṭṭhiṃ kappasahassāni  devaloke ramissati  
 sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   aptha            
 chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  
 pathaviyaṃ  sattasataṃ  vipulaṃ   rajjaṃ karissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto   asaṅkhiyaṃ     aptha            
 iminā dīpadānena dibbacakkhu bhavissati  
 samantato aḍḍhakosaṃ passissati   ayaṃ sadā   aptha            
 devalokā cavantassa nibbattantassa   jantuno  
 divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ   padīpaṃ dhārayissati  
 jāyamānassa santassa   puññakammasamaṅgiṇo   aptha            
 yāvatā nagaram āsi tāvatā jotayissati    
 upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattam atha mānusaṃ   aptha            
 ass  eva dīpadānassa aṭṭhadīpaphalena hi    
  na  jahissant  imaṃ jantuṃ   dīpadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

      ajita     
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha            
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo    aptha            
 tosayitvāna sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ  
 ajito nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   aptha            
 saṭṭhiṃ kappasahassāni  devaloke ramim ahaṃ  
 tatrāpi me dīpasataṃ  jotare  niccakālikaṃ   aptha            
 devaloke manusse vā niddhāvanti pabhā mama  
 buddhasetthaṃ saritvāna bhiyyo bhāsaṃ  janes  ahaṃ   aptha            
 tusitāhaṃ cavitvāna okkamiṃ mātukucchiyā  
 jāyamānassa santassa  āloko vipulo ahu   aptha            
 agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajim anagāriyaṃ  
 bāvarim  upasaṅkamma sissattham ajjhupāgamiṃ   aptha            
 himavante vasanto haṃ assosiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 uttamatthaṃ gavesanto upagacchiṃ  vināyakaṃ   aptha            
 danto buddho ca medhāvī  oghatiṇṇo nirūpadhī

 tam me āgamanaṃ siddhaṃ tosito haṃ mahāmuniṃ    
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ dīpam adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dīpadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       tissametteyya   
 pabbhārakuṭaṃ  nissāya sobhito nāma tāpaso  
 pavattaphalaṃ bhuñjitvā vasati pabbatantare   aptha           
 aggidārum āharitvā ujjālesim ahaṃ tadā  
 uttamatthaṃ gavesanto brahmalokupattiyā   aptha           
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mam uddharitukāmo so āgacchi  mama santike   aptha           
 kiṃ karohi mahāpuññaṃ dehi me aggidārukaṃ  
 aham aggiṃ paricare tato me suddhi hehiti    aptha           
 subhaddako tvaṃ manuja deva te tvaṃ pajānasi  
 tuvam aggim paricara handa te aggidārukaṃ   aptha           
 tato kaṭṭhaṃ gahetvāna aggim ujjālayī jino  
 na tattha kaṭṭhaṃ pajjhāyi  pāṭihīraṃ mahesino   aptha           
 na te  aggi pajjalati āhutī te na vijjati  
 niratthakaṃ vataṃ tuyham aggiṃ paricarassu me   aptha           
 kīdiso  so mahāvīra aggi tava pavuccati  
 mayham pi kathayass  etam ubho paricarāmase   aptha           
 hetudhammanirodhāya kilesājhāpanāya ca  
 issāmacchariyaṃ hitvā  tayo ete mam  āhutī   aptha           
 kīdiso tvaṃ mahāvīra  katham gotto si mārisa  
 ācārapaṭipatti te bāḷham kho mama ruccati   aptha

 khattiyamhi kūle jāto abhiññāpāramiṅgato  
 sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo n  atthi dāni punabbhavo   aptha            
 yadi buddho si sabbaññū  pabhaṅkara tamonuda  
 namassissāmi taṃ deva dukkhass  antakaro tuvaṃ   aptha            
 pattharitvājinañ cammaṃ  nisīdanam adās  ahaṃ  
 nisīda  tattha sabbaññū upaṭṭhissām  ahaṃ tavaṃ   aptha            
 nisīdi bhagavā tattha ajinamhi suvitthate  
 nimantayitvā sambuddhaṃ pabbatam agamās  ahaṃ   aptha            
 khāribhārañ ca pūretvā tindukaṃ phalam āhariṃ   
 madhunā yojayitvāna phalaṃ buddhass  adās  ahaṃ   aptha            
 mama nijjhāyamānassa paribhuñji tadā jino

 mam  assame nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
  yo me phalena tappesi pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 pañcavīsatikkhattuṃ so devarajjaṃ karissati  
 sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   aptha            
 tassa saṅkappam aññāya pubbakammasamaṅgino  
 annaṃ pānañ ca vatthañ ca sayanañ ca mahārahaṃ  aptha

 sadā pamudito cāyaṃ bhavissati anāmayo    aptha

 sabbattha sukhito hutvā manussattaṃ bhavissati   aptha

 yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato patto smi viññutaṃ  
 bhoge me ūnatā n  atthi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 varadhammam anuppatto rāgadose samūhaniṃ  
 sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo n  atthi dāni punabbhavo   aptha

       puṇṇaka   
 pabbhārakuṭaṃ nissāya sayambhū aparājito  
 ābādhiko va yo  buddho vasati pabbatantare   aptha           
 mama assamasāmantā panādo  āsi tāvade  
 buddhe nibbāyamānamhi āloko āsi tāvade   aptha           
 yāvatā vanasaṇḍasmiṃ acchakokataracchayo  
 vālā ca kesarī  sabbe abhigajjiṃsu  tāvade   aptha           
 uppādaṃ tam ahaṃ disvā pabbhāram agamās  ahaṃ  
 tatth  addasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ nibbutam aparājitaṃ   aptha           
 suphullaṃ  sālarājaṃ va sataraṃsīva uggataṃ  
 vītaccikaṃ  va aṅgāraṃ nibbutam aparājitaṃ   aptha           
 tīṇaṃ kaṭṭhañ ca pūretvā citakaṃ tatth  akās ahaṃ  
 citakaṃ sukataṃ katvā sarīraṃ jhāpayim ahaṃ   aptha           
 sarīraṃ jhāpayitvāna gandhatoyaṃ samokiriṃ  
 antalikkhe ṭhito yakkho nāmam aggahi tāvade   aptha           
 taṃ pūritaṃ  tayā kiccaṃ sayambhussa mahesino  
 puṇṇako nāma nāmena sadā hohi  tuvaṃ mune   aptha           
 tamhā kāyā cavitvāna devalokam agacch  ahaṃ  
 tattha divyamayo   gandho antalikkhe pavāyati     aptha           
 tatrāpi nāmadheyyaṃ   me puṇṇako ti ahū tadā   
 devabhūto manusso vā saṅkappaṃ pūrayām ahaṃ   aptha            
 idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate   bhavo  
 idhāpi puṇṇako nāma nāmaṃ mayhaṃ   paññāyati     aptha            
 tosayitvāna sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha            
 ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammam akariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tanukiccass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudam āyasmā puṇṇako thero i  g  a ti  
 puṇṇakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

     therāpadāna 
  
       mettagū   
 himavantass  avidūre asoko nāma pabbato  
 tatthāsi assamo mayhaṃ vissakammena  māpito   aptha           
 sumedho nāma sambuddho aggo kāruṇiko muni  
 nivāsayitvā pubbanhe piṇḍāya me upāgami   aptha           
 upāgataṃ mahāvīram sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 paggayha subhakaṃ  pattaṃ sappitelam apūrayiṃ   aptha           
 datvān  ahaṃ buddhaseṭṭhe sumedhe lokanāyake  
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna bhīyyo hāsaṃ  janes  ahaṃ   aptha           
 iminā sappidānena cetanāpanidhīhi ca  
 devabhūto manusso vā labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ   aptha           
 vinipātaṃ vivajjetvā  saṃsarāmi  bhavābhave  
 tattha cittaṃ paṇidhitvā  labhāmi acalaṃ padaṃ   aptha           
 lābhā tuyhaṃ suladdhan te yaṃ mam addakkhi brāhmaṇo  
 mama dassanam āgamma arahā tvaṃ bhavissasi    aptha           
 vissaṭṭho hohi   mā bhāyi adhigantvā  mahāyasaṃ  
 mamaṃ hi sappiṃ datvāna parimokkhasi jātiyā   aptha           
 iminā sappidānena  mettacittavatāya  ca  
 aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissasi     aptha           
 aṭṭhārase ca kkhattuṃ tvaṃ   devarājā bhavissasi    
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha

 saṭṭhikoṭī hiraññassa datvāna   pabbajiṃ ahaṃ  
 kiṃ kusalaṃ gavesanto bāvarim   upasaṅkamiṃ   aptha

      mettagū     
 tattha mante adhīyāmi  chalaṅgaṃ nāma lakkhaṇaṃ  
 tam andhakāraṃ vidhamam uppajji  tvaṃ mahāmuni   aptha            
 tava dassanakāmo haṃ āgato mhi mahāmune   
 tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna patto mhi acalaṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 tiṃsakappasahassamhi sappiṃ buddhassadās  ahaṃ  
 etthantare nābhijāne sappiṃ viññāpitaṃ mayā   aptha            
 mama saṅkappam aññāya uppajjati yadicchakaṃ  
 cittam aññāya nibbattaṃ sabbe santappayām  ahaṃ   aptha            
 aho buddhā aho dhammā aho no satthu sampadā  
 thokaṃ hi sappiṃ datvāna appameyyaṃ labhām  ahaṃ   aptha            
 mahāsamudde udakaṃ yāvatā nerupassato  
 mama sappim upādāya kalabhāgaṃ na hessati   aptha            
 yāvatā cakkavālassa kayiraṃtassa  rāsito   
 mayā nivatthavatthānam  okāso so na sammati   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 tidasehi yathā indo manujehi  purakkhato  
 nisīdi tattha bhagavā asambhīto va kesarī   aptha           
 nagare haṃsavatiyā vasāmi brāhmaṇo ahaṃ  
 chalaṅgo nāma nāmena evaṃ nāma ahaṃ muni    aptha           
 aṭṭhārasaṃ sissasatā  parivārenti maṃ tadā  
 tehi sissehi samito gaṅgātīram upāgamiṃ   aptha           
 tatth  addasāsiṃ samaṇe nikkuhe  dhotapāpake   
 bhāgīrasim taranto haṃ evaṃ cintesiṃ tāvade   aptha           
 sāyapātaṃ tarantā me buddhaputtā mahāyasā  
 viheṭhayanti  attānaṃ tesaṃ attā vihaññati   aptha           
 sadevakassa lokassa buddho aggaṃ pavuccati  
 n  atthi me dakkhiṇe kāraṃ  gatimaggavisodhanaṃ   aptha           
 yannūna buddhaseṭṭhassa setuṃ gaṅgāya kāraye   
 kārāpetvā imaṃ kammaṃ saṃsarāmi imaṃ bhavaṃ   aptha           
 satasahassaṃ datvāna setuṃ kārāpayim ahaṃ  
 saddahanto kataṃ kāraṃ vipulam me bhavissati   aptha            
 kārāpetvāna haṃ setum upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 sirasi añjaliṃ katvā imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   aptha            
 satasahassassa v  ayam  katvā   kārāpito mayā  
 tavatthāya mahāsetuṃ paṭigaṇha mahāmune   aptha            
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
  yo me setum akāresi pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 dālito pabbatato   vā rukkhato patito pi yaṃ  
 cuto pi lacchati ṭṭhānaṃ setudānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 virūḷhamūlasantānaṃ nigrodham iva māluto  
 amittā na sahissanti   setudānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 nāssa corā sahissanti   nātimaññati khattiyo    
 sabbe atikkamm   āmitte setudānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

 tassa saṅkappam aññāya nibbattissati tāvade   aptha

 mandālakehi sañchannā  nānāgandhasameritā   
 gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā aññe pupphanti kesarī   aptha            
 opupphapattā tiṭṭhanti padumā kaṇṇikā bahū  
 madhu bhisamhā  savati  khīraṃ sappi  muḷālibhi    aptha            
 samantā tena gandhena nānāgandhasameritā  
 kumudā ambagandhī ca nayitā  dissare bahū   aptha            
 jātassarassānukūlā  ketakā pupphitā bahū  
 suphullā bandhujīvā ca setavārī sugandhikā   aptha

 pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā jalajā muñjarohitā

 pārevaṭā ravihaṃsā kutthakā   ca nadīcarā

 tāni gandhāni ghāyanto bhakkhayanto phalān  ahaṃ   aptha            
 gandhodakaṃ pivanto ca nivasāmi mam  assame  
 enī migā varāhā ca pasadā khuddarūpakā   aptha

 kamaṇḍaludharā sabbe ajinuttaravāsino  
 te jaṭābhārabharitā vasanti mama assame   aptha            
 yugamattañ ca pekkhantā nipakā santavuttino  
 lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā vasanti mama assame   aptha

 na te dakam  āharanti kaṭṭham vā aggidārukaṃ  
 ayam ca upasampanno  pāṭihīrass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

 phalaṃ buddhassa datvāna agalum  anulimp  ahaṃ   
 pasannacitto sumano buddhasettham a vandi haṃ  aptha            
 paḍumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ patiggaho  
 isimajjhe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
 yo me phalañ cāgaluñ ca  āsanañ ca adāsi me  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 game vā yadi vāraññe pabbhāresu guhāsu vā  
 imassa cittam aññāya nibbattissati bhojanaṃ   aptha            
 devaloke manusse vā upapanno ayaṃ naro  
 bhojanehi ca vatthehi parisaṃ tappayissati   aptha            
 upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattam atha mānusaṃ  
 akkhobhabhogo  hutvāna saṃsarissat  ayaṃ naro   aptha            
 tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati

       nanda   
 migaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ  
 pasadamigaṃ  gavesanto sayambhum addasam ahaṃ   aptha           
 anuruddho  nāma sambuddho sayambhū aparājito  
 vivekakāmo so vīro  vanamajjh  ogahiṃ tadā  aptha           
 catudaṇḍe gahetvāna catuṭṭhāne ṭhapes  ahaṃ  
 maṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā padumapupphehi chādayiṃ   aptha           
 maṇḍapaṃ chādayitvāna sayambhum  abhivādayiṃ  
 dhanuṃ tatth  eva nikkhippa  pabbajim  anagāriyaṃ   aptha           
 naciraṃ pabbajitassa vyādhi me udapajjatha   
 pubbakammaṃ saritvāna tattha kālakato  ahaṃ   aptha           
 pubbakammena saṃyutto tusitam agamās  ahaṃ  
 tattha sovaṇṇayaṃ vyamhaṃ  nibbattati yadicchakaṃ   aptha           
 sahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ   dibbaṃ yānam   adhiṭṭhito  
 ārohitvāna taṃ yānaṃ gacchām  ahaṃ yadicchakaṃ   aptha           
 tato me niyyamānassa devabhūtassa me sato  
 samantā yojanasataṃ maṇḍapo me dhariyyati     aptha           
 sayane so tuvaṭṭhāmi   accanta   pupphasanthate  
 antalikkhā ca padumā vassante niccakālikaṃ   aptha           
 marīcike   phandamāne  tappamāne  ca ātape  
 na maṃ tapati ātapo maṇḍapassa idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 duggatiṃ samatikkanto apāyā pihitā mama  
 maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā santāpo me na vijjati   aptha            
 mahīsaññam adhiṭṭhāya loṇatoyaṃ tarām   ahaṃ  
 tassa me sukataṃ kammaṃ buddhapūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 apatham pi   pathaṃ katvāna gacchāmi anilañjase    
 aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 bodhaneyyaṃ pajaṃ  disvā piyadassī mahāmuni  
 cakkavālasahassamhi gantvā ovadate muni   aptha           
 mam uddharitukāmo so mam assamam upāgami  
 na diṭṭho me jino pubbe na ssuto  pi ca kassaci   aptha           
 uppādā supinā mayhaṃ lakkhaṇā suppakāsitā  
 paṭṭho bhumm  antalikkhasmiṃ  nakkhattapadakovido   aptha           
 so haṃ buddhassa sutvāna tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 bhuñjanto vā nisinno vā sarāmi niccakālikaṃ   aptha           
 mayi evaṃ sarantamhi bhagavā pi anussari   
 buddham anussarantassa pīti me hoti tāvade   aptha            
 kālañ ca punar āgamma upesi maṃ mahāmuni  
 sampatto  pi na jānāmi ayaṃ buddho mahāmuni   aptha            
 anukampako kāruṇiko piyadassī mahāmuni  
 sañjānāpesi attānaṃ  ahaṃ buddho sadevake   aptha            
 sañjānitvāna sambuddhaṃ piyadassiṃ mahāmuniṃ  
 sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   aptha            
 aññe  piṭṭhe ca pallaṅke āsandisu  nisīdare   
 tuvaṃ  si  sabbadassāvī nisīda ratanāsane   aptha            
 sabbaratanamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ   nimminitvāna tāvade  
 piyadassissa munino āsanam iddhinimmitaṃ   aptha            
 ratane ca nisinnassa pīṭhake iddhinimmite  
 kumbhamattaṃ jambuphalam adāsi tāvade ahaṃ   aptha            
 mama hāsaṃ janetvāna paribhuñji mahāmuni  
 tadā   cittaṃ pasādetvā satthāram abhivādayiṃ   aptha            
 piyadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 ratanāsanam āsīno imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
 yo me ratanamayaṃ pīṭham amatañ ca phalam adā  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 sattasattatikappāni devaloke ramissati  
 pañcasattatikkhattuñ ca cakkavattī bhavissati   aptha            
 dvattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto   asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 saṭṭhiṃ dhenusahassāni  sabbā kaṃsūpadhāraṇā  
 tāyo pi  chaḍḍayitvāna pabbajim anagāriyaṃ   aptha            
 saṭṭhiṃ itthisahassāni  sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā  aptha            
 āḷārapamhā hasulā susoññā tanumajjhimā  
 tā hitvā kandamānāyo  pabbajim anagāriyaṃ   aptha            
 saṭṭhigāmasahassāni paripuṇṇāni sabbaso  
 chaḍḍayitvāna taṃ rajjaṃ pabbajim anagāriyaṃ   aptha            
 nagarā nikkhamitvāna himavantam upāgamiṃ  
 bhāgīrasīnadītīre assamaṃ māpayim ahaṃ   aptha            
 paṇṇasālaṃ karitvāna agyāgāram akās  ahaṃ  
 āraddhaviriyo pahitatto vasāmi assame ahaṃ   aptha            
 maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā suññāgāre va jhāyato  
 na uppajjatha  tāso me na passe bhayabheravaṃ   aptha            
 sumedho nāma sambuddho aggo kāruṇiko muni  
 ñāṇālokena jotento loke uppajji tāvade   aptha            
 mama assamasāmantā yakkho āsi mahiddhiko  
 buddhaseṭṭhamhi uppanne ārocesi mamaṃ tadā   aptha            
  buddho loke samuppanno sumedho nāma cakkhumā  
 tāreti janataṃ sabbaṃ tvam pi so tārayissati    aptha            
 yakkhassa vacanaṃ sutvā saṃviggo āsi tāvade  
 buddho  buddho  ti cintento assamaṃ paṭisāmayiṃ   aptha            
 aggidāruñ ca chaḍḍetvā saṃsāmetvāna santhataṃ  
 assamam abhivanditvā nikkhamiṃ pavanā ahaṃ   aptha            
 tato candanam ādāya gāmāgāmaṃ purāpuraṃ  
 devadevaṃ gavesanto upagacchiṃ  vināyakaṃ   aptha            
 bhagavā tamhi samaye sumedho lokanāyako  
 catusaccaṃ pakāsento bodheti janataṃ tadā    aptha            
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna sīse katvāna candanaṃ  
 sambuddham abhivādetvā imā gāthā abbāsatha   aptha            
 vassike pupphamānamhi santike upavāyati  
 tvaṃ vīra guṇagandhena disā sabbā pavāyasi   aptha            
 campake nāgavanike atimuttakakeṭake  
 sālesu pupphamānesu anuvātaṃ pavāyati   aptha

 tato  pāsādam āruyha ubbiddhā gehalañchakā   
 tattha naccehi gītehi parivārem  ahaṃ tadā   aptha           
 turiyā āhatā  mayhaṃ samatālasamāhitā  
 naccantā itthiyo sabbā haranti ñeva me mano   aptha           
 velāmikā  vāmanikā  kujjā vā sīhi majjhikā   
 laṅghikā sokajjhāyī  ca parivārenti maṃ sadā   aptha           
 vetālino kumbhaṭhūṇī  naṭā ca naccakā  bahū  
 naṭakā nāṭakā  c  eva parivārenti maṃ sadā   aptha           
 kappakā nhāpakā sūdā mālākārā sumāpakā    
 jallā mallā ti sabbe va parivārenti maṃ sadā     aptha           
 etesu kīḷamānesu sikkhite katupāsane  
 rattindivaṃ na jānāmi indo va tidasaṃgaṇe   aptha           
 aṭṭhikā   pathikā   sabbe yācakā carakā bahū  
 upagacchanti te niccaṃ bhikkhayantā mamaṃ ghare   aptha           
 samaṇā brāhmaṇā c  eva puññakhettā anuttarā  
 vaddhayantā mamaṃ puññaṃ āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ   aptha           
 padakā   laṭukā   sabbe nigaṇṭhā pupphasāṭakā    
 tedaṇḍikā   ekasikhā āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ     aptha            
 ājīvikā viluttāvī gotamā devadhammikā  
 rajojalladharā ete āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ     aptha            
 parivattakā   siddhipattā koṇḍa puggalikā   bahū  
 tapassī   vanacārī ca āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ   aptha            
 oḍḍakā   damiḷā   c  eva sākuḷā   malayāḷakā    
 sabarā   yonakā   c  eva āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ   aptha

 dovārikā anīkaṭṭhā sandhikā  pupphachaḍḍhakā  
 hatthāruhā hatthipālā āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ   aptha            
 arindamā nāma rañño  pamattassa adās  ahaṃ   
 sattavaṇṇena  ratanena ūnattaṃ  pūrayām  ahaṃ   aptha            
 ye mayā kittitā sabbe nānāvaṇṇa bahūjanā  
 tesāhaṃ cittam aññāya tappayiṃ ratanen  ahaṃ   aptha            
 vaggūsu bhāsamānāsu vajjamānāsu bherisu  
 saṅkhesu dhamayantesu  sake gehe ramām  ahaṃ   aptha            
 bhagavā tamhi samaye padumuttaranāyako  
 sahasatasahassehi  parikkhīṇāsavehi so   aptha            
 bhikkhuhi sahito vīthiṃ  paṭipajjittha  cakkhumā  
 obhāsento disā sabbā dīparukkho   va jotati   aptha            
 vajjanti bheriyo sabbā gacchante lokanāyake    
 pabhā niddhāvate   tassa sataraṃsīva m uggato   aptha            
 kavāṭ  antarikāyam pi   paviṭṭhe na ca rasminā    
 antogharesu vipulo āloko āsi tāvade   aptha            
 pabhaṃ disvāna buddhassa pārisajje avoc   ahaṃ  
 nissaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho imaṃ vīthim upāgato   aptha            
 khippam oruyha pāsādā agamiṃ   antarāpaṇaṃ  
 sambuddham abhivādento   imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ     aptha            
 anukampatu me buddho jalajuttamanāyako    
 vasīsatasahassehi adhivāsesi so muni   aptha            
 nimantayitvā sambuddham atinesiṃ   sakaṃ gharaṃ  
 tattha annena pānena santappesiṃ   mahāmuniṃ   aptha            
 bhuttāvikālam aññāya buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino  
 sataṅgikena   turiyena buddhaṃ seṭṭhaṃ   upaṭṭh  ahaṃ   aptha            
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 antoghare nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha

      jatukaṇṇika     
 yo maṃ turiyeh  upaṭṭhāsi  annapānaṃ c  adāsi me  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhasato   aptha            
 pahūtabhakkho hutvāna sahirañño sabhojano   
 catuddīpe ekarajjaṃ kārayissat  ayaṃ naro   aptha            
 pañcasīle samādāya dasakammapathe  tato  
 samādāya pavattanto  parisaṃ sikkhapessati    aptha            
 turiyasatasahassāni nariyo  samalaṅkatā  
 vajjayissanti maṃ niccam upaṭṭhānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati   
 catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  aptha            
 catusattatikkhatuñ ca cakkavattī bhavissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gananāto asaṅkhiyaṃ    aptha            
 kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha            
 upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattam atha mānusaṃ  
 anūnabhogo hutvāna manussattaṃ gamissati   aptha            
 ajjhāyako bhavitvāna tiṇṇavedāna pāragū  
 uttamatthaṃ gavesanto carissati mahiṃ imaṃ    aptha            
 so ca pacchā pabbajitvā  sukkhamūlena codito  
 gotamassa bhagavato sāsane bhiramissati     aptha            
 ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ  
 kilesā jhāpayitvāna arahā  yaṃ bhavissati   aptha            
 pavane vyaggharājā va migarājā va kesarī  
 abhīto viharām  ajja sakyaputtassa sāsane   aptha            
 devaloke manusse vā dalidde duggatimhi vā  
 nibbattiṃ me na passāmi upaṭṭhānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 vivekam anuyutto   mhi upasanto nirūpadhī  
 nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo   aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe        aptha

 mama assamasāmantā yakkho āsi mahiddhiko  
 so me pasaṃsi  sambuddhaṃ jalajuttamanāyakaṃ    aptha            
  esa buddho samuppanno padumuttaro mahāmuni  
 khippaṃ gantvāna sambuddhaṃ payirupāsassu  tam muni    aptha

 sālapuppham āharitvā maṇḍapaṃ chādayim ahaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano abhivandiṃ  tathāgataṃ   aptha           
 yaṃ vadanti sumedho ti bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha           
 buddhassa giram aññāya sabbe devā samāgamuṃ  
 asaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā   aptha           
 sumedho nāma sambuddho āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 devasaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha           
 yo me sattāham maṇḍapaṃ dhārayī sālachāditaṃ  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 devabhūto manusso vā hemavaṇṇo bhavissati  
 pahūtabhogo hutvāna kāmabhogi bhavissati   aptha            
 saṭṭhiṃ nāgasahassāni  sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā hemakappanivāsasā   aptha            
 ārūḷhā gāmānīyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihi   
 sāyapāto  upaṭṭhānam āgamissant  imaṃ naraṃ  
 tehi nāgehi parivuto ramissati ayaṃ naro   aptha            
 saṭṭhiassasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 ājānīyā va  jātiyā sindhavā sīghavāhino    aptha            
 ārūḷhā gāmanīyehi illiyā  cāpadhārihi   
 parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 saṭṭhirathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitā  
 dīpā atho pi veyyagghā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  aptha            
 ārūḷhā gāmanīyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 saṭṭhigāmasahassāni paripuṇṇāni sabbaso  
 pahūtadhanadhaññāni   susamiddhāni sabbaso  
 sadā pātubhavissanti buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ  aptha            
 hatthī assā rathā pattī   senā ca caturaṅginī

 aṭṭhārasaṃ kappasataṃ   devaloke ramissati

      bhaddāli     
 satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñ ca devarajjaṃ karissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gananāto  asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha            
 tiṃsakappasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha            
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharissat  anāsavo   aptha            
 tiṃsakappasahassamhi addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 etthantaram upādāya gavesiṃ  amataṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 lābhā mayhaṃ suladdham me yam ahaṃ ñāsi  sāsanaṃ  
 tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ   aptha            
 namo te purisājañña namo te purisuttama   
 tava ñāṇaṃ pakittetvā patto mhi acalaṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 yaṃ yaṃ yonūpapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 sabbattha sukhito homi phalaṃ me ñāṇakittane    aptha            
 idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo  
 nāgo va bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo   aptha

 itthaṃ sudam āyasmā bhaddāli thero i  g  a ti  
 bhaddālittherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       ekachattiya   
 candabhāgā nadītīre  assamo sukato mama  
 susuddhapuḷinākiṇṇo paṇṇasālāsumāpitā   aptha           
 uttānakūlā nadikā supatitthā manoramā  
 macchakacchapasampannā suṃsumāranisevitā   aptha           
 acchā mayūrā dīpī ca karavīkā ca sālikā  
 kūjanti  sabbadā ete sobhayantā mama assamaṃ   aptha           
 kokilā mañjubhāṇī  ca haṃsā ca madhurassarā  
 abhikūjanti  te tattha sobhayantā mama assamaṃ   aptha           
 sīhā vyagghā varāhā ca vakākoka taracchayo  
 giriduggaṃ pi  nādenti sobhayantā mama assamaṃ   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 eṇī migā ca sarabhā bheraṇḍā  sūkarā  bahū  
 giriduggaṃ pi  nādenti sobhayantā mama assamaṃ   aptha           
 uddālakā campakā ca pāṭalī sindhuvāritā    
 atimuttā asokā ca pupphanti mama assame   aptha           
 aṅkolā yūthikā  ceva sattalī bimbijālikā   
 kaṇṇikā kaṇṇikārā ca pupphanti mama assame   aptha           
 nāgā sālā ca saḷalā puṇḍarīk  ettha pupphitā  
 dibbā gandhā sampavantā sobhayanti mam  assamaṃ   aptha           
 ajjunā asanā c  ettha mahānāmā ca pupphitā  
 sālā ca kaṅgupupphā  ca sobhayanti mam  assamaṃ   aptha            
 ambā jambū ca tilakā nīpā  ca sāla kalyāṇī  
 dibbā gandhā sampavantā sobhayanti mama assamaṃ   aptha            
 asokā ca kapitthā  ca bhaginimāl  ettha pupphitā  
 dibbā gandhā sampavantā sobhayanti mam assamaṃ   aptha            
 kadambā kadalī c  eva isimuggā ca ropitā  
 dhuvaṃ phalāni dhārenti sobhayanti mam assamaṃ   aptha            
 harītakā āmalakā ambā jambū vibhītakā    
 kolā bhallātakā bellā phalino mama assame   aptha            
 avidūre pokkharaṇī supatitthā manoramā  
 mandālakehi   sañchannā padumupphalakehi ca   aptha            
 gabbhaṃ ganhanti padumā aññe pupphanti kesarī  
 opattakaṇṇikā   c  eva pupphanti mama assame   aptha

 acchodakamhi vicaraṃ sobhayanti mam assamaṃ   aptha

 dibbā gandhā sampavantā sobhayanti mam assamaṃ   aptha            
 puḷinā sobhanā tattha ākiṇṇā jalasevitā  
 ovaṭṭā   pupphitā santi sobhayanti mam assamaṃ   aptha

      ekachattiya     
 te jaṭābhārabharitā ajinuttaravāsino  
 vākacīradharā sabbe sobhayanti mam assamaṃ   aptha            
 yugamattaṃ pekkhamānā  nipakā santavuttino  
 kāmagedhe  anapekkhā vasanti mama assame   aptha            
 parūḷhakacchanakhalomā paṅkadantā  rajassirā  
 rajojalladharā sabbe vasanti mama assame   aptha            
 abhiññāpāramīpattā antalikkhacarā va  te  
 uggacchantā nabhaṃ ete sobhayanti mam assamaṃ   aptha            
 tehi sissehi parivuto vasāmi pavane tadā  
 rattindivaṃ na jānāmi sadā jhānasamappito   aptha            
 bhagavā ca tamhi samaye atthadassī mahāmuni  
 tam andhakāraṃ nāsento uppajji lokanāyako   aptha            
 atha aññataro sisso āgacchi  mama santike  
 mante ajjhetukāmo so chalaṅgaṃ nāma lakkhaṇaṃ   aptha            
 buddho loke samuppanno atthadassī mahāmuni  
 catusaccaṃ pakāsento deseti amataṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 tuṭṭhahaṭṭho pamudito dhammantaragatāsayo  
 assamā abhinikkhamma imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   aptha            
 buddho loke samuppanno dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo  
 etha sabbe gamissāma sammāsambuddhasantikaṃ    aptha            
 ovādappaṭikārā te saddhamme pāramiṅgatā  
  sādhū  ti saṃpaṭicchiṃsu uttamatthaṃ gavesakā    aptha            
 jaṭābhārabharitā te ajinuttaravāsino  
 uttamatthaṃ gavesantā nikkhamuṃ pavanā tadā   aptha            
 bhagavā tamhi samaye atthadassī mahāyaso  
 catusaccaṃ pakāsento deseti amataṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 setacchattaṃ gahetvāna  buddhaseṭṭhassa dhārayiṃ  
 ekāhaṃ dhārayitvāna buddhaseṭṭham avandi haṃ  aptha            
 atthadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
 yo me chattam adhāresi pasanno sehi pāṇihi   
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 imassa jāyamānassa devatte atha mānuse  
 dhārissati sadā chattaṃ chattadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       tiṇasūlakachādaniya   
 jātijarañ ca maraṇaṃ paccavekkhiṃ  ahaṃ tadā  
 ekato abhinikkamma pabbajim anagāriyaṃ   aptha           
 caramānānupubbena gaṅgātīram upāgamiṃ  
 tatth  addasāsiṃ paṭhaviṃ gaṅgātīre supuṇṇataṃ    aptha

 āsayā abhinikkhamma gajji so medinī  viya   aptha

      tiṇasūlakachādaniya     
 nadite migarāje va  hāso me udapajjatha   
 migarājaṃ gavesanto addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha           
 disvān  ahaṃ devadevaṃ  tissaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena pūjayiṃ nāgakesaraṃ   aptha           
 uggacchantaṃ va suriyaṃ sālarājaṃ pa pupphitaṃ  
 osadhiṃ va virocantaṃ santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha           
  tava ñāṇena sabbaññū jotesi maṃ sadevakaṃ  
 tvaṃ  hi ārādhayitvāna jātiyā parimuccare    aptha           
 adassanena sabbaññū buddhānaṃ sabbadassinaṃ  
 patantyavīcinirayaṃ rāgadosehi ophuṭā    aptha            
 tava dassanam āgamma sabbaññū lokanāyaka   
 pamuccanti bhavā sabbe phusanti amataṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 yadā buddhā cakkhumantā  uppajjanti pabhaṅkarā  
 kilese jhāpayitvāna ālokaṃ dassayanti te    aptha            
 kittayitvāna sambuddhaṃ tissaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ  
 haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena tiṇasūlam  apūjayiṃ   aptha            
 mama saṅkappam aññāya tisso lokagganāyako  
 sakāsane nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
 yo maṃ pupphehi chādesi pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 pañcavīsatikkhattuṃ so devarajjaṃ karissati  
 pañcasattatikkhattuñ ca cakkavattī bhavissati  aptha            
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ    
 tassa kammassa nissando pupphāna pūjanāya   so   aptha            
 sīsaṃ nhāto c  ayaṃ poso puppham ākaṅkhate c  ayaṃ    
 puññakammena saṃyutto   purato pātubhavissati   aptha            
 yaṃ yaṃ icchati kāmehi taṃ taṃ pātubhavissati  
 saṅkappaṃ paripūritvā nibbāyissat  anāsavo   aptha            
 kilesā jhāpayitvāna sampajāno patissato    
 ekāsane nisīditvā arahattam apāpuṇiṃ   aptha

       madhumaṃsadāyaka   
 nagare bandhumatiyā sūkariko ahos  ahaṃ  
 ukkoṭakaṃ randhayitvā madhusappimhi  ākiriṃ    aptha           
 sannipātam ahaṃ gantvā ekaṃ pattaṃ gahes  ahaṃ   
 pūrayitvāna taṃ pattaṃ bhikkhusaṅghassa dās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 yo ttha therataro bhikkhu  niyyātesi mamaṃ tadā   
 iminā pattapūrena labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ   aptha           
 dve sampattiyo bhutvā sukkamūlena codito  
 pacchime vattamānamhi kilese jhāpayissati   aptha           
 tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ  
 tattha bhutvā ca pitvā  ca labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ   aptha           
 maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā pubbakammam anussariṃ  
 annapānābhivasso me abhivassati tāvade   aptha           
 idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo  
 idhāpi annapānam me vassate sabbakālikaṃ   aptha           
 ten  eva maṃsadānena  sandhāvitvā bhave ahaṃ  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha

       yāgudāyaka   
 atithiṃ  me gahetvāna āgacchiṃ gāmakam tadā  
 sampuṇṇa nadikaṃ disvā saṅghārāmam upāgamiṃ   aptha           
 āraññakā dhūtavādā jhāyino lukhacīvarā  
 vivekābhiratā dhīrā saṅghārāme vasanti te   aptha           
 gati tesam upacchinnā suvimuttāna tādinaṃ  
 piṇḍāya te na gacchanti oruddhanadikā yadi   aptha           
 pasannacitto sumano vedajāto  katañjalī  
 taṇḍulam me gahetvāna yāgudānam akās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 pañcannaṃ yāguṃ datvāna pasanno sehi pāṇihi  
 sakakammābhiraddho haṃ tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 maṇimayañ ca me vyamhaṃ  nibbattan tidase gaṇe   
 nārīgaṇehi sahito modāmi vyamha m uttame    aptha           
 tettiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ   
 tiṃsakkhattuṃ cakkavattī mahārajjam akārayiṃ    aptha           
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  
 devaloke manusse  vā anubhotvā   yasam ahaṃ   aptha           
 pacchime bhave sampatte pabbajim   anagāriyaṃ  
 saha oropite kese sabbasampattivijjh   ahaṃ     aptha           
 khayato vayato cāpi sammasanto kalebaraṃ  
  pure si  kkhāpadādāne arahattam apāpuṇiṃ   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 sudinnam me dānavaraṃ vānijjaṃ suppayojitaṃ   
 ten  eva yāgudānena patto mhi acalaṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 sokaṃ pariddavaṃ vyādhiṃ  darathaṃ cittatāpanaṃ  
 nābhijānāmi uppannaṃ yāgudānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 yāguṃ saṅghassa datvāna puññakkhette anuttare  
 pañcānisaṃse anubhom  aho yāgu suyiṭṭhatā    aptha            
 avyādhitā rūpavatā khippaṃ dhammanisantitā  
 lābhitā annapānassa āyu pañcamakaṃ mama   aptha            
 yo koci vedaṃ janayaṃ saṃghe yāguṃ  dadey ya so  
 imāni pañcaṭhānāni patigaṇheyya paṇḍito   aptha

 sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo n  atthi dāni punabbhavo   aptha

 namassamāno sambuddhaṃ dhammassa ca sudhammataṃ   aptha

       patthodanadāyaka   
 vanacārī pure āsiṃ satataṃ vanakammiko  
 patthodanaṃ  gahetvāna kammantam agamās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tatth  addasāsiṃ  sambuddhaṃ sayambhum aparājitaṃ  
 vanā piṇḍāya nikkhantaṃ disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ   aptha           
 parakammāyane yutto puññañ ca me na vijjati  
 ayaṃ patthodanam atthi bhojayissām  ahaṃ muniṃ   aptha           
 patthodanaṃ gahetvāna sayambhussa adās  ahaṃ  
 mama nijjhāyamānassa paribhuñji tadā muni   aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ   aptha

       mañcadāyaka

 vitthārike  pāvacane devamānusasakkate    aptha

 tena kammena jīvāmi tena posemi dārake   aptha           
 āsandiṃ sukataṃ katvā pasanno sehi pāṇihi   
 sayam eva upāgantvā  bhikkhusaṅghass adās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ   aptha

 paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 asītikkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī ahos  ahaṃ   aptha

       sakiṃsammajjaka   
 vipassino bhagavato pāṭalibodhiṃ  uttamaṃ  
 disvā va taṃ pā dapaggaṃ  tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ   aptha           
 sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna bodhiṃ sammajji  tāvade  
 sammajjitvāna taṃ bodhim avandiṃ pāṭaliṃ ahaṃ   aptha           
 tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā sire katvāna añjaliṃ

 cārima maggena   gacchāmi saranto bodhim uttamaṃ  
 ajagaro  maṃ pīḷesi gho ra rūpo mahābalo   aptha

      ekadussadāyaka     
 āsanne me  kataṃ kammaṃ phalena  tosayī mamaṃ  
 kalebaraṃ me gilati devaloke ramām  ahaṃ   aptha           
 anāvilaṃ mama cittaṃ vi suddhaṃ paṇḍaraṃ sadā  
 sokasallaṃ  na jānāmi cittasantāpanaṃ mama   aptha           
 kuṭṭhaṃ gaṇḍo kilāso ca apamāro vitacchikā  
 daddu kaṇḍu ca me n  atthi phalaṃ sammajjanāy  idaṃ   aptha           
 soko ca paridevo ca hadaye me na vijjati  
 asattam  ujukaṃ cittaṃ phalaṃ sammajjanāy  idaṃ   aptha           
  samādhisu na sajjā mi visuddhaṃ hoti mānasaṃ  
 yaṃ yaṃ samādhim icchāmi so  so sampajjate mama   aptha           
 rajanīye na rajjāmi atho dosaniyesu ca  
 mohanīye na muyhāmi phalaṃ sammajjanāy  idaṃ   aptha            
 ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammam ākariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phalaṃ  sammaj janāy  idaṃ   aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudam āyasmā sakiṃsammajjako  thero i  g  a ti  
 sakiṃsammajjakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       ekadussadāyaka   
 nagare haṃsavatiyā āhosiṃ tiṇahārako  
 tiṇahārena jīvāmi tena posemi dārake   aptha           
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  
 tam andhakāraṃ nāsetvā uppajji lokanāyako   aptha           
 sake ghare nisīditvā evaṃ cintesi tāvade   
 buddho loke samuppanno deyyadhammo na vijjati   aptha           
 idaṃ me sāṭakam  ekaṃ n  atthi me koci dāyako  
 dukkho nirayasamphasso  ropayissāmi dakkhiṇaṃ   aptha           
 evāhaṃ cintayitvāna sakaṃ cittaṃ  pasādayiṃ  
 ekaṃ dussaṃ gahetvāna buddhaseṭṭhassa dās  ahaṃ   aptha

  yadi buddho tuvaṃ vīra tārehi maṃ mahāmuni    aptha           
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mama dānaṃ pakittento akā  me anumodanaṃ   aptha           
  iminā ekadussena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 kappasatasahassāni vinipātaṃ na gacchasi    aptha           
 chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissasi   
 tettiṃsakkhattuṃ  rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissasi   aptha           
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ

  pāduddhāre pāduddhāre dussaṃ nibbattate mama  
 heṭṭhā dussamhi tiṭṭhāmi uparicchadanaṃ   mama   aptha

 suvaṇṇavaṇṇo hutvāna saṃsarāmi bhavābhave   aptha

 ayam me pacchimā jāti vipaccati   idhāpi me   aptha

 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ekadussass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

      ekāsanadāyaka     
  
       ekāsanadāyaka   
 himavantass  avidūre kosiko  nāma pabbato  
 assamo sukato mayhaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā   aptha           
 nārado nāma nāmena kassapo iti maṃ vidū  
 suddhimaggaṃ gavesanto vasāmi kosike  tadā   aptha           
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  
 vivekakāmo sambuddho āgacchi anilañjasā    aptha           
 vanagge gacchamānassa disvā raṃsiṃ mahesino  
 kaṭṭhamañcaṃ paññapetvāna ajinañ ca apatthariṃ    aptha           
 āsanaṃ paññapetvāna sire katvāna añjaliṃ  
 somanassaṃ pavedetvā  imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ    aptha           
 sallakatto tuvaṃ vīra āturānaṃ tikicchako  
 mamaṃ  rogaparetassa  tikicchaṃ dehi nāyaka    aptha           
 kallaṭṭhikā ye   passanti buddhaseṭṭha tavam   mune  
 dhuvaṃ ti siddhiṃ   papponti etesaṃ jajjaro bhavo     aptha           
 na me deyyaṃ tavam   atthi pavattaphalabhoji haṃ  
 idaṃ me āsanam atthi nisīda kaṭṭhamañcake   aptha           
 nisīdi tattha bhagavā asambhīto   va kesarī  
 muhuttaṃ vītināmetvā imaṃ vacanam abravi     aptha           
  vissaṭṭho hohi  mā bhāyi  laddho jotiraso tayā  
 yaṃ tuyhaṃ patthitaṃ sabbaṃ paripūressati nāgate     aptha            
 na thokaṃ taṃ kataṃ tuyhaṃ puññakkhette anuttare  
 sakkā uddharitum attā yassa cittaṃ paṇīhitaṃ     aptha            
 iminā āsanadānena cetanāpanidhīhi ca  
 kappasatasahassāni vinipātaṃ na gacchasi   aptha            
 paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissasi    
 āsītikkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissasi     aptha

     therāpadāna 
 susampannaṃ tadā khettaṃ dhaññaṃ me phalitam  ahu  
 pākakāle ca sampatte evaṃ cintes  ahaṃ tadā   aptha           
 nacchannaṃ nappaṭirūpaṃ jānantassa guṇā gu ṇaṃ  
 yo haṃ saṅghe adatvāna aggaṃ bhuñjeyya maṃ tadā   aptha           
 ayaṃ buddho asamasamo battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo  
 tato pabhāvito  saṅgho puññakkhetto anuttaro   aptha           
 tattha dassām  ahaṃ dānaṃ navasassaṃ pure pure  
 evāhaṃ cintayitvāna haṭṭho pīṇitamānaso    aptha           
 khettato dhaññam āharitvā sambuddham upasaṅkamiṃ  
 upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 vanditvā satthuno pāde imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   aptha           
 navasassañ ca sampannam  āyāgo  pi ca taṃ  mune  
 anukampam upādāya adhivāsehi cakkhumā   aptha           
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mamaṃ saṅkappam aññāya imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   aptha           
 cattāro ca paṭipannā cattāro ca phale ṭhitā  
 esa saṅgho ujubhūto paññā sīla samāhito  aptha           
 yajantānaṃ manussānaṃ puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ  
 karontaṃ opadhikaṃ  puññaṃ saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ   aptha            
 tasmiṃ saṅghe ca dātabbaṃ navasassaṃ tathetaraṃ  
 saṅghato uddisitvāna bhikkhū  netvāna saṃ   gharaṃ  
 paṭiyattaṃ ghare yan te   bhikkhusaṅghassa dehi tvaṃ   aptha            
 saṅghato uddisitvāna bhikkhū   netvāna haṃ gharaṃ  
 yaṃ ghare paṭiyattaṃ me bhikkhusaṅghassa dās  ahaṃ   aptha            
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsam agacch  ahaṃ   aptha            
 tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ   sovaṇṇaṃ sappabhassaraṃ  
 saṭṭhiyojanam ubbiddhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ   aptha            
 ākiṇṇaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ nārīgaṇasamākulaṃ  
 tattha   bhutvā pivitvā ca vasāmi tidase ahaṃ   aptha

 satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñ ca cakkavattī ahos  ahaṃ  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha

 bhoge me ūnatā n  atthi navasassass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       sovaṇṇakiṅkhaniya   
 saddhāya abhinikkhamma pabbajim  anagāriyaṃ  
 vākacīradharo āsiṃ  tapokammam  apassito   aptha           
 atthadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 uppajji tamhi samaye tārayanto mahājanaṃ   aptha           
 balañ ca vata me khīṇaṃ  vyādhinā paramen  ahaṃ  
 buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna puline thūpam uttamaṃ   aptha           
 karitvā haṭṭhacitto haṃ sahassena samokiriṃ   
 soṇṇakiṅkhanipupphāni uddaggamanaso ahaṃ   aptha           
 sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ thūpaṃ paricarim ahaṃ  
 tena cetopasādena atthadassissa tādino  aptha           
 devalokagato santo labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  
 suvaṇṇavaṇṇo tatthāsiṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 asītikoṭiyo mayhaṃ nāriyo samalaṅkatā  
 sadā mayham upaṭṭhanti  buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 saṭṭhiṃ turiyasahassāni  bheriyo paṇavāni  ca  
 saṅkhā ca deṇḍimā   tattha vaggu vadati dundubhi     aptha           
 cullāsītisahassāni hatthino   samalaṅkatā  
 tidhappabhinnamātaṅgā kuñjarā saṭṭhihāyanā    aptha           
 hemajālābhisañchannā upaṭṭhānaṃ karonti me  
 balakāye gaje   c  eva ūnatā me na vijjati   aptha            
 soṇṇakiṅkhanipupph ānaṃ  vipākam anubhon  ahaṃ  
 aṭṭhapaññāsakkhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ   aptha            
 ekasattatikkhāttuñ ca cakkavatti ahos  ahaṃ  
 pathavyā rajjam ekasataṃ mahiyā kārayim ahaṃ   aptha            
 so dāni patto amatam asaṅkhataṃ sududdasaṃ  
  saṃyojan  aparikkhīṇo n  atthi dāni punabbhavo   aptha            
 aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ puppham abhiropayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       sovaṇṇakattarika   
 manobhāvaniyaṃ buddham attadantaṃ samāhitaṃ  
 iriyamānaṃ  brahmapathe  citta vūpasame rataṃ  aptha           
 nittiṇṇa oghaṃ sambuddhaṃ jhāyi jhānarataṃ muniṃ  
 upaviṭṭhaṃ  samāpannam indīvaradalappabhaṃ  aptha

 āṇāpesi ca sambuddho padamuttaranāyako  
 imin  odakam āhatvā  pādamūle ṭhapehi me   aptha           
 sādhūti haṃ paṭissutvā satthu gāravatāya ca  
 udakaṃ lābun  āhatvā buddhaseṭṭham upānayiṃ   aptha           
 anumodi mahāvīro cittaṃ nibbāpayaṃ mamaṃ   
  iminā lābudānena saṅkappo te samijjhatu    aptha           
 pannarasesu kappesu devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ  
 tiṃsatikkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī ahos  ahaṃ   aptha           
 diva vā yadi vā rattiṃ caṅkamantassa tiṭṭhato  
 sovaṇṇaṃ kattaraṃ  gayha tiṭṭhati purato mama   aptha           
 buddhassa datvāna lābuṃ labhāmi soṇṇakattaraṃ   
 appakampikataṃ  kāraṃ vipulaṃ hoti tādisaṃ     aptha           
 satasahasse ito kappe yam alābum adaṃ   tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi alābussa idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       ekavihāriya   
 imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso  
 kassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo   aptha           
 nippapañco nirālambo ākāsasamamānaso  
 puññatā bahulo  tādi animittarato vasī   aptha           
 asaṅgacitto nikleso  asaṃsaṭṭho kule gaṇe  
 mahākāruṇiko vīro vinayopāyakovido   aptha           
 uyyutto  parakiccesu vinayanto sadevake  
 nibbānagamanaṃ maggaṃ gatipaṅkavisosanaṃ   aptha           
 amataṃ param assādaṃ   jarāmaccunivāraṇaṃ  
 mahāparisamajjhe so nisinno lokatāraṇo   aptha           
 karavīkarudo nātho brahmaghoso tathāgato  
 uddharanto mahāduggā   vippanaṭṭhe anāyake   aptha           
 desento virajaṃ dhammaṃ diṭṭho me lokanāyako  
 tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ   aptha           
 pabbajitvā tadā vāhaṃ cintento jinasāsanaṃ  
 ekako pavane ramme   vasiṃ   saṃsaggapīḷito   aptha           
 savkāyaūpakaṭṭho me   hetubhūto   mam āgami    
 manaso vūpakaṭṭhassa   saṃsaggabhayadassino   aptha

 vipassino bhagavato mahābodhimaho ahū  
 mahājanā samāgamma pūjenti bodhim uttamaṃ   aptha           
 na hi taṃ orakaṃ  maññe buddhaseṭṭho bhavissati

       pāṭihīrasaññaka   
 padumuttaro nāma jino āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 vasīsatasahassehi nagaraṃ pāvisī  tadā   aptha           
 nagaraṃ pavisantassa upasantassa tādino  
 ratanāni panādiṃsu  nigghoso āsi tāvade   aptha           
 buddhassa ānubhāvena bherivajjanaghaṭṭitā   
 sayaṃ vīṇā pavajjanti buddhassa pavisato puraṃ   aptha           
 buddhaseṭṭhaṃ namassāmi  padumuttaraṃ mahāmuniṃ

      bodhighariya     
 mama saṅkappam aññāya vyamhaṃ  nibbattate subhaṃ

 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ vedikam akārayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       bodhighariya   
 siddhatthassa bhagavato dipadindassa tādino  
 pasannacitto sumano bodhigharam akārayiṃ   aptha           
 tusitaṃ upapanno mhi vasāmi ratane ghare  
 na me sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā vāto gatte na samphuse    aptha           
 pañcasaṭṭhimh  ito kappe cakkavattī ahos  ahaṃ  
 kāsikaṃ  nāma nagaraṃ vissakammena  māpitaṃ  aptha           
 dasayojana āyāmaṃ aṭṭhayojana vitthataṃ  
 na tamhi nagare atthi kaṭṭhaṃ vallī  ca  mattikā   aptha           
 tiriyaṃ yojanaṃ āsi addhayojana vitthataṃ  
 maṅgalo nāma pāsādo vissakammena  māpito   aptha           
 cullāsītisahassāni thambhā sovaṇṇayā ahuṃ   
 maṇimayā ca niyyuhā chadanaṃ rūpiyaṃ ahū   aptha           
 sabbasovaṇṇayaṃ gharaṃ vissakammena  māpitaṃ  
 ajjhāvutthaṃ mayā etaṃ gharadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 te sabbe anubhotvāna devamānusake bhave  
 ajja patto  mhi nibbānaṃ santipadam anuttaraṃ   aptha
