       ekachattiya   
 aṅgārajātā puthuvī kukkulānugatā mahī  
 padumuttaro  bhagavā abbhokāsamhi caṅkami   aptha           
 paṇḍaraṃ chattaṃ  ādāya addhānaṃ paṭipajj  ahaṃ  
 tattha disvāna sambuddhaṃ vitti me upapajjatha   aptha           
 marīcivophuṭā  bhūmi aṅgārā va mahī ayaṃ  
 upavāyanti  mahāvātā sarīrass  ānukhepanā   aptha           
 sītaṃ uṇhaṃ viharanti   vātātapanivāraṇaṃ  
 patigaṇha imaṃ chattaṃ phassayissāmi  nibbutiṃ   aptha           
 anukampako kāruṇiko padumuttaro mahāyaso  
 mama saṅkappam aññāya patigaṇhi tadā jino   aptha           
 tiṃsakappāni devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti ahos  ahaṃ  aptha           
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇahāto  asaṅkhiyaṃ  
 anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe sukatam attano   aptha           
 ayaṃ me pacchimā jāti carimo vattate bhavo  
 ajjāpi setacchattaṃ me sabbakālaṃ dhariyyati    aptha           
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ chattam adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi chattadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       sayampaṭibhāniya   
 kakudhaṃ vilasantaṃ va devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ ko disvā nappasīdati   aptha           
 tam andhakāraṃ nāsetvā santāretvā bahūjanaṃ  
 ñāṇālokena jotentaṃ  ko disvā nappasīdati   aptha           
 vasīsatasahassehi niyyantan  lokanāyakaṃ  
 uddharantaṃ bahū satte ko disvā nappasīdati   aptha           
 āhanantaṃ  dhammabheriṃ maddantaṃ titthiye gaṇe  
 sīhanādaṃ vinādantaṃ  ko disvā na ppasīdati   aptha           
 yāvatā brahmalokato āgantvāna sabrahmakā  
 pucchanti nipuṇe pañhe ko disvā na ppasīdati   aptha           
 yass  añjaliṃ karitvāna āyācanti sadevakā  
 tena puññam anubhonti ko disvā na ppasīdati   aptha           
 sabbe janā samāgantvā sampavārenti cakkhumaṃ  
 na vikampati ajjhiṭṭho ko disvā na ppasīdati   aptha           
 nagaraṃ pavisato  yassa ra va nte  bheriyo bahū  
 vinadanti  anugajjā  ko disvā nappasīdati   aptha           
 vīthiyā  gacchato yassa sabbābhā   jotate sadā    
 abbhuṇṇatā   samā honti ko disvā na ppasīdati   aptha

       nimittavyākaraṇīya   
 ajjhogahetvā himavaṃ mante vācem  ahaṃ tadā  
 catupaññāsasahassāni sissā mayham upaṭṭhahuṃ   aptha           
 adhītā  vedagū sabbe chalaṅge pāramiṅgatā  
 sakavijjāh  upatthaddhā  himavante vasanti te   aptha           
 cavitvā tusitākāyā devaputto mahāyaso  
 uppajji mātukucchismiṃ  sampajāno paṭissato   aptha           
 sambuddhe upapajjante dasasahassī pakampatha  
 andhā cakkhuṃ alatthaṃsu  uppajjantamhi  nāyake   aptha           
 chabbikāraṃ  pakampittha   kevalā vasudhā ayaṃ  
 nigghosasaddaṃ sutvāna ubbijjiṃsu   mahājanā   aptha           
 sabbe janā samāgamma āgacchuṃ   mama santikaṃ  
  vasudhāyaṃ pakampittha kiṃ vipāko bhavissati    aptha           
 avacāsi tadā tesaṃ  mā bhetha   n  atthi vo bhayaṃ  
 vissatthā hotha sabbe pi  uppādo yaṃ sukhatthiko   aptha           
 aṭṭhahetuhi samphassa   vasudhāyaṃ pakampati    
 tathā nimittā dissanti obhāso vipulo mahā   aptha           
 asaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho uppajjissati cakkhumā  
 saññāpetvāna janataṃ pañcasīle kathem  ahaṃ    aptha

      maṇipūjaka     
  
       maṇipūjaka   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  
 vivekakāmo sambuddho gacchate anilañjase    aptha           
 avidūre himavato  mahājātassaro ahū   
 tattha me bhavanaṃ āsi puññakammena  saṃ yutaṃ   aptha           
 bhavanā abhinikkhamma addasaṃ lokanāsanaṃ  
 indīvaraṃ va jalitam ādittaṃ va hutāsanaṃ   aptha           
 vicinaṃ nāddasaṃ pupphaṃ pūjayissan ti nāyakaṃ  
 sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā avandiṃ  satthuno ahaṃ   aptha           
 mama sīse maṇiṃ  gayha pūjayiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 imāya maṇipūjāya vipāko  hotu bhadda ko   aptha           
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 antalikkhe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha           
  so te ijjhatu saṅkappo labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  
 imāya maṇipūjāya anubhohi  mahāyasaṃ    aptha           
 idaṃ  vatvāna  bhagavā jalajuttamanāmako   
 agamāsi buddhaseṭṭho yattha  cittaṃ paṇīhitaṃ   aptha           
 saṭṭhikappāni devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 anekasatakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti  ahos  ahaṃ   aptha           
 pubbakammaṃ sarantassa devabhūtassa me sato  
 maṇi nibbattate mayhaṃ ālokakaraṇo   mama   aptha            
 chalāsītisahassāni nariyo me pariggahā  
 vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā  aptha            
 aḷārapamhā hasulā   susoññā tanumajjhimā  
 parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ maṇipūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 sovaṇṇamayā maṇimayā lohitaṅkamayā tathā  
 bhaṇḍā katākatā bhonti   yadicchāya pilandhanā   aptha            
 kūṭāgārā guhā rammā sayanañ ca mahārahaṃ  
 mama saṅkappam aññāya nibbattanti yadicchakaṃ   aptha            
 lābhā tesaṃ suladdhaṃ va ye labhanti upassutiṃ  
 puññakkhettaṃ manussānam osadhaṃ sabbapāṇinaṃ   aptha

 mayham pi sukataṃ kammaṃ yo haṃ addakkhi  nāyakaṃ

       ukkāsatika   
 kosiko nāma bhagavā cittakuṭe vasī tadā  
 jhāyī jhānarato buddho vivekābhirato muni   aptha           
 ajjhogahetvā himavantaṃ nārīgaṇapurakkhato  
 addasaṃ kosikaṃ buddhaṃ puṇṇamāse va candimaṃ   aptha           
 ukkāsate  gahetvāna parivāres  ahaṃ tadā  
 sattarattindivaṃ ṭhatvā aṭṭhamena  agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
  vuṭṭhi taṃ kosikaṃ buddhaṃ sayambhum aparājitaṃ  
 pasannacitto vanditvā ekaṃ bhikkhaṃ adās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tena kammena dipadindaṃ lokajāṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  
 uppajjiṃ tusite kāye ekabhikkhass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 divasañ c  eva rattiñ ca āloko hoti me sadā  
 samantā yojanasataṃ obhāsena pharām  ahaṃ   aptha           
 pañcapaññāsakappamhi cakkavattī ahos  ahaṃ  
 cāturanto vijitā vī  jambusaṇḍassa issaro   aptha           
 tadā me nagaraṃ āsi iddhaṃ phītaṃ  sunimmitaṃ  
 tiṃsayojana āyāmaṃ vitthārena ca vīsati   aptha           
 sobhanaṃ nāma nagaraṃ vissakammena  mapitaṃ  
 dasasaddāvivittan taṃ samatālasamāhitaṃ   aptha

      pānadhidāyaka     
  
       pānadhidāyaka   
 anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 divāvihārā nikkhamma patham āruhi cakkhumā   aptha           
 pānadhiṃ  sukataṃ gayha addhānaṃ paṭipajj  ahaṃ  
 tatth  addasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ pattikañ cārudassanaṃ   aptha           
 sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā nīharitvāna pānadhiṃ   
 pādamūle ṭhapetvāna idaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   aptha           
 abhirūha mahāvīra sugat inda vināyaka  
 ito phalaṃ labhissāmi  yo me attho samijjhatu   aptha           
 anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 pānadhim  abhirūhitvā imaṃ vacanam abravi   aptha           
 yo pānadhim me adadā pasanno sehi pāṇihi   
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha           
 buddhassa giram aññāya sabbe devā samāgatā  
 udaggacittā sumanā vedajātā katañjalī   aptha           
 pānadhīnaṃ padānena  sukhito yaṃ bhavissati  
 pañcapaññāsakkhattuñ ca devarajjaṃ karissati   aptha           
 sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha           
 aparimeyye ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha            
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo   aptha            
 devaloke manusse vā nibbattissati puññavā  
 devayānapaṭibhāgaṃ yānaṃ paṭilabhissati   aptha            
 pāsādā sivikā mayhaṃ hatthino samalaṅkatā  
 rathā c  ājañña saṃyuttā sadā pātubhavanti me   aptha            
 agārā nikkhamanto pi rathena nikkhamām  ahaṃ  
 kesesu chijjamānesu arahattam apāpuṇiṃ   aptha            
 lābhā mayhaṃ suladdham me vānijjaṃ suppayojitaṃ  
 datvāna pānadhiṃ  ekaṃ patto mhi acalaṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 aparimeyy  ito kappe yaṃ pānadhim  adās  ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pānadhissa idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

      buddhasaññaka     
 tatth  addasaṃ paṃsukūlaṃ dumagge laggitaṃ tadā  
 cāpaṃ tatth  eva nikkhippa sire katvāna añjaliṃ   aptha           
 pasannacitto sumano vipulāya ca pītiyā  
 buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna paṃsukūlaṃ avandi haṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha

       buddhasaññaka   
 ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragū   
 lakkhaṇe  itihāse ca sanighaṇḍu sa keṭubhe   aptha           
 nadīsotapaṭibhāgā sissā āyanti me tadā  
 tesāhaṃ mante  vācemi rattindivam atandito   aptha           
 siddhattho nāma sambuddho loke uppajji tāvade  
 tam andhakāraṃ nāsetvā ñāṇalokaṃ  pavattayi   aptha           
 mama aññataro sisso sissānaṃ so kathesi me  
 sutvāna te etam atthaṃ ārocesuṃ maman tadā   aptha           
  buddho loke samuppanno sabbaññū lokanāyako  
 tassānuvattati jano lābho amhaṃ na hessati     aptha           
 adhiccuppattikā buddhā cakkhumanto mahāyasā  
 yannūnāhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhaṃ passeyyaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha           
 ajinam me gahetvāna vākacīraṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ  
 assamā abhinikkhamma sisse āmantayiṃ ahaṃ   aptha           
 odumbarakapupphaṃ va candamhi sasakaṃ yathā  
 vāyasānaṃ yathā khīraṃ dullabhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha           
 buddho lokamhi uppanno manussattam pi dullabhaṃ  
 ubhosu vijjamānesu savanañ ca sudullabhaṃ   aptha           
 buddho loke samuppanno cakkhuṃ lacchāma no bhavaṃ   
 etha  sabbe gamissāma sammāsambuddhasantikaṃ    aptha

       bhisadāyaka   
 ogayhāhaṃ pokkharaṇiṃ nānākuñjarasevitaṃ  
 uddharāmi bhisaṃ tattha ghāsahetu  ahaṃ tadā   aptha           
 bhagavā ca tamhi samaye padumuttara savhayo  
 rattam baradharo buddho gacchati anilañjase    aptha           
 dhunanto  paṃsukūlāni saddam assos  ahaṃ tadā  
 uddhaṃ nijjhāyamāno   haṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha           
 tatth  eva ṭhitako santo āyāciṃ   lokanāyakaṃ  
  madhu bhisehi savati khirasa  ppi muḷālibhi  
 paṭigaṇhātu me buddho anukampāya cakkhumā   aptha           
 tato kāruṇiko satthā orohitvā mahāyaso  
 patigaṇhi mamaṃ bhikkhaṃ anukampāya cakkhumā   aptha           
 patiggahetvā   sambuddho akā me anumodanaṃ   
  sukhī hohi mahāpuñña   gati tuyhaṃ samijjhatu  
 iminā bhisadānena labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ    aptha

      bhisadāyaka     
 idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho jalajuttamanāmako  
 bhikkham ādāya sambuddho ambarena gami jino   aptha           
 tato bhisaṃ gahetvāna āgacchiṃ  mama assamaṃ  
 bhisaṃ rukkhe lagetvāna  mama dānaṃ anussariṃ   aptha           
 mahāvāto vuṭṭhahitvā sañjālesi vanan tadā  
 ākāso abhinādittha  asaniyā phalantiyā   aptha           
 tato me asanipāto matthake nipatī tadā  
 so haṃ nisinnako santo tattha kālakato  ahaṃ   aptha            
 puññakammena saṃyutto tusitaṃ upapajj  ahaṃ  
 kalebaraṃ  me patitaṃ devaloke ramām  ahaṃ   aptha            
 chaḷāsītisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā  
 sāyapātaṃ  upaṭṭhanti bhisadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 manussayoniṃ āgantvā sukhito hom  ahan tadā  
 bhoge me ūnatā n  atthi bhisadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 anukampitattā  tena devadevena tādinā  
 sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā  n  atthi dāni punabbhavo  aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ bhikkham adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhisadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhisadāyako thero i  g  a ti  
 bhisadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       ñāṇatthavika   
 dakkhiṇe himavantassa sukato assamo mama  
 uttamatthaṃ gavesanto vasāmi pavane tadā   aptha           
 lābhālābhena santuṭṭho mūlena ca phalena ca  
 anomasanto cariyaṃ  vasāmi ekato ahaṃ   aptha           
 sumedho nāma sambuddho loke uppajji tāvade  
 catusaccaṃ pakāseti uddharanto mahājanaṃ   aptha           
 nāhaṃ suṇomi   sambuddhaṃ na pi me koci sāsati    
 aṭṭhavasse atikkante assosiṃ lokanāyakaṃ   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 aggidāruṃ nīharitvā  sammajjitvāna assamaṃ  
 khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna nikkhamiṃ  pavanā ahaṃ   aptha           
 ekarattiṃ vasanto haṃ gāmesu nigamesu ca  
 anupubbena candavatiṃ  tadā haṃ upasaṅkamiṃ   aptha           
 bhagavā ca tamhi samaye sumedho lokanāyako  
 uddharanto bahū satte deseti amataṃ padaṃ   aptha           
 janakāyam atikkamma vanditvā jinasāsanaṃ   
 ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā santhaviṃ  lokanāyakaṃ   aptha           
  tuvaṃ satthā ca ketu ca dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃ  
 parāyaṇo patiṭṭhā ca dīpo ca dīpaduttamo   aptha           
 nepuñño dassane vīro  tāresi janataṃ tuvaṃ  
 n  atth  añño tārako loke tav  uttaritaro mune   aptha            
 sakkā ha ve  kusaggena pametuṃ  sāgaruttamo  
 na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   aptha            
 tulamaṇḍale ṭhapetvāna   mahī   sakkā dharetave  
 na tveva tava paññāya pamāṇaṃ atthi cakkhumā   aptha            
 ākāso minituṃ   sakkā rajjuya aṅgulena pi  
 na tveva tava sabbaññū sīlaṃ sakkā pametave   aptha            
 mahāsamudde udakaṃ ākāso ca vasundharā  
 parimeyyāni etāni appameyyo   si cakkhumā     aptha            
 chahi gāthāhi sabbaññuṃ kittayitvā mahāyasaṃ  
 añjaliṃ paggahetvāna tuṇhī   aṭṭhās  ahaṃ tadā   aptha            
 yaṃ vadanti sumedho ti bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   aptha            
  yo me ñaṇaṃ pakittesi pasanno sehi pāṇihi    
 tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   aptha            
 sattasattatikappāni devaloke ramissati  
 sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati   aptha            
 anekasatakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti bhavissati  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha

      ñāṇatthavika     
 devabhūto manusso vā puññakammasamāhito  
 anūnamatasaṅkappo  tikkhapañño bhavissati  aptha            
 tiṃsakappasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo   
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha            
 agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajjissati kiñcano  
 jātiyā sattavassena arahattaṃ phusissati    aptha            
 yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato patto mhi sāsanaṃ  
 etth  antare na jānāmi cetanaṃ amanoramaṃ    aptha            
 saṃsaritvā bhave sabbe sampatt  anubhaviṃ  ahaṃ  
 bhoge me ūnatā n  atthi phalaṃ ñāṇassa thomane   aptha            
 tivaggī  nibbutā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  
 sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā n  atthi dāni punabbhavo   aptha            
 tiṃsakappasahassāni yaṃ ñāṇaṃ abhithom  ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phalaṃ ñāṇassa thomane   aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha

 ñāṇatthavikattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       candanamāliya   
 pañcakāmaguṇe hitvā piyarūpe manorame  
 asītikoṭiyo hitvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ   aptha           
 pabbajitvāna kāyena pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ   
 vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā nadīkūle vasām  ahaṃ   aptha           
 ekakammaṃ vihāraṃ taṃ buddhaseṭṭho upāgamī  
 nāhaṃ jānāmi buddho ti akāsiṃ paṭisantharaṃ    aptha           
 karitvā paṭisanthāraṃ nāmagottaṃ apucch  ahaṃ   
 devatā nu si gandhabbo uda  sakko purindado   aptha           
 ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto mahābrahmā idhāgato  
 virocesi  disā sabbā udayaṃ suriyo   yathā   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 sahassarāṇi cakkāni pāde dissanti mārisa  
 ko va tvaṃ kassa vā putto kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ   
 nāmagottaṃ pavedehi saṃsayaṃ apanehi me   aptha           
  n  amhi devo na gandhabbo n  amhi sakko purindado  
 brahmā bhāvo ca me n  atthi etesaṃ uttamo ahaṃ  aptha           
 atīto visayaṃ tesaṃ dālayiṃ kāmabandhanaṃ  
 sabbe kilese jhāpetvā patto sambodhim uttamaṃ    aptha           
 tassa vācaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ imaṃ  vacanam abraviṃ    
 yadi buddho   si sabbaññū nisīda tvaṃ mahāmune  
 tam ahaṃ pūjayissāmi dukkass  antakaro  tuvaṃ   aptha           
 pattharitvā jinaṃ cammaṃ  adāsiṃ  satthuno ahaṃ  
 nisīdi tattha bhagavā sīho va girigabbhare   aptha            
 khippaṃ pabbatam āruyha ambassa phalam aggahiṃ   
 sālakalyāṇikaṃ pupphaṃ candanañ ca mahārahaṃ   aptha            
 khippaṃ paggayha taṃ sabbaṃ upesiṃ  lokanāyakaṃ  
 phalaṃ buddhassa datvāna sālapupphaṃ apūjayiṃ   aptha            
 candanaṃ anulimpitvā avandi satthuno ahaṃ  
 pasannacitto sumano vipulāya ca pītiyā   aptha            
 ajinamhi nisīditvā sumedho lokanāyako  
 mama kammaṃ pakittesi hāsayanto  mamaṃ tadā   aptha            
  iminā phaladānena gandhamālehi cūbhayaṃ  
 pañcavīsakappasate  devaloke ramissati  
 anūnamanasaṅkappo vasavatti   bhavissati   aptha            
 chabbīsatikappasate manussattaṃ gamissati  
 bhavissati   cakkavattī cāturanto mahiddhiko   aptha            
 vebhāraṃ   nāma nagaraṃ  vissakammena   māpitaṃ   
 hessati sabbasovaṇṇaṃ nānāratanabhūsitaṃ   aptha            
 eten  eva upāyena saṃsarissati   yoniso  
 sabbattha sukhito hutvā devatte atha mānuse  
 pacchime bhave sampatte brahmabandhu bhavissati   aptha            
 agārā abhinikkhamma anāgārī bhavissati  
 aviññattipaccayo hutvā nibbāyissat  anāsavo    aptha

       puḷinuppādaka   
  pabbate himavantamhi devalo  nāma tāpaso  
 tattha me caṅkamo  āsi amānussikamāpito    aptha           
 jaṭābhārena bharito kamaṇḍaludharo tadā  
 uttamatthaṃ gavesanto pavanā abhinikkhamiṃ    aptha           
 cullāsītisahassāni  sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ  
 sakakammāni pasutā vasanti pavane tadā   aptha           
 assamā  abhinikkhamma akaṃ pulinacetiyaṃ   
 nānāpupphaṃ samānetvā taṃ cetiyam apūjayiṃ   aptha           
 tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā assamaṃ pavisām  ahaṃ  
 sabbe sissā samāgantvā  etam atthaṃ pucchiṃsu maṃ    aptha           
 puḷinena kato thūpo yaṃ tvaṃ  devam namassasi  
 mayaṃ pi ñā tum icchāma puṭṭho ācikkha ma  tuvaṃ   aptha           
 niddhiṭṭhā no mantapade  cakkhumanto mahāyasā  
 te kho ahaṃ namassāmi buddhaseṭṭhamahāyase   aptha           
 kīdisā te mahāvirā sabbaññū lokanāyakā  
 kathaṃ vaṇṇakathaṃ sīlā kīdisā te mahāyasā   aptha           
 battiṃsalakkhaṇā buddhā cattārīsaddijāpi   ca  
 nettā go pamukhā   tesaṃ jiñjukaphalasannibhā     aptha           
 gacchamānā ca te buddhā yugamattañ ca pekkhare  
 na tesaṃ jānu nadati sandhisaddo na suyyati     aptha            
 gacchamānā ca sugatā uddharantā va gacchare  
 paṭhamaṃ dakkhiṇaṃ pādaṃ  buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā   aptha            
 asambhītā ca te buddhā migarājā va kesarī  
 nev  ukkaṃsenti   attānaṃ no ca vambhenti   pāṇinaṃ     aptha            
 mānāvamānato muttā samā sabbesu pāṇisu    
 anattukkaṃsakā buddhā  buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā   aptha            
 uppajjantā ca sambuddhā ālokaṃ dassayanti te  
 chabbikāraṃ   pakampenti kevalaṃ vasudhaṃ imaṃ   aptha

      puḷinuppādaka     
 passanti nirayaṃ c  ete nibbāti nirayo tadā  
 pavassati mahāmegho  buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā   aptha            
 edisā te mahānāgā atulyā  ca  mahāyasā  
 vaṇṇato anatikkantā  appameyyā tathāgatā   aptha            
 anumodiṃsu me vākyaṃ sabbe sissā sagāravā  
 tathā va  paṭipajjiṃsu yathāsatti yathābalaṃ   aptha            
 paṭipūjenti pulinaṃ sakakammābhilāsino   
 saddahantā mamaṃ vākyaṃ buddhattaggatamānasā   aptha            
 tadā cavitvā tusitā devaputto mahāyaso  
 uppajji mātukucchismiṃ dasasahassī pakampatha   aptha            
 assamassāvidūramhi caṅkamamhi ṭhito ahaṃ  
 sabbe sissā samāgantvā āgacchuṃ  mama santikaṃ   aptha            
  usabho va mahī nadati migarājā va kuñjati   
 suṃsumāro va saddati  kiṃ vipāko bhavissati    aptha            
 yaṃ pakittemi  sambuddhaṃ sikatā thūpasantike  
 so dāni bhagavā satthā mātukucchim upāgami   aptha            
 tesaṃ dhammakathaṃ katvā kittayitvā mahāmuniṃ  
 uyyojetvā sake sisse pallaṅkaṃ ābhujiṃ ahaṃ   aptha            
 balañ ca vata me khīṇaṃ vyādhito paramen  ahaṃ  
 buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ  aptha            
 sabbe sissā samāgantvā akaṃsu citakaṃ tadā  
 kalebarañ ca me gayha citakaṃ abhiropayuṃ   aptha            
 citakaṃ parivāretvā sīse katvāna añjaliṃ  
 sokasallaparetā te vikkandiṃsu samāgatā   aptha            
 tesaṃ lālappamānānaṃ agamāsiṃ   citan tadā  
 ahaṃ ācariyo tuyhaṃ   mā socittha   sumedhasā   aptha            
 sadatthe vāyameyyātha rattindivam atanditā  
 mā vo   pamattā ahuttha khaṇo vo   paṭipādito   aptha            
 sake sisse nusāsitvā   devalokaṃ punāgamiṃ    
 aṭṭhārasāhaṃ kappāni devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ   aptha

       taraṇiya   
 atthadassī tu bhagavā sayambhū lokanāyako  
 cinatā  nadiyā tīre upāgacchi  tathāgato   aptha           
 udakā abhinikkhamma kacchapo vārigocaro  
 buddhaṃ taritukāmo haṃ upesiṃ  lokanāyakaṃ  aptha           
 abhirūhatu maṃ buddho atthadassī mahāmuni  
 ahaṃ taṃ tārayissāmi dukkhass  antakaro  tuvaṃ   aptha           
 mama saṃkappam aññāya atthadassī mahāyaso  
 ārohitvāna  me piṭṭhiṃ aṭṭhāsi   lokanāyako   aptha           
 yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato patto smi viññutaṃ  
 sukhaṃ me tādisaṃ n  atthi yathā pādatale   muni     aptha           
 uttaritvāna sambuddho atthadassī mahāyaso  
 nadī  tīramhi ṭhatvāna imā gāthā abhā satha   aptha

      taraṇiya     
 yāvatā vattate cittaṃ  kaṅkhāsotaṃ tarām  ahaṃ  
 ayaṃ hi  kacchapo rājā tāreti mama puññavā   aptha           
 iminā buddhataraṇena  mettacittavatāya  ca  
 aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissati   aptha           
  devalokā idhāgantvā  sukkamūlena codito  
 ekāsane nisīditvā kaṅkhāsotaṃ tarissati   aptha           
 yathāpi bhaddake khette bījaṃ appam pi ropitaṃ  
 sammādhāre pavassante phalaṃ toseti kassake  aptha            
 tath ev  idaṃ buddhakhettaṃ sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ  
 sammādhāre pavecchante phalam maṃ tosayissati   aptha            
 padhānaṃ pahitatto mhi upasanto nirūpadhī  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha            
 aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ kammam akariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi taraṇāya idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       dhammaruci   
 yadā dipaṅkaro buddho sumedhaṃ vyākarī  jino   
  aparimeyye ito kappe ayaṃ buddho bhavissati   aptha           
 imassa janikā  mātā māyā nāma bhavissati  
 pitā suddhodano nāma  ayaṃ hessati gotamo   aptha           
 padhānaṃ padahitvāna katvā dukkarakārikaṃ  
 assatthamūle sambuddho bujjhissati mahāyaso   aptha           
 upatisso kolito ca aggā hessanti sāvakā  
 ānando nāma nāmena upaṭṭhissat  imaṃ jinaṃ   aptha           
 khemā uppalavaṇṇā ca aggā hessanti sāvikā  
 citto ālavako c  eva aggā hessant  upāsakā  aptha           
 khujjuttarā nandamātā aggā hessant  upāsikā  
 bodhi imassa vīrassa assattho ti pavuccati    aptha

     therāpadāna 
 idaṃ sutvāna vacanaṃ asamassa  mahesino  
 āmoditā naramarū namassanti katañjalī   aptha           
 tadāhaṃ mānavo āsiṃ megho nāma susikkhito  
 sutvā vyākaraṇaṃ seṭṭhaṃ sumedhassa mahāmune   aptha           
 saṃvissattho bhavitvāna sumedhe karuṇāsaye  
 pabbajantañ ca taṃ vīraṃ sah  eva  anupabbajiṃ   aptha           
 saṃvuto pātimokkhasmiṃ indriyesu ca pañcasu  
 suddhājivo sato vīro jinasāsanakārako   aptha            
 evaṃ viharamāno haṃ pāpamittena kenaci  
 niyojito anācāre sumaggā paridhaṃsito   aptha            
 vitakkavasago  hutvā sāsanato apakkamiṃ   
 pacchā tena kumittena payutto  mātughātanaṃ  aptha            
 akarim  anantariyañ  ca ghātayiṃ duṭṭhamānaso  
 tato cuto mahāvīciṃ upapanno sudāruṇaṃ   aptha            
 vinipātagato santo saṃsariṃ dukkhito ciraṃ  
 na puno addasaṃ vīraṃ  sumedhaṃ narapuṅgavaṃ   aptha            
 asmiṃ kappe samuddamhi maccho āsiṃ timiṅgalo    
 disvāhaṃ sāgare nāvaṃ gocarattham upāgamiṃ   aptha            
 disvā maṃ vānijā bhītā buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anussaruṃ  
 gotamo ti mahāghosaṃ sutvā tehi udīritaṃ  aptha            
 pubbasaññaṃ saritvāna tato kālakato   ahaṃ   
 sāvatthiyaṃ kule ucce   jāto brāhmaṇajātiyā    aptha            
 āsiṃ dhammarucī nāma sabbapāpajigucchako     
 disvāhaṃ lokapajjotaṃ jātiyā sattavassiko   aptha            
 mahā jetavanaṃ gantvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
 upemi buddhaṃ tikkhattuṃ rattiyā divasassa ca  aptha            
 disvā disvā muni   āha ciraṃ dhammarucīti maṃ  
 tato haṃ avacaṃ buddhaṃ pubbakammapabhāvitaṃ     aptha            
 suciraṃ satapuññalakkhaṇaṃ   patipubbe na visuddhapaccayaṃ

       sālamaṇḍapiya   
 ajjhogahetvā sālavanaṃ sukato assamo mama  
 sālapupphehi sañchanno vasāmi pavane tadā   aptha           
 piyadassī ca bhagavā sayambhū aggapuggalo  
 vivekakāmo sambuddho sālavanam upāgami   aptha           
 assamā abhinikkhamma pavanaṃ agamās  ahaṃ  
 mūlaphalaṃ gavesanto  āhiṇḍāmi vane tadā   aptha           
 tatthā ddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ piyadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ  
 sunisinnaṃ samāpannaṃ virocantaṃ mahāvane   aptha           
 catudaṇḍe ṭhapetvāna buddhassa uparī ahaṃ  
 maṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā sālap upphehi chādayiṃ   aptha           
 sattā haṃ dhārayitvāna maṇḍapaṃ sālachāditaṃ  
 tattha  cittaṃ pasādetvā buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandi haṃ   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 bhagavā tamhi samaye vuṭṭhahitvā samādhino   
 yugamattaṃ pekkhamāno nisīdi purisuttamo   aptha           
 sāvako varuṇo nāma piyadassissa satthuno  
 vasīsatasahassehi upāgacchi  vināyakaṃ   aptha           
 piyadassī tu  bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  
 bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā sitaṃ pātukarī  jino   aptha           
 anuruddho upaṭṭhāko piyadassissa satthuno  
 ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā apucchittha mahāmuniṃ   aptha            
  ko nu kho bhagavā hetu sitakammassa  satthuno  
 kāraṇe vijjamānamhi satthā pātukaresi  taṃ    aptha            
 sattāhaṃ pupphachadanaṃ yo me dhāresi māṇavo  
 tassa kammaṃ saritvāna sitaṃ pātukariṃ ahaṃ   aptha            
 okāsāhaṃ na passāmi yan taṃ puññaṃ vipaccati   
 devaloke manusse vā okāso ca na sammati   aptha            
 devaloke vasantassa puññakammasamaṅgino  
 yāvatā parisā tassa sālacchannā bhavissati   aptha            
 tattha dibbehi naccehi gītehi vāditehi ca  
 ramissati tadā santo puññakammasamāhito   aptha            
 yāvatā parisā tassa gandhagandhī bhavissati  
 sālassa pupphavasso ca pavassissati tāvade   aptha            
 tato cuto yaṃ  manujo mānusaṃ agamissati  
 idhāpi sālacchadanaṃ sabbakālaṃ dhariyyati   aptha            
 idha naccañ ca gītañ ca samatālasamāhitaṃ  
 parivāressant  imaṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ  aptha            
 uggacchante ca suriye sālavassaṃ pavassati  
 puññakammena sanyuttaṃ vassate sabbakālikaṃ   aptha            
 aṭṭhārase kappasate okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha            
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat  anāsavo   aptha            
 dhammaṃ abhisamentassa sālacchadanaṃ bhavissati  
 citake jhāyamānassa chadanaṃ tattha hessati  aptha            
 vipākaṃ kittayitvāna piyadassī mahāmuni  
 parisāya dhammaṃ desesi   tappento dhammavuṭṭhiyā   aptha

       udakadāyaka   
 padumuttara buddhassa bhikkhusaṅghe anuttare  
 pasannacitto sumano pānīyaghaṭam apūrayiṃ   aptha           
 pabbatagge dumagge vā ākāse vātha bhūmiyaṃ  
 yadā pānīyam icchāmi khippaṃ nibbattate mama   aptha           
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ dānam adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi udakadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakadāyako thero i  g  a ti  
 udakadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       puḷinathūpiya   
 himavantass  avidūre samaṅgo  nāma pabbato  
 assamo sukato mayhaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā   aptha           
 nārado nāma nāmena jaṭilo uggatāpano  
 catuddasaṃ sahassānaṃ  sissā paricaranti maṃ   aptha           
 paṭisallīnako santo evaṃ cintes  ahaṃ tadā   
 sabbajano maṃ pūjeti  nāhaṃ pūjemi kañcinaṃ   aptha           
 na me ovādako atthi vattā koci  na vijjati  
 anācariyupajjhāyo vane vāsaṃ upem  ahaṃ   aptha           
 upāsamāno  yam ahaṃ garucittaṃ upaṭṭhahe   
 so me ācariyo n  atthi vanavāso niratthako   aptha           
 āyāgam me  gavesissaṃ garubhāvaniyaṃ  tatha   
 sāvassayo vasissāmi na koci garahissati   aptha           
 uttānakūlā nadikā supatitthā manoramā  
 susuddhapuḷinākiṇṇā avidūre mam  assamaṃ   aptha           
 nadī amarikaṃ   nāma upagantvā   ahaṃ tadā  
 saṃvaḍḍhayitvā pulinaṃ akaṃ pulinacetiyaṃ   aptha

 ye te ahesuṃ sambuddhā bhavantakaraṇā munī  
 tesaṃ etādiso thūpo taṃ nimittaṃ karom  ahaṃ   aptha           
 karitvā puline thūpaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃ  
 sovaṇṇakiṅkhanipupphānaṃ sahasse tīṇi pūjayiṃ   aptha            
 sāya pātaṃ  namassāmi vittijāto katañjalī  
 sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ vandiṃ  pulinacetiyaṃ   aptha            
 yadā kilesā jhāyanti vitakkā gehanissitā  
 sarāmi sukataṃ  thūpaṃ paccavekkhāmi tāvade   aptha            
 upanissāya viharam  satthavāhaṃ vināyakaṃ  
 kilese saṃvaseyyāsi na yuttaṃ tava  marisa    aptha            
 saha  āvajjite thūpe gāravaṃ hoti me tadā  
 kuvitakkaṃ  vinodemi nāgo tuttaddito  yathā   aptha            
 evaṃ viharamānaṃ maṃ maccurājā bhimaddatha  
 tattha kālakato santo brahmalokaṃ agañch   ahaṃ   aptha            
 yavatāyuṃ vasitvāna tidase upapajj  ahaṃ  
 asītikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ   aptha            
 satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñ ca cakkavatti ahos  ahaṃ  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha            
 tesaṃ kiṅkhanipupphānaṃ vipākaṃ anubhom  ahaṃ  
 dvāvīsatisahassāni parivārenti maṃ bhave   aptha            
 thūpassa pariciṇṇattā rajojallaṃ na limpati  
 gatte sedā na muccanti sappabhāso   bhavām  ahaṃ   aptha            
 aho me sukato thūpo sudiṭṭhā marikā   nadī  
 thūpaṃ katvāna   puline patto mhi acalaṃ padaṃ   aptha            
 kusalaṃ kattukāmena jantunā pāragāminā    
 n  atthi khettaṃ akhettaṃ vā paṭipatti va sārikā     aptha            
 yathāpi balavā poso aṇṇavaṃ taritussahe    
 parittaṃ kaṭṭham ādāya pakkhandeyya mahāsaraṃ  aptha            
 imāhaṃ kaṭṭhaṃ   nissāya tarissāmi mahodadhiṃ  
 ussāhena viriyena tareyya udadhiṃ naro   aptha

      puḷinathūpiya     
 tath  eva me kataṃ kammaṃ parittaṃ thokakañcanaṃ  
 kataṃ kammaṃ upanissāya  saṃsāraṃ  samatikkamiṃ   aptha            
 pacchime bhave sampatte sukkamūlena codito  
 sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto mahāsāle su aḍḍhake   aptha            
 saddhā mātāpitā mayhaṃ buddhassa saraṇaṃ gatā  
 ubho diṭṭhapadā ete anuvattanti sāsanaṃ   aptha            
 bodhipapaṭikaṃ  gayha soṇṇathūpaṃ  akārayuṃ  
 sāyapātaṃ  namassanti sakyaputtassa sammukhā   aptha            
 uposathamhi divase soṇṇathūpaṃ  vinīharuṃ   
 buddhassa vaṇṇaṃ kittentā tiyāmaṃ vītināmayuṃ   aptha            
 sahā  disvāna haṃ  thūpaṃ sariṃ pulinacetiyaṃ  
 ekāsane nisīditvā arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   aptha            
 gavesamāno   taṃ vīraṃ dhammasenāpat  addasaṃ    
 agārā nikkhamitvāna pabbajiṃ tassa santike   aptha            
 jātiyā sattavassena arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ  
 upasampādayī   buddho guṇaṃ aññāya cakkhumā   aptha            
 dāraken  eva santema kiriyaṃ   niṭṭhitaṃ mayā  
  kata m me karaṇīy   ajja sakyaputtassa sāsane   aptha            
 sabbaverabhayātīto sabbasaṅgātigo isi  
 sāvako te mahāvīra soṇṇathūpass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pulinathūpiyo thero i  g  a ti  
 puḷinathūpiyattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

       naḷakuṭikadāyaka   
 himavantass  avidūre bhāriko  nāma pabbato  
 sayambhū nārado nāma rukkhamūle vasī  tadā   aptha           
 naḷāgāraṃ karitvāna tiṇena chādayiṃ ahaṃ  
 caṅkamaṃ  sodhayitvāna sayambhussa adās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agañch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ  naḷakuṭikāya nimmitaṃ  
 saṭṭhiyojanam ubbiddhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ   aptha           
 catuddasesu kappesu devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ  
 ekasattatikkhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ   aptha           
 catuttiṃsakkhattuñ  c  eva cakkavatti ahos  ahaṃ  
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha           
 dhammapāsādam āruyha sabbāgāravarūpamaṃ   
 yadicchakāhaṃ vihareyy  sakyaputtassa sāsane   aptha           
 ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammam akariṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi naḷakuṭikāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā naḷakuṭikadāyako thero i  g  a ti  
 naḷakuṭikadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       piyālaphaladāyaka   
 migaluddo pure āsiṃ vīcine  vicaran tadā  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ   aptha           
 piyālaphalam ādāya buddhaseṭṭhass  adās  ahaṃ  
 puññakkhettassa vīrassa pasanno sehi pāṇihi    aptha           
 ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

 uddānaṃ  
 kiṅkhani paṃsukūlañ ca koraṇḍapupphi kiṃsukhaṃ 
 upaḍḍhadussī ghatado udakaṃ thūpakārako  
 naḷāgārī ca navamo piyālaphaladāyako 
 sataṃ ekañ ca gāthānaṃ navakañ ca taduttariṃ   
 kiṅkhanipupphiyavaggo paññāso   
 atha vagguddānaṃ  
 metteyya bhaddālivaggo  sakiṃsammajjako pi ca  
 eko vibheṭakī vaggo jagati sālapupphiyo

 asīti dve ca gāthāyo catuddasasatāni ca

       tīṇikaṇikārapupphiya   
 sumedho nāma sambuddho dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo   
 vivekakāmo sambuddho himavantaṃ upāgami   aptha           
 ajjhogahetvā himavaṃ  aggo kāruṇiko muni  
 pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvāna   nisīdi purisuttamo   aptha           
 vijjādharo tadā āsiṃ antalikkhacaro   ahaṃ  
 tisūlaṃ   sukataṃ gayha gacchāmi ambare tadā   aptha           
 pabbatagge yathā acci   puññamāse va candimā  
 vane   obhāsate buddho sālarājā va phullito   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 vanaggā  nikkhamitvāna buddharaṃs  ābhidhāvare  
 nalaggivaṇṇasaṅkāsā disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ   aptha           
 vicinaṃ addasaṃ pupphaṃ  kaṇikāraṃ devagandhikaṃ  
 tīṇipupphāni ādāya buddhaseṭṭhaṃ apūjayiṃ   aptha           
 buddhassa ānubhāvena tīṇi pupphāni me tadā  
 uddhavaṇṭā  adhopattā chāyaṃ kubbanti satthuno   aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ  kaṇikārīti ñāyati  
 saṭṭhiyojanam ubbiddhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ    aptha           
 sahassakaṇḍo satageṇḍu  dhajālu haritāmayo  
 satasahassa niyyūhā vyamhe  pātubhaviṃsu me   aptha            
 sovaṇṇamayā maṇimayā  lohitaṅkamayā pi ca  
 phalikāpi ca pallaṅkā yenicchakā yadicchakā   aptha            
 ma hārahañ ca sayanaṃ tū likāvikatīyutaṃ   
 uddhalomika ekantaṃ   bimbohanasamāyutaṃ   aptha            
 bhavanā nikkhamitvāna caranto devacārikaṃ  
 yadā icchāmi gamanaṃ devasaṅghapurakkhato   aptha            
 pupphassa heṭṭhā tiṭṭhāmi uparicchadanaṃ mama    
 samantā yojanasataṃ kanikārehi   chāditaṃ   aptha            
 saṭṭhituriyasahassāni sāyaṃ pātaṃ   upaṭṭhahuṃ  
 parivārenti   maṃ niccaṃ rattindivaṃ atanditā   aptha            
 tattha naccehi gītehi  tā lehi vāditehi ca  
 ramāmi khiḍḍāratiyā modāmi kāmakāmi haṃ   aptha            
 tattha bhutvā ca pitvā ca modāmi tidase tadā  
 nārīgaṇehi sahito modāmi vyamha m uttame     aptha            
 satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñ ca cakkavatti ahos  ahaṃ   
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   aptha            
 bhavābhave saṃsaranto mahābhoge   labhām  ahaṃ   
 bhoge me ūnatā n  atthi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

      tīṇikaṇikārapupphiya     
 duve bhave saṃsarāmi devatte atha mānuse  
 aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye cāpi brāhmaṇe  
 nīce kule na jānāmi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ sivikaṃ sandamānikaṃ   
 labhāmi sabbam ev  etaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 dāsīgaṇaṃ dāsagaṇaṃ nāriyo ca alaṅkatā  
 labhāmi sabbam ev  etaṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 koseyyakambalīyāni  khomakappāsikāni ca  
 labhāmi sabbam ev  etaṃ       pe       pe        aptha            
 navavatthaṃ navaphalaṃ nav agga rasa bhojanaṃ  
 labhāmi       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 ime khāda ime bhuñja imamhi sayane saya  
 labhāmi       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sabbattha pūjito homi yaso accuggato  mama  
 mahāpakkho  sadā homi abhejjapariso tadā   
 ñātīnaṃ  uttamo homi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 sītaṃ uṇhaṃ na jānāmi pariḷāho na vijjati  
 atho cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ hadaye me na vijjati   aptha            
 suvaṇṇavaṇṇo hutvāna saṃsarāmi bhavābhave  
 duvaṇṇikaṃ  na jānāmi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito  
 savatthiyaṃ pure jāto mahāsāle su aḍḍhake   aptha            
 pañcakāmaguṇe hitvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  
 jātiyā  sattavasso va  arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   aptha            
 upasampādayī  buddho guṇaṃ aññāya cakkhumā  
 taruṇo   pūjanīyo haṃ buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 dibbaṃ cakkhuṃ visuddham   me samādhikusalo ahaṃ  
 abhiññāpāramippatto buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 paṭisambhidā anuppatto iddhipādesu kovido  
 saddhamme   pāramippatto buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

       ekapattadāyaka   
 nagare haṃsavatiyā kumbhakāro ahos  ahaṃ  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ oghatiṇṇam anāsavaṃ   aptha           
 sukataṃ mattikāpattaṃ buddhaseṭṭhass  adās  ahaṃ  
 pattaṃ datvā bhagavato ujubhūtassa tādino  aptha           
 bhave nibbattamāno haṃ sovaṇṇathāle labhām  ahaṃ  
 rūpimaye ca sovaṇṇe taṭṭake  ca maṇīmaye  aptha           
 pātiyo  paribhuñjāmi puññakammass  idaṃ phalaṃ  
 yasānañ ca dhanānañ ca pattabhūto ca hom  ahaṃ   aptha           
 yathāpi bhaddake khette bījam appam pi ropitaṃ   
 sammādhāre pavecchante  phalaṃ  toseti kassakaṃ   aptha           
 tath ev  imaṃ  pattadānaṃ buddhakhettamhi ropitaṃ  
 pītidhāre pavassante phalaṃ  me tosayissati   aptha           
 yāvatā khettā vijjanti saṅghāpi ca gaṇāpi ca  
 buddhakhettasamo n  atthi sukhadānatthā  pāṇinaṃ   aptha           
 namo te purisājañña  namo te purisuttamo   
 ekapattaṃ  daditvāna patto mhi acalaṃ padaṃ   aptha           
 ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pattam adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekapattadāyako thero i  g  a ti  
 ekapattadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

       ajelaphaladāyaka

       sabbaphaladāyaka   
 varuṇo  nāma nāmena brāhmaṇo mantapāragū  
 chaḍḍetvā dasaputtāni vanam ajjhogahiṃ tadā   aptha           
 assamaṃ sukataṃ katvā  suvibhattaṃ monoramaṃ  
 paṇṇa sālaṃ karitvāna vasāmi pavane ahaṃ   aptha           
 padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  
 mam uddharitukāmo so agacchi  mam assamaṃ   aptha           
 yāvatā vanasaṇḍasmiṃ obhāso vipulo ahu  
 buddhas sa ānubhāvena pajjali  pavanaṃ tadā   aptha           
 disvān  ahaṃ  pāṭihīraṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa tadino  
 pattapuṭaṃ  gahetvāna phalena pūrayiṃ ahaṃ   aptha           
 upagantvāna taṃ buddhaṃ sākhārikaṃ  adās  ahaṃ  
 anukampāya me buddho imaṃ vacanam abravī    aptha           
 khāribhāraṃ  gahetvāna pacchato ehi  me tuvaṃ  
 paribhutte   ca   saṅghamhi puññaṃ taṃ va   bhavissati   aptha           
 puṭakantaṃ   gahetvāna bhikkhusaṅghass  adās ahaṃ  
 tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā tusitaṃ upapajj  ahaṃ   aptha           
 tattha naccehi gītehi dibbehi vāditehi ca    
 puññakammena saṃyutto anubhomi sadā ahaṃ   aptha           
 yaṃ yaṃ yon  upapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  
 bhoge me ūnatā n  atthi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 yāvatā caturo   dīpā sasamuddā sapabbatā  
 phalaṃ buddhassa datvāna issaraṃ kārayām  ahaṃ   aptha            
 yāvatā ye pakkhigaṇā ākāse uppatanti te  
 te pi maṃ vasam anventi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 yāvatā vanasaṇḍamhi yakkhā bhutā ca rakkhasā  
 kumbhaṇḍā garulā cāpi pāricariyaṃ   upenti me   aptha

      sabbaphaladāyaka     
 kumbhasoṇā madhukarā ḍaṃsā ca makasā ubho  
 te pi maṃ vasam anventi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 supaṇṇā nāma sakuṇā pakkhijātā mahābalā  
 te pi maṃ saraṇaṃ yanti phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 ye pi dīghāyukā nāgā iddhimanto mahāyasā  
 te pi maṃ vasam anventi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 sīhā vyagghā ca dīpī ca acchakokataracchayo   
 te pi maṃ vasam anventi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 osadhī tiṇa vāsā  ca ye ca ākāsavāsino  
 sabbe maṃ saraṇaṃ yanti phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 sududdasaṃ sunipuṇaṃ gambhīraṃ suppakāsitaṃ  
 passitvāna  viharāmi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 vimokhe aṭṭha passitvā viharāmi anāsavo  
 ātāpī  nipako cāhaṃ phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ  aptha            
 ye phalaṭṭhā buddhaputtā khīṇadosā mahāyasā  
 aham aññataro tesaṃ phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 abhiññāpāramiṃ gantvā sukkamūlena codito  
 sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   aptha            
 tevijjā iddhippattā  ca buddhaputtā mahāyasā  
 dibbasotaṃ samāpannā tesaṃ aññataro ahaṃ   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sabbaphaladāyako thero i  g  a ti  
 sabbaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ

       tiṇamuṭṭhidāyaka   
 himavantass  avidūre lambako nāma pabbato  
 tatth  opatisso sambuddho abbhokāsamhi caṅkami   aptha           
 migaluddo tadā  āsiṃ araññe kānane  ahaṃ  
 disvān  ahaṃ devadevaṃ tiṇamuṭṭhim adās  ahaṃ   aptha           
 nisīdanatthaṃ buddhasa datvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  
 sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho   aptha           
 aciragatamattassa migarājā aheṭhayi  
 sīhena patito santo tattha kālakato ahaṃ   aptha           
 āsanne me kataṃ kammaṃ buddhaseṭṭhe anāsave  
 sumutto  saravego ca  devalokaṃ agacch   ahaṃ   aptha           
 yūpo   tatthaṃ subho   āsi puññakammābhinimmito  
 sahassakaṇḍo satageṇḍu   dhajālu haritāmayo   aptha           
 pabhā niddhāvaṭe tassa sataraṃsīva uggato  
 ākiṇṇo devakaññābhi āmodiṃ kāmakāmi haṃ   aptha

 nāgare bandhumatiyā rājuyyāne vasām  ahaṃ  
 dhammavādī  tadā āsiṃ kamaṇḍaludharo ahaṃ   aptha           
 addasaṃ virajaṃ  buddhaṃ sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ  
 padhānapahitattan taṃ jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ vasiṃ    aptha           
 sabbakāmasamiddhiñ ca oghatiṇṇam anāsavaṃ  
 disvā pasanno sumano abbhañjanam  adās ahaṃ  aptha           
 ekanavute ito kappe yam abbhañjanam  adās ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi abbhañjanass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā abbhañjanadāyako thero i  g  a ti  
 abbhañjanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       pūpapavadāyaka   
 divāvihārā nikkhanto vipassī lokanāyako  
 lahupūpapavaṃ  datvā kappaṃ saggamhi mod  ahaṃ   aptha           
 ekanavute ito kappe pūpapavaṃ  adās  ahaṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pūpapavass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pūpapavadāyako thero i  g  a ti  
 pūpapavadāyakattherassa  apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       daṇḍadāyaka   
 kānanaṃ vanam ogayha veluṃ chetvān  ahaṃ tadā  
 ālambanaṃ gahetvāna saṅghassa adadiṃ ahaṃ   aptha           
 tena cittappasādena subbate  abhivādiya  
 ālambadaṇḍaṃ datvāna pakkāmi uttarāmukho   aptha

      girinelapūjaka     
 catunavute ito kappe yaṃ daṇḍaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi daṇḍadānass  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha

 daṇḍadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       girinelapūjaka   
 migaluddo pure āsiṃ vicine  vicaraṃ ahaṃ  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ   aptha           
 tasmiṃ mahākāruṇike  sabbasattahite rate  
 pasannacitto sumano nelapupphaṃ  apūjayiṃ   aptha           
 ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ puppham abhipūjayiṃ  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā girinelapūjako thero i  g  a ti  
 girinelapūjakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       bodhisammajjaka   
 ahaṃ pure bodhipattaṃ ujjhitaṃ  cetiyaṅgane  
 taṃ gahetvāna chaḍḍesiṃ alabhiṃ vīsatī gaṇe  aptha           
 tassa kammassa tejena saṃsaranto bhavābhave  
 duve bhave saṃsarāmi devattaṃ cāpi mānusaṃ   aptha           
 devalokā cavitvāna āgantvā mānusaṃ bhavaṃ  
 duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye cāpi brāhmaṇe   aptha           
 aṅgapaccaṅgasampanno ārohapariṇāhavā  
 abhirūpo rucī  homi sampuṇṇaṅgo  anūnako   aptha           
 devaloke manusse vā jāto vā yattha katthaci  
 bhave suvaṇṇavaṇṇo  va uttattakanakūpamo   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 mudukā maddavā niddhā  sukhumā sukumārakā   
 chavi me sabbadā hoti bodhipatte su chaḍḍite   aptha           
 yato kuto ca  gatisu sarīre samudāgate   
 na lippati  rajojallaṃ vipāko pattachaḍḍite   aptha           
 uṇhe vātātape tassa aggitāpena vā puna  
 gatte sedā na muccanti vipāko pattachaḍḍite   aptha           
 kuṭṭhaṃ gaṇḍo kilāso ca tilakā piḷakā tathā  
 na honti kāye dadduñ  ca vipāko pattachaḍḍite   aptha           
 aparam pi gaṇaṃ tassa nibbattati  bhavābhave  
 rogā na honti kāyasmiṃ vipāko pattachaḍḍite   aptha            
 aparam pi guṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave  
 na hoti cittajā pīḷā vipāko pattachaḍḍite   aptha            
 aparam pi guṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave  
 āmittā na bhavant  assa vipāko pattachaḍḍite   aptha            
 aparam pi gaṇaṃ tassa nibbattati bhavābhave  
 anūnabhogo bhavati vipāko pattachaḍḍite   aptha            
 aparam pi gunaṃ       pe       pe       pe        
 aggi rajjūhi  corehi na hoti udake bhayaṃ   aptha            
 aparam pi       pe       pe       pe        
 dāsī dāsā anucarā honti cittānuvattakā   aptha            
 yamhi āyuppamānamhi jāyate  mānuse bhave  
 tato na hāyate āyu tiṭṭhate yāvatāyukaṃ   aptha            
 abbhantarā bahicarā   negamā ca saraṭṭhakā  
 anuyuttā honti sabbe pi vuṭṭhikāmā sukhicchakā     aptha            
 bhogavā yasavā homi sirimā ñātipakkhavā  
 apetabhayasantāso bhavesaṃ sabbato   bhave   aptha            
 devā manussā asurā gandhabbā yakkha rakkhasā  
 sabbe te parirakkhanti bhave saṃsarato sadā     aptha            
 devaloke manusse vā anubhotvā ubho yase  
 avasāne   ca nibbānaṃ sivaṃ patto anuttaraṃ   aptha

      āmaṇḍaphaladāyaka     
 magge phale āgame  ca jhānābhiññāguṇesu ca  
 aññesaṃ adhiko hutvā nibbāyāmi anāsavo   aptha            
 pure haṃ bodhiyā pattaṃ chaḍḍetvā haṭṭhamānaso  
 imehi vīsataṅgehi samaṅgī  homi sabbadā   aptha

       āmaṇḍaphaladāyaka   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  
 vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā caṅkamī  lokanāyako  aptha           
 khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna āharanto  phalaṃ tadā  
 addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ caṅkamantaṃ mahāmuniṃ   aptha           
 pasannacitto sumano sire katvāna añjaliṃ  
 sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā āmaṇḍam adadaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā  
 duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi āmaṇḍassa idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha           
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha           
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āmaṇḍaphaladāyako th  i  g  a ti  
 āmaṇḍaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       sugandha   
 imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso  
 kassapo nama nāmena uppajji vadataṃ varo   aptha           
 anuvyañjanasampanno dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo   
 byāmappabhāparivuto  raṃsijālasamosaṭo   aptha           
 assāsetā  yathā cando suriyo va pabhaṅkaro  
 nibbāpetā yathā megho sāgaro va gaṇākaro    aptha

     therāpadāna 
 dharanī r iva sīlena himavā va samādhinā  
 ākāso viya paññāya asaṅgo  anilo yathā   aptha           
 sa kadāci mahāviro parisāsu visārado  
 saccāni sampakāseti uddharanto mahājanaṃ   aptha           
 tadā hi bārāṇasiyam seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso  
 ās  ahaṃ dhanadhaññassa pahūtassa pahū tadā   aptha           
 jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ migadāyam upecc  ahaṃ   
 addasaṃ tādisaṃ buddhaṃ desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ   aptha           
 vissaṭṭhakantavacanaṃ karavīkasamassaraṃ  
 haṃsadundubhi nigghosaṃ  viññāpentaṃ mahājanaṃ  aptha           
 disvā devātidevan taṃ sutvā ca madhuraṃ giraṃ  
 pahāy  ānappake bhoge pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ   aptha           
 evaṃ pabbajito cāhaṃ nacirena bahussuto  
 ahosiṃ  dhammakathiko vicittapaṭibhānavā   aptha            
 mahāparisamajjhe haṃ haṭṭhacitto punappunaṃ  
 vaṇṇayiṃ  hemavaṇṇassa vaṇṇaṃ vaṇṇavisārado    aptha            
 esa khīṇāsavo buddho anīgho chinnasaṃsayo   
 sabbakammakkhayaṃ patto vimutto satisaṅkhaye    aptha            
 esa so bhagavā buddho esa sīho anuttaro  
 sadevakassa lokassa brahmacakkappavattako   aptha            
 danto dametā santo ca sametā nibbuto isi  
 nibbāpetā ca assattho assāsetā mahājanaṃ     aptha            
 vīro suro ca dhīro ca pañño kāruṇiko   vasī    
 vijitāvī ca sa jino apagabbho   anālayo   aptha            
 anejo acalo dhīmā amoho asamo muni  
 dhorayho usabho nāgo sīho sakko gurūsu pi    aptha            
 virāgo vimalo brahmā vādisuro   raṇañjaho    
 akhilo ca visallo   ca asamo payato   suci     aptha

      sugandha     
 brāhmaṇo samaṇo  nātho bhisakko sallakattako  
 yodho buddho suto sūto  acalo mudito sito    aptha            
 tātā tantā ca hantā  ca kattā netā pakāsitā  
 sampahaṃsitā bhottā  ca chettā sotā  pasaṃsitā  aptha            
 akhilo ca visālo ca anīgho  akathaṅkathī   
 anejo virajo khattā  gandhā mettā pakāsitā     aptha            
 tāretā atha tāretā   kāretā sampadāletā    
 pāpetā sahitā hantā hantā tātāpi tāpaso     aptha            
 samacitto samasamo asahāyo dayāyaso  
 accherasanto   akuho   katāvīisi sattamo   aptha            
 nittiṇṇakaṅkho nimmāno appameyyo anūpamo  
 sabbavākyapathātīto   saccaneyyantago jino     aptha            
 sattasāravare   tasmiṃ pasādo   amatāvaho  
 tasmā buddhe ca dhamme ca saṅghe saddhā   mahiddhikā   aptha            
 guṇehi evamādīhi tilokasaraṇuttamaṃ  
 vaṇṇento parisāmajjhe akaṃ dhammakathaṃ ahaṃ   aptha            
 tato cuto haṃ tusite anubhotvā mahāsukhaṃ  
 tato cuto manussesu jāto homi sugandhiko   aptha            
 nissāso   mukhagandho   ca dehagandho tath  eva me  
 sedagandho   ca satatam sabbagandho ti seti me   aptha            
 mukhagandho   sadā mayhaṃ padumuppalacampake    
 atisanto sadā vāti   sarīro ca tath  eva me   aptha            
 guṇatthavassapupphan   taṃ phalan tu param   abbhutaṃ  
 ekaggamanasā sabbe vaṇṇayissaṃ suṇotha   me   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 guṇaṃ buddhassa vatvāna hitāya janasandhisu   
 sukhito homi sabbattha rasaddhovisamāyuto    aptha            
 yasassī sukhito kanto  jutimā piyadassano   
 vattā aparibhūto ca niddoso paññavā tathā   aptha            
 khīṇ  ev  āyu pi  nibbānaṃ sulabhaṃ buddhabhattino   
 tesaṃ hetuṃ pavakkhāmi taṃ suṇotha yathātathaṃ   aptha            
 santaṃ yasaṃ bhagavato vidhinā  abhivādayaṃ   
 yattha tatth  upapanno  pi yasassī tena bhom  ahaṃ   aptha            
 dukkhantakaraṇaṃ buddhaṃ dhammaṃ santam asaṅkhataṃ  
 vaṇṇayaṃ sukhado āsiṃ   sattānaṃ sukhito tato   aptha            
 guṇaṃ vadanto buddhassa buddhapītisamāyuto  
 sakantim parakantiñ ca janayiṃ tena kantimā     aptha            
 janoghe titthikākiṇṇo   abhibhuyya kutitthiye  
 guṇaṃ vadanto jotesiṃ   nāyakaṃ jutimā tato   aptha            
 piyakārijinassāpi   sambuddhassa guṇaṃ varaṃ    
 saraṃ divasasaṅko haṃ   ten  āsiṃ   piyadassano   aptha            
 yathāsattivasenāhaṃ sabbavācāhi   santhaviṃ  
 sugataṃ tena vāgīso   vicittapaṭibhānavā   aptha            
 ye bālā vimatiṃ   pattā   paribhonti mahāmuniṃ  
 niggahiṃ   te saddhammena paribhūto na ten  ahaṃ  aptha            
 buddhavaṇṇehi sattānaṃ kilese apaniṃ   ahaṃ  
 nikkilesamano homi tassa kammassa vāhasā   aptha

       mahākaccāna   
 padumuttaro nāma jino anejo ajitañjayo  
 satasahasse kappānaṃ ito uppajji nāyako   aptha           
 vīro kamalapattakkho sasaṅkavimalānano  
 kanakācalasaṅkāso ravidittiharippabho   aptha           
 sattanettamanohārī  varalakkhaṇabhūsito  
 sabbavākyapathātīto manujāmarasakkato   aptha           
 sambuddho  bodhayaṃ satte vāgīso   madhurassaro  
 karuṇāniḍḍhasantāno   parisāsu visārado   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 deseti madhuraṃ dhammaṃ catusaccupasaṅhitaṃ  
 nimugge mohapaṅkamhi samuddharati pāṇino   aptha           
 tadā ekacaro hutvā tāpaso himavālayo  
 nabhasā mānusaṃ lokaṃ gacchanto jinam addasaṃ   aptha           
 upecca santikaṃ tassa assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ  
 vaṇṇayaṃ tassa vīrassa sāvakassa mahāguṇaṃ   aptha           
 saṅkhittena mayā vuttaṃ vitthārena pakāsayaṃ  
 parisaṃ mañ ca toseti yathā kaccāyano ayaṃ    aptha           
 nāhaṃ evaṃ vidhaṃ kañci aññaṃ passāmi sāvakaṃ  
 tasmā  tadagge es  aggo evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo   aptha           
 tadāhaṃ vimhito hutvā sutvā vākyamanoramaṃ   
 himavantaṃ gamitvāna āhatvā  pupphasañcayaṃ  aptha            
 pūjetvā lokasaraṇaṃ tan ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   
 tadā mam  āsayaṃ ñatvā vyāhāsi  saraṇañjaho   aptha            
 passath  etaṃ isivaraṃ niddhantakanakattacaṃ  
 uddhaggalomaṃ pīn  aṃsaṃ  acalaṃ añjaliṃ ṭhitaṃ    aptha            
 hāsasupuṇṇanayanaṃ buddhavaṇṇagatāsayaṃ   
 dhammapaṭiggahavaraṃ  amatāsittasannibhaṃ     aptha            
 kaccānassa guṇaṃ sutvā taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayaṃ   ṭhito  
 anāgatamhi addhāne gotamassa mahāmune   aptha            
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito

      dabbamalla     
  
       dabbamalla   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbalokavidū muni  
 ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā   aptha           
 ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 desanākusalo buddho tāresi  janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 anukampako kāruṇiko hitesi sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 sampatte titthiye  sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi    aptha           
 evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññataṃ titthiyehi ca  
 vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tādihi   aptha           
 ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni  
 kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo   aptha           
 vassasatasahassāni āyaṃ vijjati tāvade  
 tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so  tāresi  janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso  
 upetvā lokapajjotaṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ   aptha           
 senāsanāni bhikkhūnaṃ paññāpentaṃ sa sāvakaṃ   
 kittayantassa vacanaṃ suṇitvā mudito ahaṃ   aptha           
 adhikāraṃ sasaṅghassa katvā tassa mahesino  
 nipacca sirasā pāde taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   aptha           
 tadahaṃ sa mahāvīro mama kammaṃ pakittayaṃ   
 so yaṃ  sasaṅghaṃ bhojesi sattāhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  aptha            
 so yaṃ kamalapattakkho sīhaṃso kanakattaco   
 maṃ   pādamūle patito patthayi   ṭhānam uttamaṃ   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati  aptha            
 sāvako tassa buddhassa dabbo nāmena vissuto  
 senāsanapaññāpako aggo hessat  ayaṃ   tadā   aptha            
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch   ahaṃ   aptha            
 satānaṃ tīṇikhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti ahos  ahaṃ   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   
 sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā   aptha            
 ekanavute ito kappe vipassī nāma nāyako  
 uppajji cārunayano  sabbadhammavipassako   aptha            
 duṭṭhacitto upavadi sāvakaṃ tassa tādino  
 sabbāsavaparikkhīṇaṃ   suddho  ti ca vijāniya    aptha            
 tass  eva naravīrassa  sāvakānaṃ  mahesinaṃ  
 salākaṃ paggahetvāna khīrodanam  adās  ahaṃ   aptha            
 imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso  
 kassapo nāma nāmena uppajji vadataṃ varo   aptha            
 sāsanaṃ jotayitvā so abhibhuyya kutitthiye  
 veneyye vinayitvā ca  nibbuto so sasāvako   aptha            
 sasissa nibbute nāthe attham entamhi  sāsane  
 devā kandiṃsu saṃviggā muttakesā rudammukhā   aptha            
 nibbāyissati dhammakkho  na passissāma subbate  
 na suṇissāma saddhammaṃ aho no appapuññatā   aptha            
 tadāyaṃ puthavī  sabbā acalā sācalācalā    
 sāgaro ca sasoko va   vinadī   karuṇaṃ giraṃ   aptha            
 catuddisā dundubhiyo   nādayiṃsu   samānusā    
 samantato asaniyo patiṃsu ca bhayāvahā   aptha            
 ukkā patiṃsu nabhasā dhūmaketu ca dissati  
 sabba thalaja sattā ca raviṃsu karuṇaṃ   migā   aptha            
 uppāde dāruṇe disvā sāsanatthañ ca sūcakaṃ    
 saṃviggā bhikkhavo tattha   cintayimha mayaṃ tadā  aptha            
 sāsanena vinā sammā   jīvitena alam mayaṃ  
 pavisitvā mahāraññaṃ yuñjāma jinasāsane   aptha            
 addasamha tadāraññe ubbiddhaṃ selam uttamaṃ

      dabbamalla     
 tadā ovadi no thero  buddhuppādo sudullabho  
 saddhā vo  sulabhā laddhā  thokasesañ ca sāsanaṃ   aptha            
 nipatanti khaṇātītā  anante dukkhasāgare

 catusaccaṃ pakāsentaṃ bodhayantaṃ sadevakaṃ

 nānāratanapajjotaṃ sasaṅghaṃ bhojayiṃ tahiṃ

 hemayaññopacitaṅgaṃ avadātaṃ tanuttacaṃ

      mahākoṭṭhika     
  
       mahākoṭṭhika   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbalokavidū muni  
 ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā   aptha           
 ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 desanākusalo buddho tāresi  janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 anukampako kāruṇiko hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi    aptha           
 evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññataṃ titthiyehi ca  
 vicittaṃ arahantehi  vasībhūtehi tādihi    aptha           
 ratanānaṭṭhapañ ñāsaṃ ugga to so mahāmuni  
 kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso battiṅsavaralakkhaṇo    aptha           
 vassasatasahassāni āyuṃ vijjati tāvade  
 tāvatā tiṭṭhamānaso tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 tadā haṃ haṃsavatiyā  brāhmaṇo vedapāragū   
  upetvā   sattapāraṅgaṃ  assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ   aptha           
 tadā so sāvakaṃ vīro pabhinna mati gocaraṃ  
 atthe dhamme ca nerutte paṭibhāne ca kovidaṃ  aptha           
 ṭhapesi etad aggamhi  taṃ sutvā mudito ahaṃ  
 sasāvakaṃ jinavaraṃ sattāhaṃ bhojayiṃ tadā   aptha           
 dusseh  acchādayitvāna   sasissaṃ buddhasāgaraṃ    
 nipacca pādamūlamhi taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ   ahaṃ  aptha            
 tato avoca lokaggo  passath  etaṃ dijuttamaṃ  
 vinataṃ pādamūle me kamalodarasappabhaṃ     aptha            
 buddhaseṭṭhassa bhikkhussa ṭhānaṃ patthayate ayaṃ  
 tāya saddhāya   cāgena tena dhammassavena ca  aptha            
 sabbattha sukhito hutvā saṃsaritvā bhavābhave  
 anāgatamhi addhāne lacchate taṃ manorathaṃ     aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha

   s  patiṭṭhayi

   s  ādihi  
   s  battiṅga

   s   pārago  
   g  usetvā

    s  dusse haṃ chādayitvāna

     therāpadāna 
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 koṭṭhito nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   aptha            
 taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ  
 mettacitto paricariṃ sato paññāsamāhito    aptha            
 tena kammavipākena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch  ahaṃ  aptha            
 satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti ahos  ahaṃ  aptha            
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  
 sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā   aptha            
 duve bhave saṃsarāmi devatte atha mānuse  
 aññaṃ gatiṃ na gacchāmi suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 duve kule pajāyāmi khattiye atha brāhmaṇe  
 nīce kule na jāyāmi  suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha            
 pacchime bhave sampatte brahmabandhu ahos  ahaṃ  
 sāvatthiyaṃ vippakule pacchā jāto mahaddhane    aptha            
 mātā candavatī nāma pitā me assalāyano  
 yadā me pitaraṃ buddho vinayī  sabbabuddhiyā   aptha            
 tadā pasanno sugate  pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ   
 moggallāno ācariyo upajjhāyo sarisambhavo   aptha            
 kesesu chijjamānesu diṭṭhichinnasamūlikā   
 nivāsento ca kāsāvaṃ arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   aptha            
 atthadhammaniruttīsu paṭibhāne ca me mati  
 pabhinnā tena lokaggo etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ   aptha

      uruvelakassapa     
       uruvelakassapa   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbalokavidū muni  
 ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā  aptha           
 ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 desanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 anukampako kāruṇiko hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi  aptha           
 evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññataṃ  titthiyehi ca  
 vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tadihi   aptha           
 ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni  
 kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo   aptha           
 vassasatasahassāni āyuṃ vijjati tāvade  
 tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 tadā haṃ haṃsavatiyā  brāhmaṇo sādhusammato  
 upecca lokapajjotaṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ   aptha           
 tadā mahāparisatiṃ  mahāpurisasāvakaṃ  
 ṭhapentaṃ etadaggamhi sutvāna mudito ahaṃ   aptha           
 mahatā parivārena  nimantetvā mahājinaṃ   
 brāhmaṇānaṃ sahassena saha dānaṃ ahaṃ adaṃ   aptha           
 mahādānaṃ daditvāna abhivādiya nāyakaṃ  
 ekamantaṃ ṭhito haṭṭho imaṃ  vacanam abraviṃ   aptha            
 tayi  saddhāya me vīra  adhikāraguṇena ca  
 parisā mahatī hotu nibbattissa tahiṃ tahiṃ   aptha            
 tadā avoca parisaṃ gajagajjita sussaro    
 karavīkarudo satthā  etaṃ   passatha brāhmaṇaṃ  aptha            
 hemavaṇṇaṃ   mahābāhuṃ kamalānanalocanaṃ  
 udaggatanujaṃ haṭṭhaṃ sandhāvantaguṇaṃ mamaṃ    aptha            
 esa patthayate   ṭhānaṃ sīhaghosassa bhikkhuno  
 anāgatamhi addhāne lacchate taṃ manorathaṃ   aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha

 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimito  
 kassapo nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   aptha            
 ito dvenavute kappe ahu  satthā anuttaro  
 anupamo asadiso phusso lokagganāyako   aptha            
 sa ve  sabbatamaṃ hantvā  vijaṭetvā  mahājaṭaṃ

 etha gantvā va paccantaṃ sodhetvā  avidhī balaṃ

 yācitvā   satth  upaṭṭhānaṃ   rājānaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  
 munivaraṃ   labhitvāna yāvajīvaṃ adimha   taṃ  aptha

 senāsanāni rammāni bhesajjāni hitāni ca   aptha

 anubhutā mayaṃ sabbe buddhapūjāy  idaṃ phalaṃ   aptha

      uruvela kassapa     
 māyākāro yathā laddho  dasseti  vikatiṃ  bahuṃ  
 tathā bhave bhavanto  haṃ videhādhipati ahuṃ    aptha            
 guṇ  ācelassa  vākyena micchādiṭṭhihatāsayo  
 narakaṃ maggam  ārūḷho  rujāya  mama dhītuyā  aptha            
 ovādaṃ nādayitvāna brahmunā nāraden  ahaṃ  
 bahuṃ va sāsito santo  diṭṭhiṃ hitvāna pāpikaṃ     aptha            
 pūrayitvā   visesena dasakammapathen  ahaṃ  
 hitvāna deham agamiṃ saggaṃ sabhavanaṃ yathā   aptha            
 pacchime bhavasampatte   brahmabandhu ahos  ahaṃ  
 bārāṇasiyaṃ pi tāyaṃ jāto vippamahākule   aptha            
 maccuvyādhijarābhīto   hitvāna ca   mahādhanaṃ    
 nibbānapadam esanto   jaṭilesu paribbajiṃ   aptha            
 tadā dve bhātato mayhaṃ pabbajiṃsu mayā saha  
 uruvelāya māpetvā assamaṃ nivasiṃ   ahaṃ   aptha            
 kassapo nāma gottena uruvelā nivāsitā    
 tato me āsi paññatti   uruvelāsu kassapo   aptha            
 nadīsakāse bhātā me nadī kassapasavhayo  
 āsi sakāse   nāmena gayāya   gayakassapo  aptha            
 dve satāni  nadīkassa   tīṇi majjhassa bhātuno  
  mama pañcasatā nūnā sissā sabbe mamānugā   aptha            
 tadā upecca me buddho katvā nānāvidhāni me  
 pāṭihīrāni lokaggo vinesi   narasārathi  aptha            
 satasahassaparivārena ahosiṃ     ehi bhikkhavo    
 teh  eva saha sabbehi a rahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ    aptha

       rādha   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbalokavidū muni  
 ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā   aptha           
 ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 desanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 anukampako kāruṇiko hitesi sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi  aptha           
 evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi  suññataṃ titthiyehi  ca  
 vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tādihi   aptha           
 ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni  
 kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo   aptha           
 vassasatasahassāni āyuṃ vijjati tāvade  
 tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so  tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 tadā haṃ haṃsavatiyā  brāhmaṇo mantapāragū  
 upecca taṃ naravaraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ  aptha           
 paññāpentaṃ mahāvīraṃ parisāsu visāradaṃ  
 paṭibhāneyyakaṃ bhikkhum etadagge vināyakaṃ   aptha           
 tadā haṃ kāraṃ katvāna sasaṅghe lokanāyake  
 nipacca sirasā pāde taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   aptha           
 tato maṃ bhagavā āha siṅginikkhasamappabho    
 sarena rajanīyena kilesamalahāriṇā     aptha            
 sukhī bhavassu dīghāyu sijjhataṃ paṇidhī tava    
 sasaṅghe me kataṃ kāram atīva vipulaṃ tayā   aptha

      rādha     
 satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha            
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 rādho ti nāmadheyyena hessati satthu sāvako   aptha            
 sake hetuguṇe  tuṭṭho sakyaputto narāsabho  
 paṭibhāneyyakānaggaṃ paññapessati  nāyako   aptha            
 taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ  
 mettacitto paricariṃ sato paññāsamāhito    aptha            
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ  agacch  ahaṃ   aptha            
 satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ  
 satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti ahos  ahaṃ   aptha            
 padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  
 sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā   aptha            
 pacchime bhavasampatte  giribbajapuruttame  
 jāto vippakule n  iddhe  vikalacchādanāsane   aptha            
 kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ pādāsiṃ sāriputtassa tādino  
 yadā jiṇṇo ca vuddho  ca tadārāmam upāgamiṃ   aptha            
 pabbājenti na maṃ keci jiṇṇam dubbalathāmakaṃ   
 tena jiṇṇo  vivaṇṇaṅgo soko c  āsiṃ   tadā ahaṃ   aptha            
 disvā mahākāruṇiko mam āha sa mahāmuni   
 kimatthaṃ putta sokaṭṭo  brūhi te cittajaṃ rujaṃ   aptha            
 pabbajjaṃ na labhe vīra svākkhāte tava sāsane  
 tena sokena dīno smi  saraṇaṃ hohi nāyaka     aptha            
 tadā bhikkhū samānetvā āpucchi munisattamo  
 imassa adhikāraṃ ye sarantā   vyāharantu te   aptha            
 sariputto tadāvoca  kāram assa sarāmi haṃ  
 kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ dāpesi piṇḍāya carato mama   aptha            
 sādhu sādhu kataññāsi   sāriputta  imaṃ tuvaṃ  
 pabbājesi dijaṃ vuḍḍhaṃ hessat  ājāniyo ayaṃ   aptha

       mogharāja   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbalokavidū muni  
 ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā   aptha           
 ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 desanākusalo buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ   aptha           
 anukampako kāruṇiko hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi    aptha           
 evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññataṃ titthiyehi ca  
 vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tādihi   aptha           
 ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni

 parakammāyane yutto n  atthi me kiñci sandhanaṃ    aptha           
 paṭikkamanasālāyaṃ vasanto katabhūmiyaṃ  
 aggiṃ ujjālayiṃ tattha daḷhakaṇhā siyā mahī    aptha           
 tadā parisatiṃ  nātho catusaccapakāsako  
 sāvakaṃ sampakittesi lūkhacīvaradhārakaṃ   aptha           
 tassa tamhi  guṇe tuṭṭho paṇipacca  tathāgataṃ

 tadā avoca bhagavā sāvake padumuttaro   
 passath  etaṃ purisakaṃ kucelaṃ tanudehakaṃ  aptha

 eso pattheti taṃ ṭhānaṃ saccasenassa  bhikkhuno

 evaṃ abhikkantadassāviṃ atthi pañhena āgamaṃ   
 kathaṃ  lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ  maccurājā na passati     aptha            
  suññato  lokaṃ avekkhassu  mogharājā sadā sato  
 attānudiṭṭhiṃ  uhacca  evaṃ maccutaro  siyā   aptha

 tīṇi gāthā satān  ettha bāsaṭṭhiñ c  eva   piṇḍitā  
 kaccānavaggo catupaññāso

      lakuṇṭakabhaddiya     
  
       lakuṇṭakabhaddiya   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā  
 ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā    aptha           
 tadā haṃ haṃsavatiyā  seṭṭhiputto mahādhano  
 jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ saṅghārāmam agacch  ahaṃ  aptha           
 tadā so lokapajjoto dhammaṃ desesi  nāyako  
 mañjussarānaṃ  pavaraṃ sāvakaṃ abhikittayi    aptha           
 taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā kāraṃ katvā mahesino  
 vanditvā satthuno pāde taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   aptha           
 tadā buddho viyākāsi  saṅghamajjhe vināyako  
 anāgatamhi addhāne lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ   aptha           
 satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha           
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 bhaddiyo nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch  ahaṃ   aptha           
 dvenavute ito kappe phusso uppajji nāyako  
 durāsado duppasaho sabbalokuttamo jino   aptha           
 caraṇena ca sampanno brahā  ujupatāpavā  
 hitesi sabbasattānaṃ bahū mocesi bandhanā   aptha            
 nandārāmavare  tassa ahosiṃ phussakokilo    
 gandhakuṭisamāsanne   ambarukkhe vasām  ahaṃ   aptha            
 tadā piṇḍāya gacchantaṃ dakkhiṇeyyaṃ jinuttamaṃ  
 disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā mañjunā abhikūj  ahaṃ    aptha            
 rājuyyānaṃ tadā gantvā supakkaṃ kanakattacaṃ  
 ambapiṇḍaṃ gahetvāna sambuddhass  opanāmayiṃ   aptha            
 tadā me cittam aññāya mahākāruṇiko jino  
 uppaṭṭhākassa hatthato pattaṃ paggaṇhi nāyako   aptha            
  
                                                                            s  g  nāyako  
   g  haṃsavatiyaṃ  
   s  agañch  
   g  deseti  
   g  s  madhura   
   g   kittayīṃ  
   g  vyākāsi  
   g  brahmā  
   g  nandā nāma vane  
    s  pussahokilo  g  puñña   
    g  s   samāpanno  
    g  mañjunā bhinikuj  aham  s  mañjunāninikuj  ahaṃ  
 s  ahbiñuj ahaṃ

     therāpadāna 
 dadāmi haṭṭhacitto haṃ ambapiṇḍam mahāmune  
 patte pakkhippa pakkhehi pañjaliṃ katvāna   mañjunā  aptha            
 sarena rajanīyena  savanīyena dhaṃsanā   
 vassanto buddhapūjatthaṃ  niddaṃ gantvā  nipajj  ahaṃ  aptha            
 tadā muditacittaṃ maṃ buddhapemagatāsayaṃ  
 sakuṇagghi  upagantvā ghātayi duṭṭhamānasā    aptha            
 tato cuto haṃ tusite anubhotvā mahāsukhaṃ  
 manussayoniṃ āgacchiṃ  tassa kammassa vāhasā   aptha            
 imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso  
 kassapo nāma gottena uppajji vadataṃ varo   aptha            
 sāsanaṃ jotayitvā so abhibhuyya kutitthiye  
 vinayitvā ca veneyye  nibbuto so sasāvako   aptha            
 nibbute tamhi lokagge pasannā janatā bahū  
 pūjanatthāya buddhassa thūpaṃ kubbanti satthuno   aptha            
 sattayojanikaṃ thūpaṃ sattaratanavibhūsitaṃ  
 kāressāma mahesissa  icc evaṃ mantayanti te   aptha            
 kikino kāsirājassā   tadā senāya nāyako  
 hutvā haṃ appamāṇassa pamāṇaṃ cetiye vadiṃ     aptha            
 tadā te mama vākyena cetiyaṃ yojanuggataṃ  
 akaṃsu naravīrassa nānāratanabhūsitaṃ   aptha            
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch   ahaṃ   aptha            
 pacchime ca bhave dāni jāto seṭṭhikule ahaṃ  
 sāvatthiyaṃ puravare iddhe phīte   mahādhane   aptha            
 purappavese sugataṃ disvā vimhitamānaso  
 pabbajitvāna naciraṃ arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   aptha            
 cetiyassa pamāṇaṃ yaṃ akariṃ   tena kammena    
 lakuṇṭakasarīro haṃ jāto paribhavāraho   aptha            
 sareṇa madhureṇāhaṃ pūjetvā isisattamaṃ  
 mañjussarānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ aggattam anupāpuṇiṃ     aptha

      kaṅkharevata     
 phaladānena  buddhassa guṇānusaraṇena ca  
 sāmaññaphalasampanno viharāmi anāsavo   aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā lakuṇṭakabhaddiyo thero i  g  a ti  
 lakuṇṭakabhaddiyattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       kaṅkha revata   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammesu  cakkhumā  
 ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako  aptha           
 sīhahanu brahmagiro haṃsadundrabhinisvano   
 nāgavikkantagamano candasūrādhikappabho  aptha           
 mahāmati mahāvīro mahājhāyī mahāhito   
 mahākāruṇiko nātho mahātamanisūdano    aptha           
 sa kadāci tilokaggo veneyyavinayaṃ  bahuṃ  
 dhammaṃ deseti sambuddho sattāsayavidū muni   aptha           
 jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ vīraṃ upasantaṃ anāvilaṃ  
 vaṇṇayanto parisatiṃ  toseti janataṃ jino   aptha           
 tadā haṃ haṃsavatiyā  brāhmaṇo vedapāragū  
 dhammaṃ sutvāna mudito taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   aptha           
 tadā jino viyākāsi  saṅghamajjhe vināyako  
 mudito hohi   tvaṃ brahme  lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ   aptha           
 satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha           
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 revato nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   aptha           
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch   ahaṃ  aptha            
 pacchime ca bhave dāni jāto haṃ koliye pure  
 khattiye kulasampanne iddhe phīte   mahaddhane   aptha

     therāpadāna 
 yadā kapilavatthusmiṃ buddho dhammam adesayi  
 tadā pasanno sugate pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ   aptha            
 kaṅkhā me bahuso āsi kappākappe  tahiṃ tahiṃ  
 sabbaṃ taṃ vinayī  buddho desetvā dhammam uttamaṃ  aptha            
 tato haṃ tiṇṇasaṃsāro tadā jhānasukhe rato  
 viharāmi  tadā buddho maṃ disvā etad abravi   aptha            
  yā kāci kaṅkhā idha vā huraṃ vā sakavediyā  vā paravediyā  vā  
 jhāyino tā pajahanti sabbā ātāpino brahmacariyaṃ carantā     aptha            
 satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha  
 sumutto sara vego va ki lese jhāpayiṃ  mamaṃ   aptha            
 tato maṃ jhānanirataṃ  disvā lokantagū muni  
 jhāyīnaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ aggo ti  paññāpesi mahāmuni    aptha            
 kilesā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 sāgataṃ       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 paṭisambhidā       pe       pe       pe        aptha            
 itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kaṅkhā revato thero i  g  a ti  
 revatattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ  
  
       sīvali   
 padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammesu cakkhumā  
 ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji nāyako   aptha           
 sīlaṃ tassa asaṅkheyyaṃ samādhi vajiropamo    
 asaṅkhiyaṃ   ñāṇavaraṃ vimutti ca   anopamā   aptha           
 manuj āmara nāgānaṃ brahmānañ ca samāgame  
 samaṇabrāhmaṇākiṇṇo   dhammaṃ desesi nāyako   aptha           
 sa sāvakaṃ mahālābhiṃ   puññavantaṃ jutindharaṃ  
 ṭhapesi etadaggamhi parisāsu visārado   aptha           
 tadā haṃ khattiyo āsiṃ nagare haṃsasavhaye  
 sutvā jinassa taṃ vākyaṃ sāvakassa guṇaṃ bahuṃ   aptha

      sīvali     
 nimantayitvā sattāhaṃ bhojayitvā sasāvakaṃ   
 mahādānaṃ daditvāna taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   aptha           
 tadā maṃ vinataṃ  pāde disvāna purisāsabho  
 susarena mahāvīro  imaṃ vacanam abravi   aptha           
 tato jinassa vacanaṃ sotukāmā mahājanā  
 deva dānava gandhabbā brāhmaṇā  ca mahiddhikā   aptha           
 samaṇā brāhmaṇā c  eva namassīsu  katañjalī  
  namo te purisājañña  namo te purisuttama   aptha           
 khattiyena mahādānaṃ dinnaṃ sattāhikaṃ vibho  
 sotukāmā phalaṃ tassa  vyākarohi  mahāmune    aptha            
 tato avoca bhagavā suṇotha mama bhāsitaṃ   
 appameyyamhi buddhamhi saṅghamhi suppatiṭṭhitā   aptha            
 dakkhiṇādāya kho v atthaṃ   appameyyaphalā hi sā  
 api ve  sa mahābhogo ṭhānaṃ pattheti uttamaṃ   aptha            
 lābhī  vipulalābhānaṃ yathā bhikkhu sudassano  
 tathā ham   pi bhaveyyan ti lacchate taṃ anāgate     aptha            
 satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo  
 gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   aptha            
 tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  
 sīvali nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   aptha            
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsūpago ahaṃ   aptha            
 ekanavute ito kappe vipassī lokanāyako  
 uppajji cārunayano   sabbadhammavipassako   aptha            
 tadā haṃ bandhumatiyā kulass  aññatarassa ca  
 dayito   patthito   c  eva āsi kammantavyāvaṭo   aptha            
 tadā aññataro pūgo   vipassissa mahesino  
 pariveṇaṃ akāresi mahantam iti vissutaṃ     aptha

  page      
     therāpadāna 
 niṭṭhite ca mahādānaṃ  dadaṃ khajjakasaññutaṃ   
 navadadhim  madhuṃ c  eva vicinaṃ  neva addasaṃ  aptha            
 tadā bhattaṃ  gahetvāna navaṃ dadhim madhum pi ca  
 kammasāmigharaṃ gacchan tam esantaṃ tam  addasaṃ   aptha            
 sahassam api  datvāna nālabhittha sat  aṃvayaṃ   
 tato haṃ evaṃ cintesiṃ   n  etaṃ hessati   orakaṃ   aptha            
 yathā ime janā sabbe sakkaronti tathāgataṃ  
 aham pi kāraṃ karissāmi   sasaṅghe lokanāyake   aptha            
 tadā ham evañ cintetvā dadhiṃ madhuñ ca   ekato  
 moditvā   lokanāthassa sasaṅghassa adās  ahaṃ   aptha            
 tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  
 jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch   ahaṃ  aptha            
 puṇāhaṃ bārāṇasiyaṃ rājā hutvā mahāyaso  
 sattukassa   tadā buddho   dvārarodhaṃ   akārayiṃ   aptha            
 tadā tapassino ruddhā   ekāham rakkhitā ahuṃ  
 tato tassa vipākena pāpattaṃ   nirayaṃ bhusaṃ   aptha            
 pacchime ca bhave dāni jāto haṃ koliye pure  
 suppavāsā ca me mātā mahālī   licchavī pitā   aptha            
 khattiyena puññakammena dvārarodhassa vāhasā  
 sattavassāni nivasī mātukucchimhi dukkhito   aptha            
 sattāhaṃ dvāramūḷho haṃ mahādukkhasamappito  
 mātā me chandadānena evaṃ āsi sudukkhitā   aptha            
 sāvatthito haṃ nikkhanto buddhena anukampito  
 nikkhantadivase yeva pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ   aptha            
 upajjhā sāriputto me moggallāno mahiddhiko  
 kese
